om
viṣvaksenasaṃhitā
prathamo 'dhyāyaḥ
viṣvaksenaḥ
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi bhūparīkṣāvidhiṃ param 
karṣayecchodhayedbhūmiṃ prāgudakpravaṇāṃ śubhām  Vis 
asthikeśādirahitāṃ kapālāṅgaravarjitām 
sarīsṛpādyā vyāghrādyā ye cānye duṣṭajantavaḥ  Vis 
yasyāṃ bhūmau pradṛśyante tāṃ bhūmiṃ varjayet sadā 
ārambhe śvaśṛgālaiśca saṃkīrṇā bandhunāśinī  Vis 
purīṣabhūmiḥsarveṣāṃ karturduḥkhapradā sadā 
tuṣabhasmāsthikeśaiśca kāṣṭhaloṣṭakapālakaiḥ  Vis 
krimikīṭapataṅgaiśca śarkaraiśca samanvitā 
aśubhāśrīkarī bhūmiḥ tasmādyatnāt parīkṣayet  Vis 
evaṃ durlakṣaṇaiścānyairyuktāṃ yatnena varjayet 
brāhmaṇasya sitā bhūmiḥ raktā vai kṣatriyasya tu  Vis 
pītavarṇā tu vaiśyasya kṛṣṇā śūdrasya kīrtitā 
brāhmaṇī ghṛtagandhā syāt kṣatriyā raktagandhinī  Vis 
mūtragandhā tu yā veśyā śūdrā viṣṭhānugandhinī 
madhurā brāhmaṇī proktā kaṣāyā kṣatriyā smṛtā  Vis 
ritiktā vaiśyā tu kaṭukā śūdrā ceti prakīrtitā 
evaṃ parīkṣya yatnena varṇagandharasādibhiḥ  Vis 
khātayedratnimātraṃ tu pāṃsumuddhṛtya pūrayet 
pāṃsurapyadhiko yatra sā bhūmiḥ sarvakāmadā  Vis 
uttamā yatra vai pāṃsuḥ samo hyardhaphalapradā 
madhyā pāṃsuryatra nṛna sāriṣṭā phaladādhamā  Vis 
tṛuptāni sarvabījāni prarohanti hi yatra vai 
trirātrābhyantareṇaiva sā bhūmiścottamā matā  Vis 
madhyamā pañcarātreṇa adhamā saptarātrikā 
yasyāṃ tu na prarohanti tāṃ prayatnena varjayet  Vis 
sasyānāṃ phalakāle tu gavāṃ tṛptiṃ ca kārayet 
tatastu lokapālāṃstu pūjayet sādhakottamaḥ  Vis 
annairapūpairlājaistu madhyarātre śacīpate 
evaṃ baliṃ prakurvīta pṛthagvā samayogataḥ  Vis 
tatkṣetraṃ khātayetpaścāt caturaśraṃ samantataḥ 
puruṣadvayaṃ khanitvā tu tadardhaṃ vāpi khātayet  Vis 
puruṣārdhapramāṇaṃ vā khaḍgamānapramāṇataḥ 
evaṃ kṣitiṃ khanitvā tu tanmadhye se capūra
yejjalam  Vis 
tanmadhye tu vidhiṃ pūjya brahmabījena mantravit 
gandhapuṣpairalaṃkṛtya ghaṇṭāśabdasamanvitam  Vis 
śaṅkhādighoṣasaṃyuktaṃ vīṇāveṇusamanvitam 
evaṃ vidhiṃ samabhyarcya adhivāsanamārabhet  Vis 
tasya dakṣiṇapārśve tu paścime cottare 'pi vā 
vasvādīnāṃ tu tanmadhye maṇḍapaṃ kalpya sādhakaḥ  Vis 
pūrṇakumbhaṃ nyasenmadhye pakvabimbaphalākṛtim 
droṇadvayena saṃpūrṇaṃ trisūtraiḥsamalaṃkṛtam  Vis 
gandhatoyena saṃpūrya gandhapuṣpasamanvitam 
droṇāṣṭaśālīnāstīrya padmamaṣṭadalaṃ likhat  Vis 
karṇikāyāṃ nyasetkumbhaṃ vastrayugmena veṣṭitam 
navaratnasamāyuktaṃ sauvarṇāyudhapañcayuk   Vis 
vāsudevasya mantreṇa sthāpayeddeśikottamḥ 
sarvāyudhasamāyuktaṃ sarvadevāvṛtaṃ tataḥ  Vis 
hiraṇyaṃ sarvabhūtajñaṃ sarvabhūtahṛdi sthitam 
ātmānamantarātmānaṃ paramātmānamavyayam  Vis 
nārāyaṇamaṇīyāṃsaṃ sṛṣṭisaṃhāravikramam kāraṇam 
evaṃ hi puruṣaṃ viṣṇuṃ dhyāyet kumbhodamadhyame  Vis 
evaṃ dhyātvā samabhyarcya gandhādyaiḥ sumanoramaiḥ 
pratyekaṃ droṇaśālyūrdhve vidyeśān parito nyaset  Vis 
pūrvavaddravyasaṃyuktān ghaṭeṣvabhyarcya sādhakaḥ 
svaiḥ svairmantraiśca gandhādyairupacārairmanoharaiḥ  Vis 
evaṃ saṃpūjya vidyeśān homasaṃskārakarma samārabhet 
kumbhasya pūrvadigdeśe kuṇḍaṃ ca caturaśrakam  Vis 
vṛttaṃ vā śilpinā kuryāt sthaṇḍile vā samācaret 
prāsādārambhakāle tu madhyarātre śacīpate  Vis 
śaṅkhatūryādisaṃyuktaṃ svastisūktasamanvitam 
sarvavighnopaśamanaṃ pālāśaṃ gṛhya deśikaḥ  Vis 
aṣṭottarasahasraṃ vā aṣṭottaraśataṃ tu vā 
nārasiṃhena mantreṇa madhyame juhuyāt sakṛt  Vis 
odumbarasamidbhirvāpyaṭaṣṭāviṃśatisaṃkhyayā 
pratyekaṃ mūlamantreṇa tathaivājyaṃ samācaret  Vis 
caruṃ puruṣasūktena ṣoḍaśāhutimuttamām 
juhuyāt kuṇḍamadhye tu sarvasaṃpatsukhāvaham  Vis 
evaṃ kṛtvā vidhānena pūrṇāhutimathācaret 
srucā mūlena mantrajño dvādaśākṣarasaṃjñayā  Vis 
kuḍubaṃ vā tadardhaṃ vā tasyārdhaṃ vā śacīpate 
kapilājyamathājyaṃ vā saṃgṛhya juhuyāt kriyāmkramāt  Vis 
paridhiprabhṛtīn dagdhvā dakṣiṇāmādadettataḥ 
dakṣiṇānte śacīnātha śaṅkhādyairghoṣayet kramāt  Vis 
nṛttagītādisaṃyuktaṃ supuṇyāhapuraḥsaram 
vedādhyayanasaṃyuktamadhivāsanamācaret  Vis 
evaṃ samāpya homāntaṃ pūrvarātre 'dhivāsayet 
prabhātāyāṃ tu śarvaryāṃ snātvācāryaḥ samāhitaḥ  Vis 
pūrvavat pūjayet kumbhān prokṣayet kṣitimadhyame 
svaiḥ svairmantraistu matimān sīmāyāṃ sarvadikṣu ca  Vis 
bhūtakrūrabaliṃ dadyāt aṣṭadikṣu samantataḥ 
digbandhaṃ kārayet paścāt astramantreṇa mantravit  Vis 
kumbhodakādaśeṣaṃ tu kṣitimadhye nayet kramāt 
tato 'vaṭaṃ kramāt pūrya mṛdbhiḥ sikatasaṃyutam  Vis 
kārayenamudgaraiḥsamyak vaiṣṇavairvedapāragaiḥ 
sūtraśaṅkūn khanitvā tu caitre māse śubhe dine  Vis 
sūtreṇa sūtrayet paścācchilpinā kuśalena vai 
prāsādaṃ kārayet paścāt ācāryaḥ śilpibhiḥ saha  Vis 
sādhako mantrayogyastu sthapatiḥkarmayogyataḥ kaḥ 
yadidaṃ bhūmiśuddhyarthaṃ prokṣaṇaṃ paramaṃ śubham  Vis 
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktaṃ prāsādārthaṃ śacīpate 
anenaiva vidhānena yaḥ kuryāt puṇyakarmabhāk  Vis 
sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ sa yāti paramāṃ gatim 
rāṣṭravṛddhikaraṃ puṇyamāyurārogyavardhanam  Vis 
dhanadhānyāni vardhante rājarāṣṭrādi vardhate 
ācāryaṃ pūjayet paścāt vastrairābharaṇairapi  Vis 
śilpinaṃ pūjayet tatra vastraiḥ kanakakuṇḍalaiḥ 
daivajñaṃ pūjayet paścāt navavastrāṅgulīyakaiḥ  Vis 
sadasyān pūjayet paścāt mukhavāsanapūrvakam 
evaṃkrameṇa saṃpūjya vastrābharaṇasaṃyutam  Vis 
tatastu kārayedgehaṃ śilpinā kuśalena tu 
sumuhūrte sulagne tu bālasthānamathārabhet  Vis 
bālasthānaṃ purākalpya paścānmūlālayaṃ kramāt 
kārayettu viśeṣeṇa ratnanyāsasamanvitam  Vis 
hastamātraṃ khanitvā tu brahmasthāne śacīpate 
sahasraṃ śataniṣkaṃ vā tasyārdhaṃ vārdhameva ca  Vis 
vinyaset kṣitimadhye tu taptakāñcanamuttamam 
marakatādīni ratnāni saṃgṛhyāstreṇa sādhakaḥ  Vis 
brahmādīśāvasānaṃ tu vinyaset svasvamantrataḥ 
madhyarātre suguptena yajamānena saṃyutaḥ  Vis 
śaṅkhādighāṣasaṃyuktaṃ garbhādhānaṃ samācaret 
tāmreṇa phelakāṃ kṛtvāvaṭamācchādya pūrayet  Vis 
śilābhiriṣṭakābhirvā tu pracchādyāvaṭaṃ kramāt 
gandhapuṣpādinābhyarcya ghaṇṭāśabdasamanvitam  Vis 
brahmabījena tatsarvaṃ sādhayet sādhakottamaḥ 
paścāddevīṃ samabhyarcya śriyārthaṃ paramāṃ śubhām  Vis 
vāsudevasya vaṃ sva
mantreṇa paścāt saṃpūjayet kramāt 
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktā bhūparīkṣā hyanuttamā  Vis 
iti śrīpāñcarātre viṣvaksenasaṃhitāyāṃ bhūparīkṣāvidhirnāma prathamo 'dhyāyaḥ 
dvitīyo 'dhyāyaḥ
dvitīyo 'dhyāyaḥ viṣvaksenaḥ
athātaḥsaṃpravakṣyāmi maṇḍapādikriyāṃ kramāta 
maṇḍapaścaiva kuṇḍāni sruksruvaṃvau
cāṣṭamaṅgalam  Vis 
toraṇaṃ caiva tannāma teṣāṃ pūjāvidhiṃ kramāt 
dvārapālapatākāśca teṣāṃ nyāsavidhiṃ kramāt  Vis 
śacīpate viviktena guhyādguhyavidhiṃ kramāt 
maṇḍapaṃ pūrvadigbhāge puṣṭiśrīvardhanaṃ bhavet  Vis 
sarvavighnopaśamanaṃ yāmye caiva yaśaskaram 
jayadaṃ vāruṇe bhāge dhanadaṃ cottare diśi  Vis 
āgneye naiṛte vāpi vāyavyaiśāśeśacīpate 
kalpayenmaṇḍapaṃ caivaṃ pūrvapūrvā garīyasī  Vis 
yajamānecchayā kuryāt anyadeśe na kārayet 
maṇḍapaṃ trividhaṃ proktaṃ hīnaṃ madhyamamuttamam  Vis 
hīne hīnaṃ tu kartavyaṃ madhyame madhyamaṃ punaḥ 
uttame cottamaṃ caiva maṇḍapaṃ vidhinā punaḥ  Vis 
pañcottaradaśaṃ
vāpi daśahastamathāpi vā 
ṣoḍaśastaṃbhasaṃyuktaṃ maṇḍapaṃ kārayet kramāt  Vis 
adhamaṃ tadvijānīyāt madhyamaṃ śṛṇu suvrata 
ṣoḍaśaṃ dvādaśaṃ
vāpi madhyamaṃ maṇḍapaṃ viduḥ  Vis 
caturviṃśatihastācca viṃśaddhastāntameva vā 
uttamaṃ tadvijñānīyāt sūtrapātavidhiṃ śṛṇu  Vis 
prāsādamaṇḍapādvāpi prākārāt pīṭhato 'pi vā 
ekahastaṃ dvihastaṃ vā trihastaṃ vā śacīpate  Vis 
visṛjya deśikaḥ kuryāt pratiṣṭhāmaṇḍapaṃ śubham 
sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyuktaṃ ācāryecchānurūpataḥ  Vis 
pātayedbrahmasūtraṃ tu yāvanmaṇḍapagocaram 
tribhāgīkṛtya sūtreṇa rekhāścatvārikārayet  Vis 
pūrvapaścimataścaiva tathā vai dakṣiṇottaram 
trikūṭaṃ kārayitvā tu bhāgaṃ tatra tu kārayet  Vis 
koṇeṣu caiva sarveṣu koṇastaṃbhān prakalpayet 
sūtrasandhiṣu sarveṣu stambhānanyān prakalpayet  Vis 
maṇḍapāṅgāni sarvāṇi cānyāni tu śacīpate 
yuktyā yuktiviśeṣeṇa kārayettu yathāvidhi  Vis 
caturdvārasamāyuktaṃ vitānādyairvibhūṣitam 
evaṃ tu maṇḍapaṃ kṛtvā saptāhātpūrvameva tu  Vis 
maṇḍapasyānurūpeṇa madhye vediṃ tu kārayet 
āmeṣṭakābhiḥ pakvābhiḥ vedikāṃ kārayet kramāt  Vis 
uttame 'pyuttamāṃ kuryānmadhyame madhyamāṃ kuru 
adhame 'pyadhamāṃ kṛtvā tanmāne puṭamānataḥ  Vis 
dvitākocchrāyasaṃyuktāṃ darpaṇodarasaṃnibhām 
vedikāṃ kramaśaḥ kṛtvā kuṇḍāni parikalpayet  Vis 
tritālaṃ vedikāyāṃ tu dūrībhūtāni sarvaśaḥ 
catustālaṃ dvitālaṃ vā visṛjya paritaḥ kramāt  Vis 
tritālaṃ vedikāyāstu visṛjya paritaḥ kramāt 
catustālaṃ dvitālaṃ vā dūrībhūtāni savarśaḥ  Vis 
kārayedvahnikuṇḍāni turyāśrādīni sādhakaḥ 
prākpūrvaṃpratyaksaṃsthitamantataḥ  Vis 
tasyāmāsphālayet paścādāyataṃ dakṣiṇottaram 
ekahastaṃ dvihastaṃ vā jñātvā mānaṃ tu lāñchayet  Vis 
dvābhyāṃ dvābhyāmathaikaikaṃ lāñchayet koṇamatsyakam 
diksūtrāṇi kramātteṣu prasāryāsphālya yatnataḥ  Vis 
caturaśrīkṛtaṃ kṣetraṃ catuṣkoṇasamaṃ śubham 
caturabhyadhikaṃ viṃśadaṅgulaṃ caturaśrakam  Vis 
sūtreṇa sūtrayitvā tu kṣetraṃ tāvat khanet kṣitim 
tasyārdhaṃ vā khanitvā tu śilpinā kuśalena tu  Vis 
kārayeccaturaśrādikuṇḍāni vidhivat kramāt 
tālamānena sarvatra kuṇḍāni paritaḥ kramāt  Vis 
kārayeccaturaśrādi vistārāyāmatādṛśam taḥ samam 
sūtreṇa sūtrayitvā tu kṣetraṃ tāvat khanet kṣitima  Vis 
khātasya mekhalāḥ kāryāḥtyaktvā caivāṅgulidvayam 
prathamā sātvikī proktā dvitīyā rājasī matā  Vis 
tṛtīyā tāmasī pūrvā dvādaśāṅgulamucchritā 
aṣṭāṅgulā dvitīyā tu tṛtīyā caturaṅgulā  Vis 
caturaṅgulavistārāḥ sarvāḥ kāryāstu santatam 
yonirdaśāṅgulā ramyā ṣaṭcatudvaryaṅgulāgrakā  Vis 
yoniryonirivāsamā
kārā gajoṣṭhasadṛśāpiśī tuvā 
kramānnimnā tu kartavyā caturaṅgulamāyatā  Vis 
mūlaṃ tu tryaṅgulaṃ jñeyamagraṃ tasya ṣaḍaṅgulam 
ekahastādistasya
kuṇḍasya lakṣaṇaṃ kathitaṃ tvidam  Vis 
dvihaste dviguṇaṃ proktaṃ nābhiścaiva tu mekhalā 
ekamekhalakaṃ vāpi kuṇḍaṃ saṃkṣepakarmaṇi  Vis 
kuṇḍārdhaṃ koṇabhāgārdhaṃ diśi cottarato bahiḥ 
pūrvapaścimato yatnāt lāñchayitvā tu madhyataḥ  Vis 
sarvato bhrāmitaṃ kuṇḍamardhacandraṃ bhavet sphuṭam 
tatkuṇḍaṃ sarvasiddhyarthaṃ sarvasaṃpadvivardhanam  Vis 
sarvavighnopaśamanaṃ dakṣiṇe kārayeda budhaḥ 
kuṇḍādyevaṃdyava
sthitaṃ sūtraṃ koṇe yadatiricyate  Vis 
tadarthaṃ diśi saṃsthāpya bhrāmitaṃ vartulaṃ bhavet 
vṛttaṃ tu paramaṃ jñeyaṃ sarvaduḥkhanivāraṇam  Vis 
anāvṛṣṭibhayaṃ nāsti ativṛṣṭibhayaṃ tathā 
padmākāraṃ tu sarvatra mekhalāyāṃ tu vartulam  Vis 
pratyekaikaṃ śacīnātha mekhalopari sādhakaḥ 
dvādaśaṃ vā dalaṃ likhya cāṣṭapatraṃ sakarṇikam  Vis 
tatkuṇḍaṃ padmamityuktaṃ sarvaśāstraviśāradaiḥ 
brahmavṛddhikaraṃ jñeyaṃ yajñasvādhyāyavṛddhidam  Vis 
tathaiva caturaśraṃ tu iti śāstrasya niścayaḥ 
trikoṇaṃ vābjakuṇḍaṃ vā sādhakecchānurūpataḥ  Vis 
some tu kārayeddhīmān sarvavighnopanāśanam 
pañcatriṃśāṅgulaṃ vāpi dvādaśāṅgulameva vā  Vis 
saṃgṛhyācāryataḥsūtraṃ prasāryāsphālya yatnataḥ 
naiṛte hyanile caiva lāñchayet koṇamatsyakam  Vis 
tathaiva lāñchayedaindre tattrikoṇaṃ bhavecchubham 
kārayedavaṭaṃ dhīmān śilpinā kuśalena tu  Vis 
tattudrūpeṇa kuṇḍeṣu mekhalāṃ paritaḥ kramāt 
kārayettu śacīnātha sādhakaḥ paramārthavit  Vis 
etattrikoṇamuddiṣṭaṃ śeṣaṃ sādhāraṇaṃ bhavet 
kuṇḍapaṅktiḥ samākhyātā prakṛtistriguṇātmikā  Vis 
sā yoniḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ siddhyarthaṃ tu śacīpate 
vidyāmantragaṇānāṃ tu vimukteścaiva kāraṇam  Vis 
prācyāṃ śiraḥsamākhyātaṃ bāhū koṇe vyavasthitau 
aiśānyāgneyasaṃjñe tu yaṅghā vāyavyanaiṛte  Vis 
udaraṃ kuṇḍamityuktaṃ yoniryonirvidhīyate 
mekhalātritayaṃ caiva guṇatrayamudāhṛtam  Vis 
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktaṃ kuṇḍānāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ kramāt 
sruksruvau maṅgalāṃścaiva lānyaṣṭau
toraṇāni tathaiva ca  Vis 
pravakṣyāmyadhunā caiva teṣāṃ lakṣaṇamucyate 
aśvatthakhadirādyairvā caturviṃśadbhi 
raṅgulaiḥ  Vis 
pratiṣṭhādyutsave caiva homārthaṃ kārayet sruvam cam 
saptapañcāṅgulaṃ vāpi vistāraṃ caturaśrakam  Vis 
tribhāgena bhavedgartaṃ madhye vṛttaṃ suśobhanam 
tiryagūrdhvaṃ samaṃ vāpi tadardhaṃ vā khanet sruvam cam  Vis 
aṅgulasya caturthāṃśaṃ vyapohyānte 'vaṭasya tu 
tasyānte mekhalāṃ samyak gartaṃ vai paritaḥ kramāt  Vis 
kārayenmekhalāmekāmutsedhaṃ tu tathaiva ca 
mekhalāyāstu paritaḥ likhedabjadalākṛtim  Vis 
dvādaśāṣṭadalaṃ vāpi kārayenmekhalādhare 
karṇikāṃ gartamadhye tu likhecchilpapramāṇataḥ  Vis 
dalānte valayaṃ kuryāt caturaśraṃ samantataḥ 
tadaṅgulārdhavistāraṃ kalābinduvibhūṣitam  Vis 
sarvālaṃkārasaṃyuktaṃ dvirekhāyuksamācaret 
dvādaśāṣṭakamevaṃ vā yathāruci lekhit kramāt  Vis 
kaṇṭhaṃ tribhāgavistāraṃ sārdhāṅgulasamāyatam 
dviraṅgulāyataṃ vāpi tadagre tu mukhaṃ bhavet  Vis 
caturaṅgulavistāraṃ pañcāṅgulamathāpi vā 
trikaṃ dvyaṅgulamātraṃ syānmadhye dhārāṃ suśobhanām  Vis 
suṣiraṃ kaṇṭhadeśe syāt praviśecchibika yathā 
dhārāyā dakṣiṇe vāme mukhe vṛttaṃ samālikhet  Vis 
kaṇṭhordhve tu likhedāsyaṃ suśobhanamataḥ param 
nāsikāmukhamekaṃ vā varāhānanameva ca  Vis 
vyāghragomukhameva syāt yathāruci samācaret 
srukpṛṣṭhaṃ śodhayitvā tu parito 'ṣṭadalaṃ likhet  Vis 
vṛttāpādaṃ tato bāhye nyaseddvyaṅgulameva tu 
tathaiva daṇḍamūle tu padanyāsaṃ yathāvidhi  Vis 
aṅguṣṭhāṅgulamānena tadvṛttāṅghriṃ samācaret 
daṇḍadvitīyamadhyānte tṛtīyasyādhare 'mbujam  Vis 
aṣṭapatrasamāyuktamālikhet phalakāyutam 
ghṛtādimadhyame bhāge kārayet paritaḥ kramāt  Vis 
daṇḍamūle 'bjamukulaṃ trilekhāyuksamācaret 
caturabhyadhikaṃ viṃśadaṅgulaṃ tacchacīpate  Vis 
sruvaṃ tu kārayetpaścāt ānanena samanvitam 
caraṣakaṃ dvyaṅgulaṃ vṛttaṃ kartavyaṃ tu suśobhanam  Vis 
goṣpadaṃ tu yathāmagnamalpapaṅke tathā bhavet 
sruvasruco
mūle mukhādye ca trirekhā yavamānataḥ  Vis 
kārayettu śacīnātha sā ca sruk sarvasiddhidā 
mukhāditryaṅgulaṃ hitvā tadante 'ṅghriṃ samācaret  Vis 
vṛttaṃ suśobhanaṃ pṛṣṭhe taddehāṅgulamānataḥ 
tathaiva sruvamūle 'ṅghriṃ vistārāyāmatādṛśam  Vis 
padmasya mukulākāraṃ sruvamūle 'tha kārayet 
parasyākṣyaṅghrihīnena
kārayedvātha sruksruvau  Vis 
etat sruksruvamākhyātaṃ maṅgalāṣṭakamucyate 
lohajānyeva kurvīta alābhe kāṣṭhajāni ca  Vis 
aśvatthaṃ vā palāśaṃ vā khadiraṃ vaṭameva vā

dvyaṅgulaṃ tu ghanaṃ jñeyaṃ pīṭhaṃ tu caturaṅgulam 
tasyopari likhetpadmamaṣṭapatraṃ sakarṇikam  Vis

nyagrodhaṃ tu pratīcyāṃ vai sāmaṃ
varuṇadaivatam  Vis 
uttare somadaivatyaḥ plakṣaścātharvaṇo bhavet

saptahastasamāyuktaṃ pañcahastamathāpi vā  Vis 
caturhastāyataṃ vāpi yathāruci samācaret

śūlāyāmaṃ dvitālaṃ vā pādonaṃ vā śacīpate

vattaṃ vā caturaśraṃ vā yuktyā kuryādyathāvidhi

athaikatālamānaṃ vā khātayedavaṭaṃ dharām  Vis 
tattadgarteṣu saṃsthāpya toraṇāni yathākramam

subandhuṃ vāruṇe caiva suhotraṃ nāma cottare

śaṅkukarṇaḥ sarpanetraḥ pratīcyāṃ dvārapālakau 
uttaradvārapālau tu sumukhaḥ supratiṣṭhitaḥ  Vis

iti śrīpāñcarātre viṣvaksenasaṃhitāyāṃ maṇḍapādilakṣaṇavidhirnāma dvitīyo 'dhyāyaḥ
tṛtīyo 'dhyāyaḥ

ācāryaḥsamalaṃkṛtya navavastrāṅgulīyakaiḥ

nirgacchedvṛkṣamāsādya śilpibhiḥsaha sādhakaḥ

kaṇṭakāt khadiraṃ grāhyamasāraṃ parivarjayet

tatpūrvabhāge tantrajñaḥ sāyāhne cādhivāsayet  Vis

dakṣiṇordhvakare padmamadhaḥ kaumodakīṃ nyaset  Vis 
vāmordhvādhaḥ sthite haste śaṅkhacakraṃ tu vinyaset 
itthaṃ pradyumnamūrtaṃ te devarṣe varṇito 'dhunā taṃ mayā  Vis 
aniruddhaṃ vadāmo 'tra myatra
śṛṇu nārada tattvataḥ 
nīlajīmūtasaṃkāśaṃ kālāñjanacayopamam  Vis 
śaṅkhacakradharaṃ devaṃ pītavastraṃ caturbhujam 
sarvābharaṇasaṃyuktaṃ sarvāvayavaśobhitam  Vis 
sarvālaṃkārasaṃyuktamaniruddhamitīritam 
asya vāmakare cordhve śaṅkhamanyakare gadām  Vis 
dakṣiṇordhve nyaseccakramanyatrābhayamiṣyate 
aniruddhaṃ jagannāthamanantopari śāyinam  Vis 
śriyaṃ dakṣiṇataḥ pārśve puṣṭiṃ vāme 'sya vinyaset 
śayane sati mūlārcā dvibhujaṃ vā caturbhujam  Vis 
kalpayenmuniśārdūla sarvasaṃpat sukhāvaham 
devasya pādapārśve tu śriyaṃ puṣṭiṃ tu vinyaset  Vis 
atha vā kalpayeddevamaulipārśve śriyaṃ mune 
citraṃ vāpyardhacitraṃ vā citrābhāsaṃ tu vā mune  Vis 
yajamānecchayā kuryāt devīnāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ kramāt 
itthaṃ śriyādimūrtīnāṃ pūrvapūrvā garīyasī  Vis 
aniruddha iti prokto matsyādīn śṛṇu nārada 
śatapatramayasyātha puṇḍarīkasya madhyame  Vis 
padmāsanasthaṃ matsyāṣṭaparītaṃ kanakaprabham 
triṇetraṃ dvibhujaṃ caiva prāṅmukhaṃ padmadhāriṇam  Vis 
sarvāvayavasaṃpūrṇaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam 
matsyābhimāninaṃno
mūrrtiṃtaṃ
itthamuktaṃ ca nārada  Vis 
padmapūrvadale matsyaṃ sauvarṇaṃ vinyased budhaḥ 
āgneyadigdale matsyaṃ rājataṃ cātha vinyaset  Vis 
yāmyadigdalamadhye tu matsyaṃ tāmranibhaṃ nyaset 
naiṛtyadigdale matsyaṃ kṛṣṇavarṇaṃ tu vinyaset  Vis 
vāruṇe digdale matsyaṃ raktavarṇaṃ tu vinyaset 
vāyavyadigdale matsyaṃ śyāmavarṇaṃ tu vinyaset  Vis 
saumyadigdalamatsyaṃ tu dhūmravarṇaṃ tu vinyaset 
īśānadigdale matsyamagnivarṇaṃ tu vinyaset  Vis 
ityaṣṭadigdalasthaistu matsyairabhimṛkhīkṛtam 
matsyābhimāninaṃ no
mūrtaṃ tava snehāt pradarśitam  Vis 
asya dakṣiṇapārśve tu śriyaṃ puṣṭiṃ paratra ca 
vinyasenmatsyarūpaṃ vai kūrmarūpaṃ tataḥ śṛṇu  Vis 
kālāñjanagiriprakhyaṃ triṇetraṃ svāṅgaśobhitam 
caturbāhuyutaṃ caiva sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam  Vis 
añjanamṛtsaṃnibhamūrtiḥ dvādaśapatre vartitamabje 
padmasamākhyasvāsanayuktaḥ kūrmaśarīrī viṣṇurihāste  Vis 
prākkramato 'bjadvādaśapatrārūḍhaśarīrairdvādaśakūrmaiḥ 
añjanavarṇaprakhyaśarīrerāvṛtamūrtiḥsvābhimukhasthaiḥ  Vis 
śaṅkhacakradharaścaiva padmahastastathaiva ca 
tato dvādaśakūrmā hi kūrmairhi
devo 'pyabhimukhīkṛtaḥ  Vis 
asya dakṣiṇahastordhve cakrapadmocakraṃ padmaṃkarāntare 
vāmordhve śaṅkhamityuktaṃ padmaṃ cādhaḥsthite kare  Vis 
asya dakṣiṇapārśve tu śriyaṃ vinyasya buddhimān 
puṣṭiṃ vāme nyasedevaṃ kūrmamūrtirudāhṛtā  Vis 
vārāhaṃ śṛṇu vakṣyāmi rājāvartanibhaṃ mune 
śaṅkhavarṇaṃ tu vā śyāmaṃ sarvalakṣaṇalakṣitam  Vis 
navayauvanasaṃpūrṇāṃ sarvāvayavasundarīm 
nārīṇāmuttamāṃ devīṃ sukeśāṃ paṅkajānanām  Vis 
vidyullatāprabhāṃ vāpi śyāmāṃ vāpi kṛtāñjalim 
sarvālaṃkārasaṃyuktāṃ nimagnāṃ jagatīṃ śubhām  Vis 
vāmadoṣṇā samāliṅgya proddhṛtyāliṅgya susthitām 
vāmena bāhunāśliṣya jighran devīmukhaṃ prabhuḥ  Vis 
vāmenāliṅgya hastena tasyāḥ skandhaṃ taponidhe 
gṛhītvoruṃ dṛḍhaṃ tasyāḥ dakṣiṇena kareṇa ca  Vis 
sūkarāṅgaṃ caturbāhuṃ śaṅkhacakradharaṃ prabhum 
dakṣiṇe tu nyaset cakraṃ vāme śaṅkhaṃ tu vinyaset  Vis 
itthaṃ varāharūpaṃ te prathamaṃ paripaṭhyate 
atha vā kroḍavaktraṃ ca mahākāyaṃ sudaṃṣṭrakam  Vis 
sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpannaṃ śrīvatsāṅkitavakṣasam 
tiryaksaṃsthitasūtraṃ ca rūpaṃ vai yanmahātmanaḥ  Vis 
vārāhaṃ madhyamaṃ proktaṃ saṃkṣepāttu taponidhe 
atha vā śṛṇu vakṣyāmi rūpaṃ vārāharūpiṇaḥ  Vis 
uddhṛtya nāsikātulyaṃ vāmahastasya kokūrparam 
vāmapārśvārdhabhāge tu nirīkṣan kokūr
paraṃ sadā  Vis 
kaṭipradeśamālambya pāṇinā dakṣiṇena tu 
evaṃ rūpaṃ mahāviṣṇoḥ śaṅkhacakradharasya ca  Vis 
asya dakṣiṇahastāgre cakraṃ śaṅkhaṃ pare ca hi 
iti vārāhamūrtasya tridhā rūpaṃ tu darśitam  Vis 
evamuktasya rūpasya tridhākārasya nārada 
itthaṃ rūpaṃ tu kartavyaṃ nṛsiṃhasya tataḥ śṛṇu  Vis 
galādadhastānnararūpadhārī paratra siṃhānanabhṛtsvarūpaḥ 
bibharti netrāṇi hutāśanārkaprabhā ñcitānyeva vibhīṣaṇāni  Vis 
śaṅkhacakradharaścaiva sarvābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ 
sarvāvayavasaṃpūrṇaḥ sarvasiddhikaraḥśubhaḥ  Vis 
cakraṃ ca dakṣiṇe haste śaṅkhaṃ vāme nyasedbudhaḥ 
śvetaparvatasaṃkāśaṃ sarvaduḥkhavināśanam  Vis 
raktacandanadigdhāṅgaṃ kālābhroddāmaniḥ svanam 
śaradindukalādaṃṣṭraṃ kruddhaṃ hāṭakatāṭakam  Vis 
suphullavadanaṃ śaśvat duṣṭānāmatibhīṣaṇam 
evaṃ rūpaṃ nṛsiṃhasya kṛtvā pūrvaṃ mṛdā mudā mune  Vis 
paryaṅkakalpitaṃ kṛtvā āsīnaṃ viṣṭare śubhe 
hastayoḥkokūr
pare tasya jānvorupari vinyaset  Vis 
itthaṃ nṛsiṃharūpaṃ te varṇitaṃ vaṇatocitam 
vāmanasya vadāmo 'tra myatra
rūpaṃ śruṇu mahāmune  Vis 
susmitaṃ padmanābhena
vāmanaṃ vāmanākṛtim 
bālakuñjarasaṃkāśaṃ bṛhatskandhaṃ mahābhujam  Vis 
śyāmalaṃ nīrajākṣaṃ tu āyatāmalalocanam 
kṣoṇītalaṃ padanyāsaiḥ ḍolayanniva nārada  Vis 
jaṭāṭavīsamāyuktaṃ sarveṣāṃ ca manoharam 
dvibhujaṃ savyahastena muṣṭinā daṇḍadhāriṇam  Vis 
ākuñcitaṃ vāmapādaṃ svāgataṃ dakṣiṇaṃ bhujam 
hārakuṇḍalakeyūrabhūṣaṇairbhūṣitaṃ mune  Vis 
lambayajñopavītena mekhalānāṃ trayeṇa ca 
saṃyuktaṃ yuktarūpaṃ tu kāśyapaṃ brahmacāriṇam  Vis 
kaupīnadhāriṇaṃ vāpi pītavāsasameva ca 
rakṣārthaṃ viṣṭāpānāṃ tu vāmanatvamupāgatam  Vis 
evaṃ sulakṣaṇopetaṃ rūpaṃ kāryaṃ mahāmune 
jāmadagnyasya rāmasya rūpaṃ vakṣyāmyataḥ param  Vis 
tasya varṇaṃ suvarṇābhaṃ dvibhujaṃ śvetaraktakam 
āsīnaṃ tu prasannāsyaṃ brahmalakṣmīsamāvṛtam  Vis 
sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpūrṇaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam 
sarvālaṃkārasaṃyuktaṃ jaṭāmaṇḍalamaṇḍitam  Vis 
paraśuṃ dakṣiṇe haste vāme cāpaṃ sapatriṇam 
vāme kamaṇḍaluṃ vāpi cākṣasūtraṃ tu dakṣiṇe  Vis 
itthaṃ rūpaṃ mune tubhyaṃ jāmadagnyasya varṇitam 
rāmasyātha vadāmo 'tramyatra
rūpaṃ dāśarathestava  Vis 
atīvarūpasaṃpannau nīlavellitamūrdhajau 
vyūḍhoraskau natāṃsau ca keyūrāṅgadacitritau  Vis 
dīrghabāhū śriyopetau saumyau prahasitānanau 
karṇāntalocanau sākṣāt prathame vayasi sthitau  Vis 
saundaryāmṛtatoyaiśca siñcantāviva viśvataḥ 
khaṅgahastau dhanuṣpāṇī bhujavikhyātavikramau  Vis 
baddhagodhāṅgulitrāṇau mune vaiśravaṇopamau 
audāryarūpasaṃpadbhiḥ nṛṇāṃ cittāpahāriṇau  Vis 
kausalyāyāḥ sumitrāyāḥ prītidau vīryavattarau 
rākṣasadhvāntatigmāṃśū śūrau daśarathātmajau  Vis 
naranārāyaṇākhyātau tāvubhau raghunandanau 
jagatāṃ pālanārthāya manuṣyatvamupāgatau  Vis 
puṇḍarīkaviśālākṣau tāvubhau pītavāsasau 
bhujānte baddhatūṇīrau bāṇapāṇī mahāmune  Vis 
nivasantau śriyā sākaṃ vālmīkeḥ kavikāvyasāgare 
rakṣasāṃ mṛtyusaṃkāśau rāvaṇasyātirāvaṇau  Vis 
nṛpasūnū raghuśreṣṭhau bhrātarau rāmalakṣmaṇau 
sarvaiśca lakṣaṇairyuktau sthāpayettantravittamaiḥ  Vis 
samastalakṣaṇopetāṃ sītāṃ rāmasya vallabhām 
naiṛtānāṃ vināśāya jātāṃ śuddhāmayonijām  Vis 
triguṇātmamayīṃ māyāṃ mūlaprakṛtisaṃsthitām 
vyaktarūpeṇa saṃjñāpi sākṣādavyaktarūpiṇīm  Vis 
pativratāṃ mahābhāgāṃ strīṇāmapyuttamāṃ śriyam 
raktapadmakarāṃ devīṃ padmāṃ padmopamānanām  Vis 
yauvanoddāmadivyāṅgīṃ sītāṃ janakanandinīm 
pātivratyaguṇopetāṃ sītāṃ rāmasya vallabhām  Vis 
sarvālaṃkārasaṃyuktāṃ nīlālakaśiroruhām 
mālānibaddhadhammillāṃ madavibhrāntalocanām  Vis 
kālapītāmbaradharā sthāpayedrāmapārśvataḥ 
savyamuṣṭiṃṣṭau
lalāṭāntaṃ kṛtordhvamukhamantaram  Vis 
tasmin tryavanataṃ cāpaṃ bāṇaughajadhanaṃdṛḍham 
vāsavāstraṃ vāmabāhau kārayenamunisattama  Vis 
sāyakaṃ kaṭisūtre tu vāmapāṇiṃtu dakṣiṇe 
kālāgnisadṛśaṃ bāṇaṃ paulastyāntakaraṃ dṛḍham  Vis 
antare 'sya mukhaṃ kṛtvā golakaṃ colbaṇaṃ bhavet  
mardantaṃ rāvaṇapuraṃ svabalaṃ sabalaṃ
cāyuṣaṃ tathā  Vis 
nihatya rāmahastasthaṃ 
sthāpayeddakṣiṇe kare 
vasutālena vā vidvān navatālakrameṇa vā  Vis 
berasya cānurūpeṇa caret sarvāyudhāni vai 
kuñcitaṃ vāmapādaṃ tu susthitaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ padam  Vis 
kaniṣṭhikāṅkitasthāne tvaṅguṣṭhasya sthitirbhavet 
stokakuñcitajānuśca pādo vāmasthito bhavet  Vis 
mukhe śarīre kaṭyāṃ ca triṣvaṅgeṣveṣu nārada 
tribhaṅgitvānmuniśreṣṭha tribhaṅgīti prapaṭhyate  Vis 
mukhaṃ dakṣiṇato bhaṅgaṃ tanumadhyaṃ tu vāmataḥ 
dakṣiṇe kaṭibhaṅgastu bhaṅgatrayamudāhṛtam  Vis 
vāmahastaḥ sacāpaḥ syāddakṣiṇaḥsaśilīmukhaḥ 
lakṣmaṇasya bhavedevaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ bharatasya tu  Vis 
śatrughnasyāpyathaivaṃ syāditi tantreṣu niścitam 
saṃsthāpya madhyame rāmaṃ vāmapārśve 'sya lakṣmaṇam  Vis 
dakṣiṇe sthāpayeddevīṃ sītāṃ janakanandinīm 
śatrughnabharatau kāryāvuttare dakṣiṇe kramāt  Vis 
cāmarāsaktabāhū tau parivāravidhāvapi 
iti svatantre nirdiṣṭaṃ paratantre vadāmyaham  Vis 
lohaiśca nirmite bere cottamādikramairmune 
lalāṭapaṭṭaparyantaṃ pādāṅguṣṭhāt samucchrayam  Vis 
dvātriṃśadaṅgulaṃ viddhi uttamaṃ kautukaṃ dvija 
asmāt saptāṅgulairhīnaṃ madhyamaṃ beramucchrayam  Vis 
asmāt navāṅgulairhīnamadhamaṃ parikīrtitam 
iti dāśarathermūrtamutsedhaṃ munisattama  Vis 
sītālakṣmaṇayoścāpi bharatasyāpi sāmpratam 
śatrughnasyāpi devarṣe vadāmyāyāmamadya te  Vis 
devasya bāhumūlāntaṃ devyutsedhaṃ pracakṣate 
lakṣmaṇasyocchrayaścāpi rāmasyāsyāntamīritam  Vis 
lakṣmaṇasya bhujāntaṃ syāt śatrughnasyocchrayo bhavet 
iti dīrghapramāṇoktaṃ śeṣaṃ pūrvavadācaret  Vis 
svatantre paratantre ca lakṣaṇaṃ tava bhāṣitam 
balarāmasya vakṣyāmi śṛṇu nārada lakṣaṇam  Vis 
balabhadraḥ nibhā sitā
bhikhyaḥ kundendudhavalaprabhaḥ 
paṅkajākṣo 'ṅganāvaktraḥ sarvāvayavaśobhitaḥ  Vis 
sarvālaṃkārasaṃyuktaḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ 
sarvāvayavasaṃpūrṇaḥ prabhāmaṇḍalamaṇḍitaḥ  Vis 
asya dakṣiṇabāhau tu musalaṃ vāmake kare 
halaṃ tu vinyaseddhīmān balarāmasya mantravit  Vis 
dakṣiṇe tu śriyaṃ devīṃ saumye tu garuḍaṃ nyaset 
pītaṃ kṛtāñjaliṃ tvevaṃ balarāmastvatheritaḥ  Vis 
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi kṛṣṇaṃ kṛṣṇāñjanaprabham 
sthāpanaṃ kāryamasyaiva sthānakaṃ tu viśeṣataḥ  Vis 
tribhaṅgyā saṃmitaṃ taṃ tu sthitaṃ pīṭhe mahāmune 
krīḍāyaṣṭisamāyuktaṃ devyā ca paramaṃ harim  Vis 
sthāpayeddaivike sthāne sarvajñaṃ sarvakāraṇam 
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktaṃ viviktenādhunā mune  Vis 
ataḥśyāmanibhaṃ vāpi pītāmbarasamanvitam 
vāsudevaṃ guḍākeśaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam  Vis 
krīḍāyaṣṭidharaṃ devaṃ tribhaṅgasthitisaṃyutam

triṣu mārgeṣubhāgeṣu
bhaṅgitvāt tribhaṅgitvaṃ vidhīyate

kaṭidakṣiṇato bhaṅge bhaṅgatrayamudāhṛtam 
kārayeddakṣiṇaṃ hastaṃ suyaṣṭiṃ kaṭakānvitam  Vis

vāmaṃ karatalaṃ caiva nābhisūtreṇa yojayet  Vis 
dakṣiṇaṃ kaṭihastaṃ tu vaktrasūtreṇa yojayet 
tribhāgamānamāyāmaṃ mukhaṃ mūrdhni trigolakam  Vis 
hanugrīvaṃ trimātrārdhamardhamātraṃ galaṃ smṛtam

saṃkṣepeṇa muniśreṣṭha kalkilkī

atiśoṇavaṇita
saṃkāśo triṇetro bhīmarūpavān 
śaṅkhacakragadāpāṇiścaturbāhuḥ kirīṭadhṛk  Vis

sarvālaṃkārasaṃyuktaḥ pītavastrasamanvitaḥ  Vis 
evaṃ kalkirmayā prokto hetinyāsaṃ vadāmi te

śeṣaṃ sādhāraṇaṃ smṛtam

adimūrtiḥ paro devo vāsudevaḥ sanātanaḥ  Vis

catasro mūrtayastvetāḥ pratiṣṭhāyāḥ pṛthak pṛthak  Vis

dvitīyā sthāpyate mūrtiḥ kṣatriyairmokṣakāṃkṣibhiḥ  Vis 
pradyumnākhyā tu viprendra vaiśyaiḥ sthāpyā mumukṣubhiḥ

śaṅkhakundanibhaṃ vāpi hyathavā śyāmameva ca  Vis 
śaṅkhacakragadāpāṇiṃ śrīvatsāṅkitavakṣasam 
sarvāvayavasaṃpūrṇaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam  Vis 
pītāmbarasamāyuktaṃ caturbāhuṃ kirīṭinam 
evaṃ dhyāyenmuniśreṣṭha bhuktimuktipradaṃ harim  Vis 
astravinyāsabhedaṃ ca pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu kramāt 
dakṣiṇordhvakare cakraṃ vāmordhve śaṅkhamudvahan  Vis 
gadāṃ vāmādhare haste nīrajaṃ dakṣiṇādhare

nārāyaṇamatho vakṣye śṛṇu nārada sattama 
kundapuṣpanibhaṃ vāpi śyāmaṃ vā raktameva vā  Vis 
śaṅkhacakragadāpāṇiṃ caturbāhuṃ kirīṭinam 
pītāmbarasamāyuktaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam  Vis 
sarvāvayavasaṃyuktaṃ sarvālaṃkāraśobhitam 
sarvadevamayaṃ sūkṣmaṃ trailokyādhipatiṃ harim  Vis 
evaṃ rūpaṃ tu saṃcintya hetinyāsamatho śṛṇu 
dakṣiṇe tu kare cordhve padmaṃ mukulakaṃ nyaset  Vis

śaṅkhapuṣpadalaprakhyaṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharam  Vis 
sarvāvayavasaṃpūrṇaṃ sarvālaṃkāraśobhitam 
sarvābharaṇasaṃpūrṇaṃ caturbāhuṃ kirīṭinam  Vis 
mādhavastvadhunā proktaḥ madhukaiṭabhanāśanaḥ 
astravinyāsabhedaṃ tu śṛṇu cāsya mahāmune  Vis

adhohaste nyasedraktaṃ padmaṃ ca daśapatrakam  Vis 
dakṣiṇordhvakare cakramadhastāllakuṭaṃ nyaset

pītavastraṃ caturbāhuṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam

śaṅkhacakragadāpāṇiṃ pītavastraṃ caturbhujam 
sarvālaṃkārasaṃyuktaṃ dhyāyedviṣṇuṃ sanātanam  Vis

śaṅkhacakragadāpāṇiṃ sarvāvayavaśobhitam

sarvāvayavasaṃpūrṇaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam 
sarvālaṃkārasaṃyuktaṃ sarvasiddhipradaṃ param  Vis

madhusūdanamūrtasya lakṣaṇaṃ viddhi nārada

taptahāṭakasaṃkāśaṃ śyāmaṃ vagninibhaṃ tu vā 
sarvālaṃkārasaṃyuktaṃ sarvāvayavaśobhitam  Vis 
sarvābharaṇasaṃyuktaṃ pītavastraṃ caturbhujam

trivikramasya saṃproktaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ ca samṛddhidam 
gadāṃ prathamahaste tu hyadhastāccakramudvahan  Vis 
vāme padmamadhaḥśaṅkhaṃ dṛśyate yatra kutracit 
yathākāmaṃ tu vā cāstravinyāsaṃ munisattama  Vis 
evaṃ cāyudhavinyāso prokto vāmana ucyate 
karṇikāradalaprakhyaṃ raktavarṇaṃ caturbhujam  Vis 
sarvāvayavasaṃpūrṇaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam 
sarvālaṃkārasaṃyuktaṃ sarvasiddhipradaṃ param  Vis

taptajāmbūnadaprakhyaṃ śrīvatsāṅkitavakṣasam  Vis 
sarvāvayavasaṃpūrṇaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam 
pītavastraṃ caturbāhuṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharam  Vis 
śrīdharasya mayā proktaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ bhuktimuktidam 
ūrdhve cakramadhaḥ padmaṃ dakṣiṇe tu kare nyaset  Vis 
vāme caiva gadā jñeyā hyadhaḥśaṅkhaṃ virājitam 
tathā śrīdharamūrtistu vijñeyā deśikottamaiḥ  Vis 
evaṃ pradyumnabhedastu aniruddhākhya ucyate 
nīlotpaladalaprakhyaṃ caturbāhuṃ kirīṭinam  Vis 
śaṅkhacakragadāpāṇiṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam 
śrīvatsavakṣasopetaṃ hṛṣīkeśaṃ sanātanam  Vis 
dakṣiṇe 'sya mahācakra gadāṃ ca tadadhaḥsthitām 
vāmahaste mahāpadmamadhastācchaṅkhameva ca  Vis 
sā mūrtistu tadā jñeyā hṛṣīkeśetiśasyanārada 
padmanābhasya vakṣye 'haṃ lakṣaṇaṃ bhuktimuktidam  Vis 
nīlavarṇanibhaṃ vātha śyāmaṃ vā munisattama 
saṃjñātvā lakṣaṇaṃ tatra sarvajñaṃ sarvakāraṇam  Vis 
kārayenmuniśārdūla śilpibhiḥ saha sādhakaḥ 
sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpannaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam  Vis 
sarvāvayavasaṃpūrṇaṃ caturbāhuṃ kirīṭinam 
śaṅkhacakragadāpāṇiṃ pītāmbarasamanvitam  Vis 
śrīvatsavakṣasopetaṃ padmanābhamavaive hi tam 
prathame 'sya kare padmamadhastācchaṅkha eva tu  Vis 
vāme ca dṛśyate cakraṃ gadā ca tadadhaḥ sthitā 
sā mūrtiḥ padmanābheti namaskāryā vicakṣaṇaiḥ  Vis 
vinyasedvā yathākāmaṃ śastravinyāsamatra tu 
atha vā padmanābhasya lakṣaṇaṃ śṛṇu suvrata  Vis 
dvibhujaṃ paṅkajākṣaṃ tu śyāmaṃ vāgninibhaṃ tu vā 
dhyāyettasmin muniśreṣṭha kārayellakṣaṇairyutam  Vis 
śayane sati saṃproktaṃ padmanābhasya nārada 
atra karmārcanādīnāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ vakṣyate 'dhunā  Vis 
yogamudrāsamāyuktaṃ śaṅkhacakrasamanvitam 
kārayettu muniśreṣṭha karmārcāṃ pūrvavattu vā  Vis 
ityevaṃ padmanābhasya lakṣaṇaṃ parikīrtitam 
bhittipārśve 'sya nābhyūrdhve raktapadmaṃ sunālakam  Vis

tadardhaṃ vārdhakaṃ vāpi dalaṃ padmasya nārada  Vis 
karṇikāgre vidhiṃ dhyāyet lakṣaṇaiḥsaha nārada

padmāsanasamāyuktaṃ vidhiṃ kanakasaṃnibham 
caturbhujaṃ samāsīnaṃ caturvaktraṃ sanātanam  Vis 
sarvāvayavasaṃpūrṇaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam 
sarvadevamayaṃ sūkṣmaṃ sṛṣṭisthitilayātmakam  Vis 
evaṃ rūpaṃ tato dhyāyet brahmāṇaṃ kamalodbhavam 
brahmaṇo dakṣiṇe haste sruksruvākṣāṃśca vinyaset  Vis 
vāmahaste nyaset padmaṃ ūrdhve caiva kamaṇḍalum 
abhayaṃ varadaṃ vāpi vāmahastādharaṃ mune  Vis 
evaṃ rūpaṃ tu saṃcintya brahmāṇaṃ kamalāsanam 
atha vā kārayennyāsaṃ śṛṇu guhyopari kramāt  Vis 
viparītena hastābhyāmūrumūle tu saṃspṛśet 
aṅgulyagre muniśreṣṭha yogamudre 'yamucyate  Vis 
yogamudrā mayā proktā sarvayogeṣu yojayet 
asya dakṣiṇapārśve tu medhāṃ vāme sarasvatīm  Vis 
vinyasecca svatantre tu paratantre tayorvinā 
evaṃ kṛtvā vidhānena brahmāṇaṃ kamalāsanam  Vis 
padmanābhasya mūrtāṅgaṃ paratantramiti smṛtam 
svatantre muniśārdūla śilpibhiḥ saha mantravit  Vis 
kalpayedvidhivat padmaṃ saṃsthāpya kamalāsanam 
brahmasthāne 'thavā pūrve dakṣiṇe paścime 'tha vā  Vis 
grāmasyottarapārśve vā kalpayedāspadaṃ kramāt

yajamānecchayā kalpyo prāsādo vidhivat kramāt

śṛṇu devamuniśreṣṭha mantrānukramaṇaṃ param 
soddhāraṇaṃ ṛṣiśchando daivaṃ varṇādimeva ca  Vis

anyaṃ tathāgatādyaṃ syādagnimāyudhasaṃhṛtiḥ  Vis 
paramātmā dvitīyaṃ tu tṛtīyaṃ vāsudevakam 
saṃkarṣaṇaṃ tato mantraṃ pradyumnasya tathaiva ca  Vis 
aniruddhasya vidyā ca matsyamantramanantaram 
kūrmavidyā tataḥ kroḍaṃ daśamaṃ nārasiṃhakam  Vis 
paścādvāmanamantraṃ ca jāmadagnyamataḥ param 
vidyā dāśaratherūrdhvaṃ balarāmamanantaram  Vis

nārāyaṇasya vidyāṃ tāṃ mādhavasya punaḥ kramāt  Vis 
govindasyāpi viṣṇośca madhusūdanavidyayā 
traivikramaṃ vāmanaṃ ca śrīdharākhyamatho mune  Vis 
hṛṣīkeśaṃ ca mantraṃ ca padmanābhamataḥ param 
brahmamantraṃ tathā caiva dāmodaramanukramāt  Vis 
viśvarūpasya mantraṃ ca yajñamūrterataḥ param 
vedamūrteratho mudrāmantraṃ śrīmantrameva ca  Vis 
puṣṭividyā tathā medhāvidyā sarasvatī tathā

puruṣasya ca vidyā ca viśvamantramataḥ param

yajuṣāmāntalāntaṃ ca sāntamāntena yojayet 
praṇavena puṭīkṛtya dvitīyaṃ bindunā yutam  Vis 
namasā bhagavānekādaśayuktaṃ paraḥ param

turīyādi sahaihāraṃ sacūḍāmaṇiṣāntakam  Vis 
vargādimanyakāreṇa śāntaṇonantaraṃ tathā 
māntamāntaṃ tathākāramuddharet sādhakottamaḥ  Vis 
amityādyuparataṃ me kuryānnamaḥ śabdamanantaram 
bhagavantaṃ caturthyantaṃ pañcamānilamātiyuk  Vis 
caturthasya tṛtīyena vāyupañcamabheditam

pañcamaṃ ca caturthaṃ ca prathamasya tṛtīyakam  Vis 
lāntaṃ tu turyapūrvā ca svaraikādaśasaṃyutam

pañcamasvarayuktyā tu turīyaṃ tricaturthakam 
āntāntamanilaṃ paścāt ṣoḍaśasvaramuddharet  Vis 
anilādimathāddhṛtyānalamaukārameva ca

vāntadevāyamatpūrvaṃ ṣāntavāyuṃ tathāyakaḥ 
tato vāyuṃ ca rūpāya mantrādīṃśca tatoddharet  Vis 
dvitīyaṃ binduśīrṣeṇa lānto nāthopari nyaset 
namasā bhagavacchabdaṃ viṣṇuśabdaṃ ca pūrvavat  Vis 
ṣaṭśikhaṃ kaṃ ca vahniṃ ca makāreṇātha kūrparam 
ṣaṣṭhasvaraṃ ca pānteyamuddharenmantravittamaḥ  Vis 
nikāmādibakārāntaṃ ṣaṣṭhasvaravibhūṣitam 
savisargaṃ namaḥ śabdaṃ bhagavacchabdamuddharet  Vis 
ekārāntaṃ śakārādi makārāntaṃ ca yāntakam 
sāntaṃ dvitīyasaṃyuktaṃ vāyumāntaṃ ca bhūriti  Vis 
āntāyaṃ mukhamuddhṛtya lāntaṃ binducaturdaśaiḥ 
yathāmatau tathāntepi namo bhagavate tathā  Vis

padmanābhasya tu muniḥ vaiśampāyana ucyate

āditaḥtyaḥ

lakṣmyādikramayogena pūjayettu dine dine

mūlaberasya devīnāṃ pratiṣṭhāmātrayāma pyalam 
vivāhādikramastatra neṣyate munisattama  Vis 
svabījaireva kartavyaṃ sthāpanaṃ munisattama 
medhā sarasvatīdurgetyevamādiṣu mūrtiṣu  Vis 
evamāduṣu kartavyaḥ pratiṣṭhādikramo mune 
prokṣayet svasvamantraistu brahmakumbhasthavāriṇā  Vis 
svaiḥ svairmantraistu saṃsthāpya pūjayettu vidhānataḥ 
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktaḥ devīnāṃ sthāpanakramaḥ  Vis 
evaṃ yaḥ kārayedbhaktyā śaktīnāṃ sthāpanaṃ param 
āyuraiśvaryaputrādīn sarvān kāmānavāpnuyāt  Vis 
iha loke sukhaṃ labdhvā paraloke tathaiva ca

atra kaścidviśeṣo 'sti śrīvatsasya haripriyam 
lakṣaṇaṃ sthānabhedaṃ ca mantramārādhanaṃ tathā  Vis 
evamādīni cānyāni viśeṣāṇimahāmune

sarvasaṃpatsamṛddhyarthaṃ sarvakāmaśubhapradam 
suvarṇarajatenāpi tathā tāmramayena tu  Vis 
uttamadikrameṇaiva kārayet phalakāspadam 
ṣaḍaṅgulaṃ tathāyāmaṃ tasya vistārameva ca  Vis 
pañcāṅgulāyataṃ vāpi tanmadhye tatsamaṃ bhavet 
dvyaṅgulaṃ tasya vistāraṃ maulerekāṅgulaṃ tu vā  Vis 
evaṃ jñātvā muniśreṣṭha kuryādāspadamuttamam

ekāṅgulavihīnaṃ tu madhyamaṃ paripaṭhyate

tryaṅgulalena
vihīnaṃ tat kuryāttasyādhamādhamam 
madhyamādhamakārye 'smin adhamādhamameva ca  Vis 
tasyānurūpataḥ kuryāt vistāraṃ munisattama

sādhayet kamalāṃ devīṃ taptakāñcanasaṃnibhām 
sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyuktāṃ padmāsanasamanvitām  Vis 
padmahastāṃ śriyaṃ devīṃ padmanābhapriyāṃ śubhām

evaṃ saṃcintya tāṃ devīṃ śriyaṃ trailokyanāyakīm 
harervakṣasi pārśve tu dakṣiṇe munisattama  Vis 
sthāpayettāṃ śriyaṃ devīṃ jagatsaṃrakṣaṇārthakam 
sarvasaṃpatsamṛddhyarthamiti śāstrasya niścayaḥ  Vis

gandhapuṣpaistu saṃpūjya saṃsmaredamṛtārṇavam 
tanmadhye pūrvavat kuryāt jalavāsaṃ vidhānataḥ  Vis 
etat krameṇa vā kuryāt acyutasya mahāmune 
darpaṇe saṃsthite bere citrādīnāṃ viśeṣataḥ  Vis

kārayejjalavāsaṃ tat kanīyasamudāhṛtam  Vis 
jalādhivāsane prokto viśeṣo munisattama 
dviprakāraṃ mayā proktaṃ yathāyogaṃ samācaret  Vis 
mūlaberāttu tāṃ devīmāvāhyātraiva yojayet 
mūlamantreṇa matimān kumbhatoyena hastayoḥ  Vis 
saṃyojyātraiva mantreṇa sādhakaḥ paramārthavit 
mantrakośe mayā proktastantre 'smin munisattama  Vis 
saṃproktaṃ paramaṃ mantraṃ guhyadguhyaṃ varapradam 
tenaiva prokṣayeddevīṃ mahākumbhasthavāriṇā  Vis 
taddehe nyāsamārgeṇa vinyasettantravittamaḥ 
pañcaviṃśatitattvāni tatpañcākṣarameva ca  Vis 
śaṅkhacakrābjamudrāṃ tu darśayettantravittamaḥ 
tatastvārādhayeddevīmardhyādyaṣṭopacārakaiḥ  Vis 
arghyaṃ pādyaṃ tathācāmaṃ gandhapuṣpaṃ tathaiva ca 
dhūpadīpaṃ nivedyaṃ ca pāyasaṃ gulasaṃyutam  Vis 
evamuktaprakāreṇa ghaṇṭādundubhisaṃyutam 
kārayed balidānaṃ tu sarvakāmapradaṃ śubham  Vis 
bilvapatrākṣatairyuktaṃ padmaṃ pālāśamutpalam 
karavīrādisaṃyuktaṃ pūjayet kamalālayām  Vis

pāyasānnaṃga gulopetaṃ bilvapatrāṅkurairyutam  Vis

kārayedbalidānaṃ tu sarvakarmakāma 
pradaṃ śubham

tanmadhye pūjayellakṣmīṃ lakṣmayai nama iti bruvan  Vis 
praṇavādisamāyuktaṃ pañcākṣaramiti smṛtam 
tasyāgre tu baliṃ kuryāt pūvoktena vidhānataḥ  Vis 
gandhapuṣpasamāyuktaṃ dhūpadīpasamanvitam 
evaṃ saṃpūjayitvā tu mukhavāsaṃ pradāpeyat  Vis 
balyante tu muniśreṣṭha śrīsūktaṃ tu paṭhet tridhā 
śrīmantraṃ tatstutiṃ vāpi paṭhettantravicakṣaṇaḥ  Vis 
tataḥ pañcamahāśabdaṃ ghoṣayecca punaḥ punaḥ 
pūrvavat pūjayeddevīṃ sāyāhne munisattama  Vis 
pūjānte kārayeddhomaṃ samidājyacarūnapi 
bilvādyanyatamasyātha padmakuṇḍe yathecchayā  Vis 
saṃkalpyaikaṃ muniśreṣṭha tanmadhye homamācaret 
bilvapālāśasamidhaḥ pratyekaṃ ṣoḍaśāhutīḥ  Vis 
juhuyānmūlamantreṇa kapilājyena homayet 
tathaiva pāyasaṃ brahman juhuyāt ṣoḍaśāhutīḥ  Vis 
tathaiva bilvapatraiśca padmairekadalairapi 
sākṣataiḥ karavīraistu juhuyāttu punaḥ punaḥ  Vis 
homaṃ kṛtvā tu vidhivat kuṇḍāddevīṃ samuddharet 
taddhomaḥ paramo guhyaḥ grāmarājñorvivṛddhikṛt  Vis 
sarvarogavinirmuktarṃmoktā
sarvakāmapradaḥ śubhaḥ 
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena rātrau homaṃ samācaret  Vis 
homānte dakṣiṇāṃ dadyāt yathāvittāmusārataḥ 
ācāryaṃ pūjayet paścāddhemavastrāṅgulīyakaiḥ  Vis 
brāhmaṇān pūjayet paścāddaivajñamanupūjayet 
uktalakṣaṇahīnena yadi kuryāt pramādataḥ  Vis 
grāmarājñośca rāṣṭrasya yajamānasya nāśanam 
na phalanti kriyāstatra nātra kāryā vicāraṇā  Vis 
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena kārayedvidhicoditam

viśeṣaścātra saṃproktaḥ śeṣaṃ pūrvāvadācaret

viṣvaksenaḥ
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi cāṅganyāsādilakṣaṇam 
śṛṇu guhyamanā bhūtvā sādhakānāṃ hitāya vai  Vis 
aṅganyāsakramaṃ caiva mudrāyā lakṣaṇaṃ tathā 
phalāni vividhānyatra sarvavidyāprakāśakam   Vis 
ācāryaḥ prayato bhūtvā prāṅmukho vāpyudaṅmukhaḥ 
paṅkajaṃ vāsanaṃ baddhvā svastikaṃ vā yathecchayā  Vis 
pūjārambhe 'ñjaliṃ kṛtvā namaskṛtya yathāvidhi 
uttāne vāmahastāgre tiryagdakṣiṇamañjasā  Vis 
maṇḍalākṛti saṃspṛśya
vāmāntamitareṇa tu 
vāmāṅguṣṭhaṃ tato baddhvā muṣṭyordhvāṅguṣṭhayā mune  Vis 
muṣṭiṃ kṛtvā gato dhāma dhyātvā mantraṃ samāhitaḥ 
saṃspṛśya hṛdayaṃ devaṃ trimātre śirasā tathā  Vis 
praṇamya pāṇivyatyāsaṃ baddhvā mudrāṃ tathā punaḥ 
praviśyāñjalimudrāṃ tu pūjāmantreṇa mantravit  Vis 
namo 'ntaṃ hṛdayaṃ mūrdhni śikhāyāṃ kavace tathā 
astre netre tato dhyātvā taccihnena nyasedbudhaḥ  Vis 
mudrāyā lakṣaṇaṃ cāpi niruktaṃ ca tataḥ śṛṇu 
labdhayā tu yayā yasmāt sādhako devavairiṇām  Vis 
drāvayīta mudaṃ tasmāt mudrā tallakṣaṇaṃ śṛṇu 
baddhāyāstu bahirmuṣṭyā ṛjumaṅguṣṭhamāyatam  Vis 
kṛtvāto madhyamāyāṃ tu tanmūlaṃ hṛdaye spṛśet 
āhṛtya tarjanīṃ samyak baddhvāṅguṣṭhena muṣṭikam  Vis 
athāṅguṣṭhalalāṭānte śikhordhvamahatīṃ tathā  
bṛhadagradvayenaiva kṣudramudrasya
bandhanam  Vis 
hastābhyāmūrdhvamāyamya kṛtvā cānābhimaṇḍalam 
kavacasya dhiyā nyasya kavacasya tu mudrikā  Vis 
aparāstrasya mudraiṣā kathyate dakṣiṇāgrakam 
muṣṭiṃ baddhvā tatastarjanyagramaṅguṣṭharekhayā  Vis 
spṛṣṭvā sphoṭamudakṣepaḥ pūrvādi daśadikṣvapi 
kaniṣṭhānāmike baddhvā nahatā talamadhyage  Vis 
tarjanīmadhyamāgrābhyāṃ netrayornetramudrikā 
madhyamutthāpitaṃ kṛtvā hastaṃ saṃkocya yatnataḥ  Vis 
kanīyasaṃ tu saṃhṛtya śeṣayorubhayorapi 
atho vaktramukhāṃ śeṣāṅgulinā vāmakena tu   Vis 
kareṇa dakṣiṇaṃ spṛṣṭvā bhrāmayeddīpamudrikā 
lalāṭe hṛdi vā samyak saṃpuṭo 'ñjalirūrdhvagaḥ  Vis 
nāmnā mudreyaṃ vijñeyā praṇāme 'ñjalimudrikā 
uktānāmiha vānyeṣvapyanuktānāṃ prayatnataḥ  Vis 
pradarśane 'pyaśaktaḥ san añjaliṃ tu pradarśayet 
añjalirnāma mudreyaṃ sarvamudrāmayā priyā  Vis 
viṣṇoḥ praṇāmamudraiṣā sarvakāmān pradāpayet 
etābhirnyastasarvāṅgo japahomādikān mune  Vis 
yaḥ karoti svarakṣāṃ ca dīrghamāyuryaśaskaram 
sukhamaiśvaryabalatāṃ kalpyatāṃ ca labhet parām  Vis 
vidyā hi vividhāṃ śreṣṭhāṃ bhuktimuktistathaiva ca

mūrtimantraprakāreṇa sādhakaḥ sakṛdarcayet 
tasya sarvamabhiprāyaṃ siddhyatyeva na saṃśayaḥ  Vis 
anāvṛṣṭibhayaṃ nāsti ativṛṣṭibhayaṃ tathā 
vyādhidurbhikṣacorādi pīḍākālamṛtistathā  Vis 
bahunātra pralāpena kiṃ sarvān sādhayiṣyati 
yadyat kāmayate svasya samṛddhaṃ puruṣo bhuvi  Vis 
tattadeva labhet samyak harestasya nivedayet 
sādhakaścāpi vā bhaktyā prayataḥ samyagarcayet  Vis 
tattatsarvaṃ labhedevaṃ mṛṣṭānnaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ 
nṛpo vā nṛpamātro vā vedamantraistathā mune  Vis 
mūrtimantrairaśakto vā svadravyairarcanādikān 
kārayīta muniśreṣṭha sādhakena yathāvidhi  Vis 
saphalaṃ sukṛtaṃ prāpya viṣṇusārūpyamṛcchati

viṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
viṣvaksenaḥ
śṛṇu nārada tattvena sādhakānāṃ hitāya vai 
pūjābhedaṃ pravakṣyāmi paramātmādimūrtiṣu  Vis 
pūte manorame deśe vane puṇyatame 'pi vā 
tīrthe vā kṣetravarye vā grāme vā nagare 'pi vā  Vis 
kharvaṭe kheṭake vāpi pattane vā taṭe taṭe 
mahāgrāme viśeṣeṇa paścime madhyame 'pi vā  Vis 
kārayenmandiraṃ samyak saumyaṃ sumanasāṃ prabhoḥ 
viṣṇoḥ pūrvoktamārgeṇa kalpayedbahuberakam  Vis 
lakṣaṇaṃ pūrvamuktena tatra yadyekaberakam  
rāmatrayādikānāṃ tu kalyayedbahuberakam  Vis 
ātmārthaberamekaṃ vā svatantraparatantrayoḥ 
pūjābhedaḥ suramune kiñcikaści
dasti taducyate  Vis 
āvāhanaṃ visargaṃ ca svatantre triṣu sandhiṣu 
agnikāryaṃ baliṃ caiva paratantreṣu tairvinā  Vis 
ātmarthe phalakāyāṃ vā paṭe vālikhya yatnataḥ 
pūrvoktalakṣaṇopetaṃ pratiṣṭhāyāḥ krameṇa ca  Vis 
saṃprokṣya navaratnānvā āvāhyabhyarcayeta vā 
sthaṇḍile pratimāyāṃ vā lauhyāmicchānurūpataḥ  Vis 
indranīlaṃ maratakaṃ sphaṭikaṃ vajrameva ca 
padmarāgaṃ pravālaṃ ca vaiḍūryaṃ muktameva ca  Vis 
māṇikkamiti ratnāni nava teṣāṃ yathākramam 
kālaṃ vakṣye tathārcāyāḥ prātarmadhyāhna eva ca  Vis 
sāyāhnaśca pradoṣaścāpyardharātramuṣastathā 
iti ṣaṭkaṃ parārthe tu pūjāyāmuttamaṃ smṛtam  Vis 
madhyamārādhane sāyamuṣaśca parivarjayet 
adhame cārdharātraṃ ca sāyāhnaṃ ca vivarjayet  Vis 
prātarmadhyapradoṣeṣu balibhramaṇamācaret 
nānyeṣūttamapūjāyāmapi vā madhyamārcane  Vis 
balihīne tu kāle tu pūjābhedamatho śṛṇu 
āhvānamarghyapādyaṃ ca ācāmaṃ gandhapuṣpakam  Vis 
dhūpo dīpo nivedyaṃ ca mukhavāsavisarjane 
iti karmottamādīnāṃ nāḍīkālaḥ pravakṣyate  Vis 
prathamā saptanāḍī syāt madhyamā pañcanāḍikā 
kanīyasī trināḍī syāt iti śāstrasya niścayaḥ  Vis 
divākarodayāt pūrvamācāryaḥ snānamācaret 
arkodaye muniśreṣṭha pūjākarma samācaret  Vis 
snānapūrvāḥ kriyāḥsarvāḥ phalasaṃsiddhihetavaḥ 
atastānstat
prathamaṃ vakṣye sādhakānāṃ hitāya vai  Vis 
samudragāminyo vāpi hrade nadyāṃ jalādiṣu 
taṭāke nirjhare vāpi snānaṃ kurvīta sādhakaḥ  Vis 
brāhme muhūrte cotthāya dharmamokṣārthacintakaḥ 
prāgudagdiśamāsādya sādhakaḥ snānamācaret  Vis 
prācyuttare nīrarāśau snānaṃ kuryādvicakṣaṇaḥ 
vāyavye nairṛtāgneyyāṃ varuṇāyāṃ visarjayet  Vis 
varjite deśanīre tu yo mohāt snānamācaret 
tat snānaṃ niṣphalaṃ yāti punaḥsnānaṃ samācaret  Vis 
prātarutthāya mūrtīnāṃ yāṃ mūrtiṃ svayamarcati 
tanmūrtyarcanamantreṇa sādhakaḥ snānamācaret  Vis 
viṣṇumantreṇa vā sāṅgamathavā mūlavidyayā 
avagāhya jale madhye trirācamya ca mantrataḥ  Vis 
visṛjyārdrāmbaraṃ cānyat vastrayugmena veṣṭayet 
sapavitrakareṇaiva mantrācamanamācaret  Vis 
suvārṇādyaṅgulīyaivāyaṃ vā
dhārayeddakṣiṇe bhuje kare

tarpayet svasvamantreṇa snānakarma samācaret 
aśaktaḥ punarācamya proktāṃ vidyāmanusmaran  Vis 
saṃprokṣya snānakāryāṇi kṛtvā kāryaṃ viśedbudhaḥ 
praviśya kṛtasacchaucaḥ pūjāmantreṇa mantravit  Vis 
kavāṭodghāṭanaṃ kṛtvā mantreṇādyena vā mune 
vāyumantreṇa vā dvāraṃ kavāṭoddhāṭanaṃ kramāt  Vis 
taddvāraṃ tu dvidhā kṛtvā sādhako mantravittamaḥ 
sūtrasyottarapārśve tu pratiśeddakṣiṇāṅghriṇā  Vis 
praṇamya sādhako mantraṃ ṣaḍakṣaramanusmaran 
nityadīpaṃ tato jvālya viṣṇumantreṇa mantravit  Vis 
sūtrasya dakṣiṇe pārśve uttarābhimukhaḥ svayam 
same śucau pradeśe tu kṛṣṇājinakuśāstare  Vis 
phalake vā samāsīnaḥ svasthāntaḥkaraṇaḥśuciḥ 
padmaṃ vā svastikaṃ vāpi baddhvā svecchānurūpataḥ  Vis 
tena mantreṇa digbandhamaṣṭadikṣu niveśayet 
rakṣārthaṃ yāgadeśaṃ taditi tattvārthadarśinaḥ  Vis 
evaṃ kṛtvā tu digbandhaṃ prāṇāyāmamathārabhet 
savyāhṛtiṃ sapraṇavāṃ gāyatrīṃ śirasā saha  Vis 
prāṇānāyamya yastisraḥ prāṇāyāmottamaḥ smṛtaḥ 
pañcaviṃśatikṛtvāntaḥ prāṇānāyamya mānasaḥ  Vis 
abhyāso 'ṣṭākṣarasyaikaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ sa madhyamaḥ 
prāṇo vāyuḥ śarīrasthaḥ tasyāyāmo nirodhakaḥ  Vis 
pūrakaṃ kumbhakaṃ caiva recakaṃ trividha smṛtam 
jānuṃ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya na drutaṃ na vilambitam  Vis 
kriyate cāṅgulisphoṭaḥ sā
mātrā parikīrtitaḥ 
tathā dvādaśamātrābhiḥ pūrakaṃ kriyate kramāt  Vis 
tasmāddviguṇamātrābhiḥ kumbhakaṃ kriyate budhaiḥ 
tathaiva recakaṃ kṛtvā budhāstattvārthadarśinaḥ  Vis 
prāṇāyāmamidaṃ proktamadhamaṃ mutisattama 
tripradhāne vidhāne 'tra yathāsaṃbhavamācaret  Vis 
prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ kṛtvā pañca vā sapta vāthavā 
prāṇāyāmaṃ prakurvīta prāṇāyāmavidāṃ vara  Vis 
tatastu kāyaśuddhyarthaṃ varṇaṃ dhūmrādi vinyaset 
śabdaḥsparśaśca rūpaṃ ca raso gandhaśca pañcamaḥ  Vis 
ahaṅkāramano buddhiyuktamātmānamānayet 
sadāviṣṇau tu saṃyojya dhātudehaṃ suśodhayet  Vis 
yadbījaṃ nābhimadhyasthaṃ dhūmraṃ caṇḍānilātmakam 
viśoṣayedaśeṣaṃ tu dhyāyeddehasthakalmaṣam  Vis 
kṣaumaṃ hṛtpadmamadhyasthaṃ bījaṃ tejomayaṃ smaret 
athordhvatiryagābhiśca jvālābhiḥ kalmaṣaṃ dahet  Vis 
śaśāṅkākṛtivaddhāyannambarasthaṃ sudhāmbudhim 
hṛtpadmavyāpibhirdehaṃ svakarma bhrāmayet sudhīḥ  Vis 
suṣumnā yogamārgeṇa sarvanāḍīvisarpibhiḥ 
paścācchabdādiviṣayān yojayenmūrdhnimadhyame  Vis 
evaṃ cāmṛtarūpaṃ tu mayā proktaṃ tu nārada

aṅguṣṭhānāmikābhyāṃ tu kṣaumabījaṃ hṛdi nyaset

bījamuttamam  Vis 
yakārādi vakārāntaṃ dhūmramavyāruṇāsitam 
evaṃ saṃśodhya dehaṃ tu ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ samācaret  Vis 
ūrdhvapuṇḍravidhiṃ vakṣye śṛṇu nārada tattvataḥ 
sarvāghanāśanaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvatīrthaphalapradam  Vis 
svamūrtyarcanamantreṇa lalāṭādi kakutparam 
candanaṃ śvetamṛd bilvatulasīmūlatoyakaiḥ  Vis 
ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ likhedvidvānanāmikyā tu sādhakaḥ 
dvādaśa śaiḥ 
dvādaśairmāsairnāmabhirvā viśuddhaye  Vis 
evaṃ pūto bhavedūrdhvapuṇḍrāṇāṃ dhāraṇānmune 
sṛṣṭisthityādivaśato hastāṅganyāsayordvayoḥ  Vis 
vinābhyapyar
cā phalavatī mūrtimantraprabhāvataḥ 
ārādhanakramaṃ vakṣye dvārapūjādi nārada  Vis 
sādhakaḥsiddhasarvāṅgaḥ subhago rogavarjitaḥ 
kuṣṭhāpasmārarahito dvārapūjāṃ samācaret  Vis 
caṇḍapracaṇḍagaruḍāḥ caturthyantaṃ namo 'ntakam 
dakṣiṇottarapūrve tupūrveṣu
dvāre ca praṇavaiḥ saha  Vis 
caṇḍādhare tu cakraṃ syāt pracaṇḍasyādhare 'mbujam 
gandhapuppādibhirdvārapūjāmevaṃ samācaret  Vis 
athavā dvārapūjāyāḥ kramaṃ śṛṇu mahāmune 
caṇḍādīn pūrvavat pūjya cakrādirahitena tu  Vis 
dhātāraṃ pūjayedvāme vidhātāraṃ tu dakṣiṇe 
sūtrasya dakṣiṇe sthitvā ācāryo mantravitamaḥ  Vis 
adhobhāge tu bhūmiḥ syāduparyaṅgaṃ pūjayecchriyam 
durgā gaṇapatī caiva kavāṭasthau prapūjayet  Vis 
śaṅgapadmanidhī caiva śākhayormūladeśataḥ 
gaṅgāṃ ca yamunāṃ caiva kavāṭādhārake nyaset  Vis 
utkarṣaṇīṃ karṣaṇīṃ ca antaryantre hyadhopari 
gandhapuṣpākṣatairdhūpaiḥ dīpādyairdvāramarcayet  Vis 
atha caṇḍaṃ pracaṇḍaṃ ca garuḍāntaṃḍaṃ ca
samarcayet 
praṇavādi snanāmnā ca mantramityabhidhīyate  Vis 
pūrvavat pūjayeddvāradevāṃstantravicakṣaṇaḥ 
triprakāraṃ mayā proktaṃ yathāyogaṃ samācaret  Vis 
praṇavādisvanāmnā ca pūjayediha nārada 
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktaḥ dvārapūjāvidhikramaḥ  Vis 
kāṃsyaghaṇṭādhvaniṃ kṛtvā dvāramācchādya vāsasā 
praviśeddevapārśve tu sādhakaḥ saṃyatendriyaḥ  Vis 
pūvoktamāsanaṃ kṛtvā devasyāsanamārabhet 
sauvarṇe rājate vātha tāmre vātha mahāmune  Vis 
kuśena vātha puṣpeṇa kalpayedāsanaṃ hareḥ 
devasya purataḥ kṛtvā hyāsanaṃ saṃyatendriyaḥ  Vis 
ādhāraḥ praṇavo jñeyaḥ śaktirvāgīśvarī tathā 
kandaṃ ca pṛthivīṃ smṛtyatvā
nālamākāśarūpakam  Vis 
nālasyāgre smaret padmaṃ hṛtpadmaṃ paramālayam 
ādhārādīni sarvāṇi hyāsanasya mahāmune  Vis 
ajñānāt kalpayenmohāt niṣphalaṃ syānna saṃśayaḥ 
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena ādhārādīni kalpayet  Vis 
ādhāraṃ prathamaṃ nyasya śaktiṃ caiva tataḥ param 
śaktyopari nyaseddhīmān kandaṃ caiva mahāmune  Vis 
kandasyopari vinyasya nālamākāśarūpakam 
nālasyāgre tu vinyasya dharmādīni yathākramam  Vis 
dharmādīnāṃ tu tanmadhye padmaṃ śvetāṣṭapatrakam 
dharmaṃ jñānaṃ ca vairāgyaṃ aiśvaryaṃ ca catuṣṭayam  Vis 
catvāryetāni koṇeṣu āgneyādiṣu vinyaset 
madhye tu rudraṃ vinyasya nālamūlasya madhyame  Vis 
adharmājñāna nā
vairāgyānaiśvaryaṃ ca catuṣṭayam 
vinyasecca caturdikṣu pūrvādiṣu yathākramam  Vis 
dharmādīni nyasedādau mantreṇādyena saṃyutam 
svanāmnā caiva sarveṣāṃ mantramityabhidhīyate  Vis 
adharmādīni sarveṣāṃ svasvanāmnā ca sādhakaḥ 
vinyasecca caturdikṣu pūrvādikramayogataḥ  Vis 
evaṃ nyāsaṃ kramāt kṛtvā hyādhārādi mahāmune 
nāradaḥ
dharmajñānādirūpāṇi śrotumicchāmyahaṃ prabho  Vis 
āyudhāni ca sarveṣāṃ yathāvadvaktumarhasi 
viṣvaksenaḥ
śṛṇu nārada tattvajña viṣṇupādaparāyaṇa  Vis 
dharmādīnāṃ svarūpāṇi pravakṣyāmyāyudhāni ca 
caturvaktraṃ caturbāhuṃ dvipādaṃ cāsitānanam  Vis 
śaṅkhacakradharaṃ saumyaṃ pītāmbarasamanvitam 
jātipuṣpadalaprakhyaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam  Vis 
dharmamūrtiriti khyātaṃ jñānamūrtiṃ bravīmi te 
dvipādaṃ ca caturbāhuṃ caturvaktraṃ sanātanam  Vis 
nīlotpaladalaprakhyaṃ śaṅkacakragadādharam 
jñānamūrtiriti khyātaṃ vairāgyasya vadāmyaham  Vis 
raktākṣitrayasaṃyuktaṃ caturvaktraṃ caturbhujam 
pītāmbaradharaṃ saumyaṃ śaṅkhacakradharaṃ sadā  Vis 
karṇikāradalaprakhyaṃ vāyavyaṃ diśamāśritam 
vairāgyasyemi
ti nirdiṣṭaṃ aiśvaryasya vadāmi te  Vis 
raktotpaladalaprakhyaṃ caturvaktraṃ caturbhujam 
pītābhbadharaṃ saumyaṃ śaṅkhacakradharaṃ sadā  Vis 
sitānanasamāyuktaṃ muktāhārasamanvitam 
aiśvaryasyeti nirdiṣṭamīśvarasya vadāmi te  Vis 
kundendumukta
saṃkāśaṃ dvipādaṃ ca caturbhujam 
raktākṣitrayasaṃyuktaṃ jaṭāmakuṭadhāriṇam  Vis 
pītāmbaradharaṃ saumyaṃ paraśuṃīśvaraṃ
śūladhāriṇam 
sarvābharaṇasaṃyuktaṃ sarvaśobhitaśobhanam  Vis 
itthaṃ harasya rūpaṃ tu devarṣe viddhi nārada 
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktaṃ dharmajñānādirūpakam  Vis 
adharmādīni gātrāṇi 
vakṣyāmi śṛṇu nārada 
raktavarṇaṃ mahākāyaṃ kambugrīvaṃ caturbhujam  Vis 
ekavaktraṃ bṛhatkukṣiṃ netratrayasamanvitam 
raktāmbaradharaṃ raudraṃ khaṅgamudgaradhāriṇam  Vis 
adharmasayaivamuktaṃ tu ajñānasya vadāmi te 
pītavarṇaṃ bṛhatkukṣiṃ mahākāyaṃ caturbhujam  Vis 
śūlakhaṅgadharaṃ raudraṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam 
etadajñānarūpaṃ syādavairāgyaṃ vadāmi te  Vis 
dūrvāśyāmanibhaṃ brahman dvipādaṃ ca caturbhujam 
paraśupāśadharaṃ raudraṃ raktāmbaradharaṃ sadā  Vis 
akṣitrayasamopetaṃ jaṭāmakuṭadhāriṇam dhārakam 
avairāgyasya rūpaṃ syāt anaiśvaryaṃ vadāmi te  Vis 
dhūmrākāraṃ bṛhatkukṣiṃ caturbāhuṃ mahāhanum 
ekavaktraṃ mahākāyaṃ muktakeśasamanvitam  Vis 
aśrīkaramasaumyaṃ ca akṣitrayasamanvitam 
anaiśvaryasya rūpaṃ tu nirdiṣṭamadhunā mune  Vis 
dharmādipañcapādāni adharmādīni nārada 
teṣāṃ rūpaṃ smarennityaṃ nyasettasmin yathākramam  Vis 
anyathā kalpayenmohāt ādhārādinirūpakam 
tatpūjā niṣphalā yāti grāmasyāgnibhayaṃ bhavet  Vis 
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena smaredrūpāṇi sādhakaḥ 
nyasedaṣṭadalaṃ padmaṃ teṣāmupari nārada  Vis 
tatrārkasomavahnīṃśca uparyupari vanyiset 
vṛttākāraṃ tu raktābhamarkamaṇḍalakaṃ nyaset  Vis 
tatropari nyaseddhyātvā śvetaṃ vṛttaṃ śaśāṅkakam 
agnimagninibhaṃ dhyātvā trikoṇaṃ maṇḍalopari  Vis 
evaṃ rūpaṃ tu saṃcintya maṇḍalārkādi nārada 
maṇḍalopari vinyasya tāmasādi guṇatrayam  Vis 
tāmasaṃ rājasaṃ caiva sātvikaṃ ca yathākramam 
tāmasaṃ kṛṣṇarūpaṃ tu rājasaṃ raktarūpakam  Vis 
sātvikaṃ śvotavarṇaṃ tu varṇānyetāni saṃsmaret 
tatra tadvarṇakaṃ cintya maṇḍalopari vinyaset  Vis 
tāmasādini vinyasya nyasedātmadvayaṃ budhaḥ 
ātmānaṃ cāntarātmānaṃ vāsudevaparāyaṇau  Vis 
ātmā tu śvetavarṇaḥ syādantarātmā tathaiva ca 
ś teṣāṃ varṇaṃ tu saṃcintya nyasedātmāntarātmake  Vis 
ādhārādyantarātmāntaṃ nyāsakramamatho śṛṇu 
ādhāraṃ prathamaṃ nyasya śvetavarṇaṃ trimūrtiyuk  Vis 
śaktinyāsaṃ dvitīye tu kandanyāsamataḥ param 
nālamākāśarūpaṃ syāttamovarṇaṃ caturthakam  Vis 
nālasyāgneyakoṇe tu dharmamūrtiṃ tu pañcamam 
ṣaṣṭhaṃ tu nairṛte nyasya jñānamūrtiṃ tu nārada  Vis 
saptame tu nyasedvidvān vairāgyaṃ vāyugocare 
aiśvaryamaṣṭamaṃ nyasya īśāne tantravittamaḥ  Vis 
navamaṃ nālamūle tu rudramūrtiṃ sadāśivam 
daśamaṃ nālasyāgre tu pūrve 'dharmaṃ tu vinyaset  Vis 
ekādaśe tu vinyasya dakṣiṇe 'jñānarūpakam 
paścime tu nyaset paścādavairāgyaṃ tu nārada  Vis 
udīcyāṃ vinyaseddevamanaiśvaryaṃ trayodaśa 
nālasyāgre smaredvidvān padmaṃ tatparamālayam  Vis 
etat padmāsanaṃ proktaṃ tridaśaiḥ pūjitaṃ sadā 
tatropari nyaset paścāt maṇḍalārkādi nārada  Vis 
guṇatrayaṃ nyasenmadhye tāmasādi yathākramam 
guṇamadhye nyaseddhīmānātmānaṃ cāntarātmakam  Vis 
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ prokta āsanasya kramo mayā 
āsanasyārcanaṃ vakṣye saṃkṣepādvidhipūrvakam  Vis 
ādhārādyantarātmāntaṃ mūrtīnāṃ munisattama 
vyastaiḥsaṃpūjayet sarvaṃ samastairvā samāhitaḥ  Vis 
arcayedgandhapuṣpādyaiḥ pūjayettaṃ manoramaiḥ 
teṣāṃ svanāmakairmantrairdadyāt sarvaṃ yathākramam  Vis 
etat kalpyaṃ muniśreṣṭha āhvānaṃ ca vadāmyaham 
svarṇādyanyatamaṃ pātraṃ kuḍubadvayapūritam  Vis 
itthaṃ hi lakṣaṇaṃ proktaṃ sarvapātrāṇi nārada 
āvāhanādi pātraṃ tat pañcaṣaṭsapta eva vā  Vis 
pūjakasyāgrataḥ sthāpya prokṣayenmūlavidyayā 
eteṣāmapyalābhe tu śaṅkhaśuktimathāpi vā  Vis 
kṣālayet sarvapātrāṇi viṣṇugāyatriyā mune 
āḍhakadvayasaṃpūrṇāṃ pakvabimbaphalākṛtim  Vis 
vardhanīṃ vāmapārśve tu vinyasyāpūrayedbudhaḥ 
gālitairudakairyasyāṃ gandhapuṣpayutāṃ nyaset  Vis 
śeṣaṃ dakṣiṇapārśve tu parito vāgrato 'pi vā 
sthāpayettu krameṇaiva pūjādravyaṃ samastakam  Vis 
tat pātreṣvekapātraṃ tu saṃgṛhya munisattama 
ṣaḍakṣareṇa mantreṇa saṃprokṣya tu punaḥ punaḥ  Vis 
tatpātraṃ tu punaḥ prokṣya gandhodena prapūrayet 
tasmin śirasi 
puṣpaṃ ca nyasettoyaṃ sapuṣpakam  Vis 
uddhṛtya pūjāmantreṇa dhyātvātra mahāmune 
yadrūpaṃ cintitaṃ samyak tadrūpaṃ cintya
sādhakaḥ  Vis 
avatīrṇaṃ mahāberādāgacchāntena mūrdhni ca 
prokṣya caivāsanaṃ dadyāt kevalena jagadguroḥ  Vis 
prakṣipya vādamūle tu puṣpamuṣṭiṃ tataḥ param 
namaskṛtyāñjaliṃ paścāt darśayenmunisattama  Vis 
ardhyaṃ pādyaṃ tathācāmaṃ datvā devāya mantravit 
tatastu parivārāṇi pātraśeṣeṇa kalpayet  Vis 
parivārakramaṃ vakṣye yathātattvena yathātathyena nārada 
āvāhanāṃśatoyena kalpeyattu yathākramam  Vis 
pūrve tu vāsudevaṃ tu śuddhasphaṭikasaṃnibham 
śaṅkhacakragadāpāṇiṃ pītāmbaravibhūṣitam  Vis 
saṃkarṣaṇaṃ nyasedyāmye śaśibālārkasaṃnibham 
śaṅkhacakrasamopetaṃ caturbāhuvirājitam  Vis 
pradyumnaṃ paścime nyasya śātakumbhanibhaṃ mune 
śaṅkhacakragadāpāṇiṃ pītāmbaravibhūṣitam  Vis 
aniruddhaṃ nyasettasminnuttare nīlarūpiṇam 
śaṅkhacakrasamāyuktaṃ pītavastraṃ caturbhujam  Vis 
śriyaṃ suvarṇavarṇābhāṃ śvetarūpāṃ sarasvatīm 
raktavarṇāṃ ratiṃ paścāt śāntiṃ kuṅkumasaṃnibhām  Vis 
āgneyādiṣu koṇeṣu vinyasecchaktirūpakam 
paiśāce tu nyaset paścāt śaṅkhādīnāṃ tu nārada  Vis 
pūrve śaṅkha niyuñjīta śvetavarṇaṃ sacanādayuk 
kālāgnisadṛśākāraṃ dakṣiṇe cakramuttamam  Vis 
paścime tu gadāṃ nyasya haridrābhāmanuttamām 
raktavarṇanibhaṃ padmamuttare tu nyasedbudhaḥ  Vis 
musalaṃ kṛṣṇavarṇaṃ tu āgneyyāṃ diśi vinyaset 
nairṛtāyāṃ nyasettatra khaṅgamākāśasaṃnibham  Vis 
pañcavarṇa tathā śārṅgaṃ vāyavye tantravittamaḥ 
sarvavarṇamayākārāṃ vanamālāṃ tathaiśake  Vis 
etaddbrijīyāvaraṇaṃ garbhāgāre prakīrtitam 
dvārasya dakṣiṇe caṇḍaṃ kṛṣṇavarṇaṃ caturbhujam  Vis 
śaṅkhacakragadāpāṇiṃ triṇetraṃ raktalocanam 
evaṃ rūpaṃ tu saṃcintya pracaṇḍaṃ tu tataḥ śṛṇu  Vis 
śaṅkhacakragadāpāṇiṃ raktavarṇaṃ caturbhujam 
dvārasyottarapārśve tu triṇetraṃ bhīmarūpiṇam  Vis 
purato vainateyaṃ ca suvarṇābhaṃ kṛtāñjalim 
karaṇḍamakuṭaṃ nīlavāsasaṃ priyadarśanam  Vis 
nīlāgranāsikāyuktaṃ nāgābharaṇabhūṣitam 
evaṃ tu garuḍaṃ cintya balarāmasya mūrtivat  Vis 
yo bhaktyā devamabhyarcet tathaiva garuḍaṃ yajet 
bhagavatpramukhaṃ paścādgarutmantaṃ niyojayet  Vis 
raktavarṇaṃ caturbāhuṃ dvibāhuṃ vā munīśvara 
sarvābharaṇasaṃyuktaṃ sarvaśobhanaśobhitam  Vis 
kālāgnisadṛśākāraṃ cakradhṛṅmakuṭānvitam 
evaṃ cakrādhidaivaṃ tu pūjayeddvārapārśvake  Vis 
śaṅkhābhaṃ saumyarūpaṃ tu sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam 
upavītayutaṃ śvetaṃ śaṅkhadhṛṅmakuṭānvitam  Vis 
caturbāhuṃ dvibāhuṃ vā dhyāyeddvārasya vāmake 
dhātāraṃ pītavarṇaṃ vidhātāramaruṇaprabham  Vis 
śyāmavarṇā tu bhūmiḥ syāt raktavarṇāṃ haripriyām 
durgāṃ ca komalaśyāmāṃ śvetarūpaṃ vināyakam  Vis 
śaṅkhapadmanidhī caiva śvetaraktanibhau mune 
gaṅgāṃ ca yamunāṃ caiva śvetakṛṣṇanibhe mune  Vis 
utkarṣaṇīṃ tu raktāṃ vai karṣaṇīṃ raktavarṇakām 
evaṃ dvāre tu saṃcintya trisandhyāyāṃsu
prapūjayet  Vis 
nārcayedupasandhyāyāṃ caṇḍādīn dvārapālakān 
ajñānādarcayenmohāt sthānanāśo bhaviṣyati  Vis

vimānāgneyayāmye tu tanmadhye gaṇanāyakam 
pūrvavadvarṇakaṃ cintya hastivaktraṃ caturbhujam  Vis 
vimāne dakṣiṇe kuryāt dakṣiṇāmūrtimīśvaram 
akṣamālādharaṃ devamaṣṭākṣaraparāyaṇam  Vis 
triṇetraṃ śvetasaṃkāśaṃ saumyaṃ somārdhadhāriṇam 
nāradādyṛṣisaṃghaiśca sevitaṃ dakṣiṇāmukham  Vis 
evaṃ rahasyarūpaṃ te saṃkṣepeṇa vidhīyate

kalpayenmuniśārdūla sarvasaṃpatsukhāvaham 
ālayasyottare mātṝḥ kalpayedbā munīśvara  Vis 
teṣāṃ nāma kramādguhyaṃ śṛṇuṣvāvahito 'dhunā

vidyākāntiśca saptaitāḥ kathitā viṣṇumātaraḥ

hayaśīrṣaḥsuvarṇābho varṇā etāḥ te
prakīrtitāḥ  Vis 
tathaiva vīrabhadrādi varṇaṃ tu paripaṭhyate

itthaṃ hi lakṣaṇopetaṃ sarvadevairnamaskṛtam 
saumyāsyeśānayormadhye durgāṃ śyāmanibhāṃ yajet  Vis 
tasyottare tu vinyasya mama rūpaṃ camūpateḥ 
śyāmalaṃ piṅgalākṣaṃ tu piṅgaśmaśruḥ sanātanam  Vis

pītāmbaradharaṃ saumyaṃ vivṛttākṣisamanvitam  Vis 
tarjayan vāmatarjanyā nāsāgrāsannayā jagat 
evaṃ hi mama rūpaṃ te tu
paṭhyate munisattama  Vis 
parivāravidhānoktamatha bāhyeṣu vinyaset

dakṣiṇe śaṅkhavarṇaṃ tu śaṅkhacakragadādharam

vāmapārśve nyaseccakramagnirūpaṃ caturbhujam 
triṇetraṃ bhīmasaṃkāśaṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharam  Vis 
tanmūrdhni vinyaseccakraṃ nīlāmbarakirīṭinam 
evaṃ tu lakṣaṇaṃ proktaṃ śaṅcakrādirūpakam   Vis 
indrādīśānaparyantaṃ sveṣu sthāneṣu yojayet

saundaryamindradaivatyaṃ dhyāyedindraṃ kirīṭinam

kirīṭahārakeyūramakuṭādivibhūṣitam 
sarvapretādhināthasya lakṣaṇaṃ kathitaṃ mayā  Vis 
tatastu rakṣasāmīśaṃ nirṛtiṃ raktamūrdhajam 
khaṅgabāhuṃ mahākāyaṃ raktavaktraṃ triṇetrakam  Vis 
etattu lakṣaṇaṃ proktaṃ rākṣasādhipatestataḥ 
sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyuktaṃ sarvālaṃkārabhūṣitam  Vis 
śyāmalaṃ pāśahastaṃ ca jaleśaṃ paṅkajāsanam 
dhūmravarṇanibhākāraṃ dhvajayuktaṃ mahābhujam  Vis 
dvipādaṃ ca dvihastaṃ ca sarveṣāṃ prāṇasaṃjñitam 
itthaṃ te muniśārdūla lakṣaṇaṃ paripaṭhyate  Vis 
dhyāyet saumye tu matimān yakṣeśvaramanuttamam 
taptahāṭakasaṃkāśaṃ sarvalakṣaṇalakṣitam  Vis 
dvipādaṃ ca dvihastaṃ ca daṇḍapāṇiṃ dhaneśvaram 
śvetādriśikharākāraṃ dvipādaṃ ca caturbhujam  Vis 
vṛṣadhvajaṃ triṇetraṃ ca śūlapāṇīndumaulinam 
evaṃ dhyāyet kramāt sarvān svanāmnā pūjayet pṛthak  Vis 
etattṛtīyāvaraṇe dvārapārśvendusūryayoḥ 
raktavarṇaṃ mahākāyaṃ kambugrīvaṃ caturbhujam  Vis 
śaṅkhacakragadāpāṇiṃ triṇetraṃ bhīmarūpiṇam 
cintaceddakṣiṇe pārśve tṛtīyadvārake ravim  Vis 
kundapuṣpanibhākāraṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharam 
caturbhujaṃ triṇetraṃ ca pītavastraṃ ca cintayet  Vis 
dvārasya vāmapārśve tu śaśāṅkākṛtimuttamam 
maulipṛṣṭhasya sūryādau cintayenmaṇḍalākṛtim  Vis 
evaṃ śaśiṃ raviṃ dhyātvā tṛtīyadvārapārśvayoḥ 
kumudādīni sarvāṇi nyaset pūrvādiṣu kramāt  Vis 
kumudaḥ kumudākṣaśca puṇḍarīko 'tha vāmanaḥ 
śaṅkukarṇaḥsarpanetraḥ sumukhaḥ supratiṣṭhitaḥ  Vis 
eteṣāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ proktaṃ dhyāyedasmin mahotsave 
tadvat jñātvātra bhūteśān pūjayet sādhakottamaḥ  Vis 
purataḥ sthāpayet sarvān viṣṇupāriṣadān bahūn 
sarvavarṇadharāḥsarve sarve śastrāstrapāṇayaḥ  Vis 
mahāpīṭhe tu saṃsmṛtya sarvān bhūtagaṇānvitān 
pūjākāle tato dhyāyet svarūpaṃ pūjakaḥ kramāt  Vis 
svanāmnā parivārāṇāṃ praṇavādinamontakam 
arghyapādyādibhirvāpi gandhādyairvā munīśvara  Vis 
arcayennityapūjāyāṃ praṇavādimanusmaran 
asmin tantre mayā proktaṃ caṇḍādyāvaraṇārcanam  Vis 
utsave parivārāṇāmarcanāvidhiruttamaḥ 
tathaivābhyarcya matimān parivārānatandritaḥ  Vis 
evamabhyarcya bhūteśān paścāt pūjāṃ samācaret 
kṣālayet sarvapātrāṇi pūrvoktena vidhānataḥ  Vis 
sarvadravyāṇi saṃprokṣya nirīkṣyādyena mantrataḥ 
āvāhanādibhiḥ sarvairupacārakrameṇa tu  Vis 
devadevaṃ samabhyarcya sa yāti paramāṃ gatim 
upacārakramaṃ vakṣye yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ  Vis 
pūrvamāvāhanaṃ kuryāt punarāsanameva ca 
tṛtīyaṃ puṣpavikṣepaṃ turīyaṃ tu namaskṛtim  Vis 
pañcamo 'ñjalimudrā ca syāt
ṣaṣṭhamardhyaṃ tathaiva ca 
pādyaṃ tu saptamaṃ kuryāt tathācamanamaṣṭamam  Vis 
snapanaṃ navamaṃ vidyāddaśamo vasanaṃ bhavet 
ekādaśo bhūṣaṇaṃ syāt dvādaśastūpavītakam  Vis 
trayodaśaścācamanaṃ gandhaścaiva caturdaśaḥ 
puṣpaṃ pañcadaśaścaiva ṣoḍaśo dhūpa eva ca  Vis 
dīpaḥ saptadaśaścaiva mudrāṣṭādaśa ucyate 
havirekonaviṃśaśca pānīyaṃ viṃśakastathā  Vis 
ekaviṃśastathācāmaḥ tāmbūlaṃ ca dvāviṃśakaḥ 
upacārastrayoviṃśa ācāmastadanantaram  Vis 
mukhavāsaḥ pañcaviṃśaḥ ṣaḍviṃśo geyamucyate 
purāṇaṃ saptaviṃśaśca nṛttahomamataḥ param  Vis 
balibhramaṇamekonatriṃśa ardhyamataḥ param 
puṣpaṃ vā muniśārdūla dadyādicchānurūpataḥ  Vis 
ekatriṃśo mukhavāsaścodvāsanamataḥ param 
dvātriṃśadupacārāṇāmuktamevaṃ mahāmune  Vis 
vakṣye kalopacārāṇi rāṃstu
śṛṇuṣvāvahito bhava 
ādya āvāhanaṃ paścāt āsanaṃ tadanantaram  Vis 
pādyaṃ tṛtīya ardhyaṃ syādācāmaṃ pañcamaḥ smṛtaḥ 
ṣaṣṭhaṃ tu snapanaṃ vidyāt saptamo vasanaṃ bhavet  Vis 
aṣṭamastūpavītaṃ syānnavamaṃ gandha ucyate 
daśamaḥ puṣpavinyāsaḥ dhūpa ekādaśo bhavet  Vis 
dīpastataḥ paraṃ vidyāt caruṇastu caroścaiva nivedanam 
caturdaśyañjalimudrā pradakṣiṇamataḥ param  Vis 
udvāsanaṃ ṣoḍaśaḥ syādityevamaparaḥkramaḥ 
evaṃ ṣoḍaśadhā proktā upacārāṇirāṃstunārada  Vis 
ekādaśopacārāṇāṃ kramaṃ śṛṇu mahāmune 
āvāhanaṃ tu prathamaḥ dvitīyaścāsanaṃ bhavet  Vis 
arghya cānantaraṃ vidyāt pādyaṃ caiva tataḥ param 
devasyācamanaṃ vidyāt pañcamaṃ tu vicakṣaṇaḥ  Vis 
gandhaṃ cānantaraṃ vidyāt saptamaṃ puṣpameva ca 
dhūpaṃ tu cāṣṭamaṃ vidyāt dīpastu navamaḥ smṛtaḥ  Vis 
daśamastu nivedyaṃ syādudvāsanamataḥ param 
mukhyagauṇakrameṇaiva viniyogaṃ tataḥ śṛṇu  Vis 
yatra pūjottamā tatra kuryānmukhyopacārakam 
madhyamārādhanaṃ yattu trakṛdhyamaprayojayet  Vis 
arcā kanīyasī yatra tatraivaikādaśena tu 
prayojyamiti śāstrasya niścayaḥ sādhakottamaiḥ  Vis 
sarve sarvatra vā pūjā deśakālānurūpataḥ 
sādhakecchānurūpeṇa kuryādvā munipuṅgava  Vis 
aniārirādhayiṣurmūtrā yadyadvai sādhakottamaḥ 
tattadvai mūrtimantreṇa kuryāt sarvopacārakam  Vis 
snapane mantrabhedo 'sti mūrtīnāṃ munisattama 
nitye naimittike vāpi viṣṇornukamathāvapi  Vis 
nārāyaṇopaniṣadaṃ dvādaśākṣarameva ca 
nārāyaṇaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ
vā ato devīve
ti vā punaḥ  Vis 
sahasraśīrṣaṃ devamaṣṭākṣaramathāpi vā 
sahasraśīrṣā puruṣo mantraṃ vā parameṣṭhinaḥ  Vis 
eteṣvanyatamaṃ vāpi snapanaṃ sādhakaḥ śuciḥ 
kurvan svarāṣṭramuddhṛtya viṣṇulokamavāpnuyāt  Vis 
kevalaṃ mūlamantreṇa pūjakaḥ puruṣottama 
āvāhanādibhiḥ sarvairupacāraiḥ samarcayet  Vis 
suguṇo vaṃśasaṃpanno nirdeṣo rogavarjitaḥ 
āvāhanādi karmāṇi sarvāṇyetāni sarvadā  Vis 
aṣṭākṣareṇa vā kuryāt mūrtīnāṃ munisattama 
pūjakasyottamatvācca nirdeṣatvānmahāmune  Vis 
kevalaṃ puṣpamātreṇa deveśastṛpyate 'tra tu 
sā pūjā saphalaṃ yāti vṛddhikṛt grāmarājyoḥ  Vis 
evaṃ yaḥ kārayedbhaktyā sa yāti paramāṃ gatim 
yatirvā brahmacārī vā pūjako munisattama  Vis 
dviguṇaṃ phalamāpnoti nātra kāryā vicāraṇā 
evaṃ saṃpūjayedbhaktyā viṣṇuṃ sakalamavyayam  Vis 
iha loke śriyaṃ prāpya paraloke tathaiva ca 
sarvān kāmānavāpnoti sarvayajñaphalaṃ bhavet  Vis 
viśeṣamatra vakṣyāmi ātmārthasya parasya ca 
upacārakramaṃ sarvaṃ sādhakānāṃ hitāya tu  Vis 
arghyādimukhavāsantaṃ kramāddevāya kalpayet 
arghyaṃ pādyaṃ tathācāmaḥ madhuparkaḥ punaśca tat  Vis 
tāmbūlaṃ gandhapuṣpaṃ ca akṣato dhūpa eva ca 
dīpo hyañjalimudrā tu nivedyaṃ tu mahāmune  Vis 
pānīyācamanīyaṃ ca mukhavāsastathaiva ca 
evaṃ kramo muniśreṣṭha tatkrameṇāthavārcayet  Vis 
kṣālayet sarvapātrāṇi pūrvavattantravittamaḥ 
tattat pātreṣu taddravyaṃ nikṣipyāpūrya puṣpakam  Vis 
arghyatoyaṃ svamantreṇa mukhamālepayaddhareḥ 
pādyaṃ devasya pāde ca dīyatedadyādvai
svasvavidyayā  Vis 
devasya dakṣiṇe haste hyācāmaṃ madhuparkakam 
punarācāmatāmbūlaṃ tathaiva ca punaḥ punaḥ  Vis 
jātiśrīkaṇṭhakhaṇḍa
mādāya peṣayet piṣṭhapaṅkavat 
karpūreṇa samāyuktaṃ kuḍubadvayapūritam  Vis 
kevalaṃ candanaṃ vāpi gandhaṃ ṣaṇmuṣṭimātrakam 
puṣpaprasthacatuṣkaistu mūrtīnāṃ tu pṛthakpṛthak  Vis 
dāpayettu prayatnena sādhakaḥ paramārthavit 
dhūpaṃ surabhiṇā vyāptaṃ prāptajvālocchritojjñitam  Vis 
bahurekhamanāragnyaṃ daśamātraṃ pradāpeyat  
dīpaṃ saptāṅgulotthānaṃ ghṛtakarpūradīpitam  Vis 
dhūpaṃ tu dāpayedgandhaṃ nāsikāyāṃ tu dakṣiṇe 
dadyādyathākramaṃ sarvaṃ vāsudevāya bhaktitaḥ  Vis 
kalamādīni 
sarvāṇi śeṣāṅgaṃ mardayedbudhaḥ 
vāmahastena mantrajñaḥ puṣpaṃ gṛhya samāhitaḥ  Vis 
dakṣiṇena kareṇaiva dadyāddevasya pādayoḥ 
muṣṭimātraṃ pradadyāttu trivāreṇa raṃ ca
svavidyayā  Vis 
madhyamānāmikāmadhye cāṅguṣṭhena samanvitam 
akṣataṃ tu tato dadyāt tathaiva ca punaḥ punaḥ  Vis 
devasya vāmanāsau canāsāyāṃ
dhūpaṃ dadyāt samāhitaḥ 
dakṣiṇe devadṛkpārśve dīpaṃ dadyāttu mantravit  Vis 
trimātrakaṃ tu mudrāyā darśanaṃ dakṣiṇādṛśi 
kapilājyena saṃsrāvya hyannasuktena saṃspṛśet  Vis 
pariṣicyādi mantreṇa pāṇiṃ dadyāttu pāṇinā  
dadyāttaddakṣiṇe haste haviḥprāśanamudrayā  Vis 
pānīyācamanīyaṃ ca mukhavāsaṃ tathaiva ca 
evaṃ ṣoḍaśadhā proktaṃ viśeṣeṇopacārakam  Vis 
dadyādyathākramaṃ sarvaṃ bhaktipūtena cetasā 
tatastu sādhakaḥ samyak praṇamyāñjalimudrayā  Vis 
devasya pādau hastābhyāṃ saṃspṛśettat samāhitaḥ 
tatastvatharvavede tu śaunakāyāṃ tu śākhayā  Vis 
nārāyaṇopaniṣadaṃ uccārya ca punaḥ punaḥ 
tribhiḥ kāṇḍaiḥsamuccārya mantreṇaiva mahāmune  Vis 
deveśastṛpyate caiva nātra kāryā vicāraṇā 
rājarāṣṭravivṛddhiḥ syāt grāmādiṣu tathaiva ca  Vis 
arcayennānyathā mohādābhicārakaro bhavet 
sā pūjā niṣphalā caiva rogavṛddhirbhaviṣyati  Vis 
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena tribhiḥ kāṇḍaiḥ samarcayet 
agnikāryaṃ tu pūrvoktaṃ kuryāttantravicakṣaṇaḥ  Vis 
samidho mūlamantreṇa ājyamājyena mantrataḥ 
caruṃ puruṣasūktena pratyekaṃ ṣoḍaśāhutīḥ  Vis 
hutvā hutvāgnimadhye tu sādhako mantravittamaḥ 
śeṣadravyāṇi sarvāṇi pūrvoktenaiva kārayet  Vis 
agnikāryaṃ samāpyaivaṃ balidānamathocyate 
balidānakramaḥ sarvaḥ saṃkṣepādvakṣyate 'dhunā  Vis 
nitye naimittike caiva sarvasaṃpat sukhāvaham

tālaṃ tu karṇikā proktaṃ tatpādārdhatalaṃ tathā 
pādaṃ tu tadbahiḥ kuryāt tadante valayaṃ bhavet  Vis 
balipātraṃ samākhyātaṃ tāmrarājatahaimakam 
uttamādhamamadhyaṃ syāt vibhavasyānurūpataḥ  Vis 
kārayedbalipātraṃ tu ekadravyeṇa śilpinā 
ācāryo 'laṃkṛtaḥ samyak pātramādāya maṇḍale  Vis 
sādhitaṃ prokṣitaṃ paścāt gālitenodakena tu 
tasminmadhye tu kurvīta sudṛḍhaṃ haviṣāsanam  Vis

kārayecchibikādyeṣu balibhramaṇamuttamam 
kalpayet saparīvāramantarāvaraṇasthitam  Vis

suvarṇakusumaiścitraiḥ prabhāvāsitasaṃyutam   Vis 
vāsikādyābhirmālābhiḥ 
bhūṣitaṃ sumanoramam 
sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ vāpi tāmraṃ vātīva sundaram  Vis

alābhe kāñcane vāpi rājataṃ tāmrameva vā  Vis

prakalpayet  Vis 
śanaiḥ śanairmuniśreṣṭha śaṅkhādyairgeyasaṃyutam

yo mohādbimbahīne tu balikarmaṇi cenmune  
tatsthānaṃ nidhanaṃ yāti tatrasthā narakaṃ vrajet  Vis

paścāddevaṃ mahābhāgo nītvārghyādyaiḥsamarcayet

evaṃ balividhiḥ prokto ekāvaraṇapūjane  Vis 
punaḥ prākāramatraiva kalpitaścenmunīśvara

indrādi supratiṣṭhāntaṃ punaḥsaṃsthāpya mantravit  Vis

taṃ baliṃ madhyamamidaṃ pūrvā pūrvā garīyasī   Vis

matsyaḥ kūrmaśca tārkṣyaśca ananto bhujagottamaḥ  Vis 
ityete ṣoḍaśa proktāḥ ghaṭikānāṃ tu devatāḥ 
viṣṇvādyā dvādaśa ye ca haṃso 'tha bala eva ca  Vis 
kapilaśca halaścaiva śarāvāṇāṃ tu devatāḥ

ṣaḍviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
viṣvaksenaḥ

yenopasargā

dhvajotthāpanamācaret

hastamātraṃ parityajya balipīṭhasya cāntare  Vis 
kalpayeddhvajapīṭhaṃ tu mānaṃ tasya pracakṣate

caturhastaṃ tadardhaṃ vā vistārāyāmataḥ samam

ekahastaṃ tathā bhūmau gartaṃ pīṭhādadhaḥ śubham 
stambhasya paritaḥ kuryāt mekhalātritayaṃ budhaḥ  Vis

mekhalocchrāyamāyāmamekaikaṃ caturaṅgulam

iti padmadalaṃ vidhiḥ

tathā vā phalakaṃ kāṃ

paṭasya lakṣaṇaṃ tasmin viśeṣaṃ kathaya mi te  Vis 
śṛṇuṣvāvahito bhūtvā sarvasaṃpatsukhāvaham

āyāmamiti saṃproktaṃ vistāramadhunocyate

navahastācca nūnyū
naṃ vai mahāgehe tu neṣyate

ālikhedgaruḍaṃ tatra suvarṇābhaṃ suvarcasam

karaṇḍamakuṭaṃ nīlavāsasaṃ priyadarśanam

mahākṣabja

atho 'mṛtasya kalaśaṃ padmaṃ caivātra saṃlikhet 
tābhyāmubhayataḥ kuryāt dīpau dvau śubhadarśanau  Vis 
citrābhāsapratiṣṭhāṃ tu kārayenmantravittamaḥ 
chāyādhivāsanaṃ kuryāt jalaṃ saṃhṛtya deśikaḥ  Vis 
śāyayitvā tato vedyāṃ saṃhṛtyotpādya tattvataḥ 
dhānyarāśiṃ vinikṣipya vedimadhye samantataḥ  Vis 
vedikākalaśeṣvaṣṭāvanantādīn prapūjayet

nyasya pūrvādikramayogataḥ

pratyaggrīvaṃ tato vastraiḥ saṃcchādya patageśvaram

 paritastathā

yāvadrātratrya

rātrāntakaṃārātryantaṃ

nālikeraphalaṃ caiva pañcadravyasamanvitam 
balyannametaiḥ saṃyojya balidānaṃ tu cotsave  Vis 
krameṇa kārayet paścāt pūrvavaddhomapūrvakam 
dhvajotthānaṃ divā kuryādrātrāvāhanameva ca  Vis 
sa taddhvaje devatāhvānaṃ madhyāhne tu viśeṣataḥ 
ārohaṇaṃ divā kuryāt ketorniśyaṅkurārpaṇam  Vis 
haviṣā balidānaṃ tu kṛtvā dvārāgrapīṭhayoḥ 
madhye hastasamāṃ vediṃ madhye devān samarcayet  Vis 
āramya balidānaṃ tu kuryādgrāmādivāstuṣu

pādagātrakabhedena vimṛjet paritaḥ krama t  Vis

tṛtīyaṃ dalasandhīnāṃ dalāgrāṇāṃ caturthakam

kesarāgreṣu saṃsthāpya dalāntaṃ bhrāmayettataḥ

tāmasaṃ kokūr

śālibhirvātha sarveṣāṃ snāpayenmūlavidyayā 
ghṛtādisnehadravyāṇāmāḍhakaṃ vārdhameva vā  Vis 
sarveṣāmapyalābhe tu pūrayedgandhavāriṇā 
tenaiva snāpayeddevaṃ yathāvittānusārataḥ  Vis 
yatproktaṃ cotsave puṣpaṃ tasyā 
evaṃ tu mantravit 
tattaddoṣaṃ smaret kṣipya tulasī cotpalākṣatam  Vis 
evaṃ dravyaṃ tu saṃproktaṃ daivataṃ kathayāmi te 
dāmodarāvasānāśca keśavādyāśca mūrtayaḥ  Vis 
ghṛtādikalaśānāṃ tu devatāḥ parikīrtitāḥ 
rakṣārthaṃ kalaśānāṃ tu kumudādīni daivatam  Vis 
uddhāraṇakramaṃ yena tatproktaṃ daivataṃ kramāt 
evaṃ saṃsthāpya vidhivat paścācchuddhiṃ samācaret  Vis 
puṇyāhaṃ vācayitvā tu prokṣayet kuśavāriṇā 
evaṃ saṃprokṣya vidhivat tataḥ snapanamācaret  Vis 
ghṛtena dadhnā payasā madhunoṣṇākadakena ca 
snāpayet pañcacūrṇaiśca saṃprapūjya prabhuṃ mune  Vis 
aṣṭākṣareṇa gandhāmbhaḥ puṣpāmbho dvādaśākṣaraiḥ 
maṅgalaṃ viṣṇugāyatryā śuddhāmbhaḥ praṇavena tu  Vis 
tīrthacūrṇaṃ tataḥ snāpya mūlamantreṇa sādhakaḥ 
snapanānte tu saṃsthāpya rajanīcūrṇamuttamam  Vis 
ājyādiniśi
cūrṇāntaṃ evaṃ saṃsnāpayet kramāt 
gandhapuṣpādinābhyarcya dīpāntaṃ ca mahāmune  Vis 
snapanānte tu mantrajñaḥ kumudādīṃśca rakṣakān 
devasya śirasi bhrāmya bhaktānāṃ tu pradāpayet  Vis 
evaṃ tu snapanaṃ kṛtvā nadīsnānaṃ tu kārayet 
tīre devaṃ samānīya kuśakūrcena mārjayet  Vis 
pādyādidīpaparyantaṃ arcayet kautukaṃ tataḥ 
avagāhya ca tattīrthaṃ tīrthānāvāhya sarvataḥ  Vis 
kṛtvāghamarṣaṇaṃ tatra pañcamantraiḥ samāhitaḥ 
jalakeliṃ tataḥ kṛtvā tīramāsādya deśikaḥ  Vis 
tatra tīrthajale snātaḥ sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate 
alaṃkṛtya tu vastrādyairgandhapuṣpādinārcayet  Vis 
havirmahāhavirvāpi datvā nṛttādi kārayet 
devasya pūrvadigdeśe baliṃ dadyāt samāhitaḥ  Vis 
namo 'stu sarvadevebhya evamuccārya mantrataḥ 
pālikādyairalaṃkṛtya yānamāropayeddharim  Vis 
punaḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ kuryāt grāmaṃ vā nagaraṃ tu vā 
ālayaṃ vāpyabhāve tu yathāvittānusārataḥ  Vis 
svastivācanasaṃyuktaṃ śaṅkhabherīravākulam 
pradīpaśatasaṃyuktaṃ nṛttagītādisaṃyutam  Vis 
puṣpavṛṣṭisamāyuktamakṣatā
lājasaṃyutam 
sāmagītasamāyuktaṃ jayaśabdasamanvitam  Vis 
pradakṣiṇaṃ parikramya nadrutaṃ navilambitam 
yāgabhūmiṃ samāsādya pūjayitvā yathākramam  Vis 
snapanaṃ vidhivat kṛtvā puṣpayāgaṃ samārabhet 
kṛtvā padmaṃ cakrakaṃ maṇḍalaṃ vā tatra sthāne vāsudevādikāṃ kā śca  Vis 
śaṅkhādyā vai bāhyato lokapālāḥ viṣvakseno vainateyaśca bāhye 
bhūteśā vai bāhyataḥ pūjanīyāḥ gaulyannaṃ vai bhakṣyamagneśca kāryam  Vis 
puṇyāhārghyaṃ puṣpamekaṃ baliṃ ca pūjāpujye mūlabimbe sthitaṃ vai 
cakralakṣaṇamārge tu śeṣamasminniyojayet  Vis 
dhvajāvarohaṇaṃ kuryāt udvāsyaiva tu devatāḥ 
datvā mahābaliṃ tābhyo mudgānnāpūpalājakaiḥ  Vis 
saktubhirgrāmabāhye ca madhye caiva kṣamāpya ca 
dhvajādvisarjayeddevaṃ vainateyaṃ svamantrataḥ  Vis 
ekarātridvirātre vā trirātre tu mahāmune 
dhvajāvarohaṇaṃ kuryāt adhikaṃ tu na kārayet  Vis 
adhikaṃ yadi cettatra snapanaṃ kārayet kramāt 
utsavapratimāyāṃ tu snapanaṃ tvadhamottamam  Vis 
pañcaviṃśatibhirvāpi kalaśairdvādaśaistu vā 
yathāvittānusāreṇa 
 snapanaṃ kārayeddharim  Vis 
dhvajāvarohaṇaṃ paścāt kārayenmantravittamaḥ 
karṣaṇādiṣu pūjāyāṃ pratiṣṭhārohaṇādiṣu  Vis 
dhvājārohaṇavelāyāṃ dhvajasyāpyavarohaṇe 
utsave balidāne tu śaṅkhādyaiścaiva ghoṣayet  Vis 
śaṅkhatūryādinirghoṣaṃ haritṛptikaraṃ mune 
rakṣovidrāvaṇaṃ caiva rājaśāntikaraṃ tathā  Vis 
rāṣṭravṛddhikaraṃ samyak yajamānasukhāvaham 
snapanasthāpanādīnāṃ yā mudrā yasya kathyate  Vis 
tāṃ tathāśaknuvan kartuṃ mūlamantraṃ nyaset kare 
tena kurvan kriyāḥ sarvāḥ kareṇa munipuṅgava  Vis 
tṛtīyaṃ samanudhyānaṃ te cānte 'ñjalikārakāḥ 
tṛptiṃ kurvanti devasya jalasthānajaleśvarān  Vis 
tṛpta tarpa
yedātmanastṛptimiti guhyopadeśakaḥ 
devotsavādikriyayā nṛpasya balāyurārogyajayaśriyaśca  Vis 
rāṣṭrasya vṛddhirdhanadhānyayugvai prayojayitrādi phalaṃ sukhādi 
utsavāṅgamatho vakṣye yāgamaṇḍapamuttamam  Vis 
dakṣiṇe gopurasyaiva āneyyāṃ diśi vai tathā 
yāmyāyāmuttare vātha kārayedyāgamaṇḍapam  Vis 
tatpūrvabhāge kartavyaṃ kuṇḍaṃ lakṣaṇasaṃyutam 
kuṇḍapārśve muniśreṣṭha vediṃ kuryādyathāvidhi  Vis 
caturhastapramāṇena kārayedvedimuttamām 
vistārāyāmatulyā syādyāgavedirmahāmune  Vis 
trihastaṃ vā dvihastaṃ vā kārayedvedimuttamām 
ratnimātrasamutsedhāmathavā tālamātrakām  Vis 
darpaṇodarasaṃkāśāṃ yāgavedimanuttamām 
evaṃ kṛtvā vidhānena vediṃ bhuktiśubhapradām  Vis 
tatropari likhet padmamaṣṭapatradalākṛti 
gomayena samālipya dvādaśākṣaravidyayā  Vis 
prokṣayettena mantreṇa kuśapūtena vāriṇā 
pālikā cāṅkuropetamaṣṭamaṅgalasaṃyutam  Vis 
pūrvādikramayogena śaṅkhādīn maṅgalānnyaset 
uttamādikramaṃ proktaṃ vedikālakṣaṇaṃ mune  Vis 
puṇyāhaṃ vācayitvā tu prokṣayitvā kuśāmbhasā 
svastisūktaṃ tatoccārya
brāhmaṇaiḥ saha mantravit  Vis 
tatra madhye muniśreṣṭha śālinā vedimācaret 
pañcabhārapramāṇaṃ vā tasyārdhaṃ vārdhameva vā  Vis 
vistīrya vedimadhye tu raktaśālyantameva vā 
pūrvavadvilikhedraktapadmamaṣṭadalairyutam  Vis 
tatra madhye tu saṃsthāpya navakumbhān yathākramam 
sūtratrayasamopetān gālitodakapūritān  Vis 
vastrayugmairalaṃkṛtya gandhapuṣpasamanvitān 
pañcaratnasamopetān kūrcatrayasamanvitān  Vis 
aśvatthapallavairyuktāṃścakrikābhiḥ pidhāya tu 
evaṃ lakṣaṇasaṃyuktakumbheṣvāvāhayet kramāt  Vis 
mahāberānnayecchaktiṃ madhyakumbhe mahāmune 
pūrvādi caṣṭakumbheṣu vāsudevādikān yajet  Vis 
arghyapādyādinābhyarcya havīṃṣi mukhavāsakam 
dāpeyat kumbhamadhyasthadevāya munisattama  Vis 
pūrvādi cāṣṭakumbheṣu taccheṣeṇa baliṃ kṣipet 
vāsudevādikān jñātvā svanāmnaiva pṛthak pṛthak  Vis 
tatastu kumudādīnāṃ kumbhasya paritor'cayet 
ghaṇṭāśabdasamopetaṃ kukkuṭāṇḍapramāṇataḥ  Vis 
svastivācanasaṃyuktaṃ dhūpadīpasamanvitam 
svanamnā balidānaṃ tu sādhayet sādhakottamaḥ  Vis 
nārikelaphalaṃ dadyāt sandhyayorevamarcayet 
tatpūjānte tu mantrajño homakarma samārabhet  Vis 
aṣṭottaraśataṃ vāpi tadardhaṃ vārdhameva vā 
samidāditilāntaṃ tu juhuyāt sādhakottamaḥ  Vis 
homānte balidānaṃ tu kārayedgrāmavāstuṣu 
tatastīrthasya divase pūrvāhṇe homapūjanam  Vis 
kārayet pūrvavat samyak sādhakaḥ paramārthavit 
homānte cānayet kumbhāttaccakṣurmūlaberake  Vis 
tatastu vāsudevādīn nayet pūrvavadāvṛte 
vatsare vatsare brahman kartavyaṃ paramaṃ śubham  Vis 
nityapūjāvihīnasya prāyaścittaṃ mahotsavam 
evaṃ saṃpūjayeddevaṃ cotsave yāgamaṇḍape  Vis 
tīrthasya divasaṃ yāvattāvat saṃpūjayet kramāt 
yāgamaṇḍapapūjāyāmaṅkurārpaṇapūjane  Vis 
baliśeṣaṃ homaśeṣaṃ pātraśeṣaṃ tathaiva ca 
asminniveditaṃ sarvamācāryāya pradāpayet  Vis 
anyathā niṣphalaṃ yāti yajamānasya rogakṛt 
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena kārayecchāstracoditam  Vis 
yaḥ kārayettu matimān tatphalaṃ samavāpnuyāt 
yāgamaṇḍapapūjāṃ tu vinā cedutsavaṃ kuru  Vis 
kevalaṃ homamātreṇa cāpyalaṃ tu mahotsavam 
dhanyaṃ yaśasyamāyuṣyaṃ sarvapāpanikṛntanam  Vis 
iti śrīpāñcārātre viṣvaksenasaṃhitāyāṃ utsavavidhirnāma saptaviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ 
aṣṭāviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
viṣvaksenaḥ
amāvāsyotsavaṃ vakṣye māsi māsi munīśvara 
devajanmarkṣake vāpi pratiṣṭhārkṣamathā ṛkṣakepivā  Vis 
yajamānasya janmarkṣe rājajanmarkṣake 'pi vā 
ayane viṣukāle vā niścayitvāṅkurān purā  Vis 
navāhe saptapañcāhe tryahaikāhamathāpi vā 
aṅkurārpaṇameteṣu sarvasampatsukhāvaham  Vis 
kārayedvidhivat samyak sāyāhne munisattama 
anaṅkurārpaṇaṃ kāryamanarthamaśubhāvaham  Vis 
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena kārayedaṅkurārpaṇam 
aṅkurārpaṇakārye 'smin velādīni na vīkṣayet  Vis 
pālikāghaṭikā caiva śarāvaśca tridhā mune 
uktamasmin mahātantre cotsave ṣoḍaśān kramāt  Vis 
pratyakaṃ pālikādīni lakṣaṇaiḥ saha nārada 
kaścidasmin viśeṣo 'sti taṃ viśeṣaṃ śṛṇu kramāt  Vis 
pratyekaṃ dvādaśaṃ vāpi kevalāḥ pālikāstathā 
pālikāṣoḍaśaṃ vāpi dvādaśaṃ navakaṃ tu vā  Vis 
dūrvābhiḥ saśirīṣābhiḥ pālikādīn suveṣṭayet 
tilādidaśabījāni mudgamekamathāpi vā  Vis 
payobhiḥ kṣālayet pañcamantrairvāribhireva vā 
evaṃ bījāni saṃkṣālya kārayedaṅkurārpaṇam  Vis 
aṅkurārpaṇakārye 'smin sūtrapātaṃ na kārayet 
viśeṣamatra vakṣyāmi padmasūtravidhiṃ śṛṇu  Vis 
trihastaparimāṇaṃ tu caiva gomayenānulepayet 
tasyordhve śālimāstīrya tanmadhye 'bjamathālikhet  Vis 
tryahaikāhotsave caiva snapane munisattama 
amāvāsyādikārye 'smin ṣoḍaśaṃ dvādaśaṃ tu vā  Vis 
karṇikādidalān likhya pratyekaṃ tatra vinyaset 
pratiṣṭhotsavayoścaiva pavitrārohaṇe mune  Vis 
tathā dīkṣāvidhāne tu pratyekaṃ ṣoḍaśa kramāt 
dvādaśaṃ vātha niḥśeṣaṃ pālikādīṃśca kārayet  Vis 
śeṣakarmāṇi sarvāṇi likhedabjamanuttamam 
padmasya dalasaṃkhyāstu śṛṇu cāsmin mahāmune  Vis 
pālikā ṣoḍaśaṃ cettu dalaṃ pañcadaśaṃ likhet 
dvādaśaṃ pālikā cettu tādṛśaṃ padmamālikhet  Vis 
karṇikadidaleṣveṣu kārayet prathamākṣaram 
athavā muniśārdūla aṣṭapatrābjamālikhet  Vis 
pūrvavadvilikhedbījaṃ pūrvādiṣvakṣarān vasūn 
prokṣayettena mantreṇa śākhāmūlena vā mune  Vis 
indrādīśāvasāneṣu pālikān navakān nyaset 
tena mantreṇa matimānan prokṣayedgandhavāriṇā  Vis 
puṇyāhaṃ vācayettasmin brāhmaṇaistantrapāragaiḥ 
tilādibījānabhyarcya taṇḍulopari nārada  Vis 
jitanta iti mantreṇa sarvabījāni vāpayet 
gandhapuṣpādinābhyarcya sugupte sthāpayet kramāt  Vis 
viśeṣaścātra saṃproktaḥ śeṣaṃ sādhāraṇaṃ bhavet 
sāyāhne vātha pūrvāhṇe balimasmin samācaret  Vis 
haviṣā cākṣatairvāpi puṣpairvātha baliṃ kṣipet 
amāvāsyotsavādyeṣu saṃproktaṃ cāṅkurārpaṇam  Vis 
utsavapratimāṃ vāpi snapanārcāmathāpi vā 
balibimbaṃ tu vā cakrabimbamekamathāpi vā  Vis 
tadgṛhītvā tu mantrajñaḥ śuddhasnānaṃ tu kārayet 
pūrvarātrau tu kartavyaḥ sūtrabandho yathāvidhi  Vis 
vāsādhivāsavat kṛtvā maṇḍapālaṃkṛtirmune 
caturaṅgulamutsedhaṃ caturhastapramāṇataḥ  Vis 
śālibhirvedikāṃ samyak kṛtvā maṇḍapamadhyame 
tadardhaṃ taṇḍulairvediṃ tanmadhye tu samācaret  Vis 
dhānyābhāve yathāvediryathālābhaṃ praśasyate 
yajamānecchayā vediṃ kuryāttantravicakṣaṇaḥ  Vis 
pūrvavat padmamālikhya tanmadhye 'ṣṭākṣaraṃ nyaset 
aṣṭākṣarasya madhye tu catuṣpādāsanaṃ nyaset  Vis 
prokṣayenmūlamantreṇa dharmajñānādikān nyaset 
gandhapuṣpādinābhyarcya tanmadhye harimānayet  Vis

kautukaṃ bandhayet paścāt puṇḍarīkākṣavidyayā  Vis 
āḍhakatrayasaṃpūrṇaṃ śālitaṇḍulamuttamam 
sauvarṇādiṣu pātreṣu hyekaṃ gṛhya vicakṣaṇaḥ  Vis 
pūrayettaṇḍulaṃ śuddhaṃ kundendudhavalaprabham 
taṇḍulordhve 'bjamālikhya cāṣṭapatraṃ sakarṇikam  Vis

dhūpāt bhasmaṃ
samādāya rakṣāṃ kṛtvā samantrataḥ  Vis

apūpādīni sarvāṇi upahārāṇi dāpayet

rātriṃrātrau
visarjayet paścāt pūrvoktairdravyavistaraiḥ  Vis

tatastu viṣṇugāyatryā yaruṃ hutvākṣamātrataḥ

pūrṇāhutiṃ tato hutvā dvādaśākṣaravidyayā

pūrvavadbalidānaṃ tu prāsāde tu yathākramam  Vis

madhyāhne tvaghanāśaṃ tannagarādiṣu vṛddhikṛt

vāsitādyaiśca mātrābhistoṣitaṃ sumanoramam  Vis

rathaṃ tu śibikāṃ vāpi gajaṃ vāśvavaraṃ tu vā  Vis 
prokṣayedgāruḍenaiva bhūṣayedgaruḍaṃ smaran

devāgāreṣu sarveṣu mahāśāstālayeṣu ca  Vis 
kūpe caiva kūpeṣu ca
taṭākeṣu saṅgameṣu ca vīthitaḥ

pāyasānnaṃ gulopetaṃ tulasīpatrasaṃyutam  Vis 
karavīrasamāyuktaṃ śvetaraktākṣatairyutam
