balyante paramātmānamarghyapādyādinārcayet  Vis 
sarvamaṅgalakārye 'smin maṅgalālāpanaṃ kuru 
tṛtīyasavane gatvā devāgāre munīśvara  Vis 
pādyādisaptakaṃ datvā tataḥ snapanamārabhet 
maṇḍapaṃ samalaṃkṛtya śālinā vedimācaret  Vis 
tatra madhye tu matimān kalaśān viniveśayet 
śālmalīkiṃśukāpuṣpasaṃkāśān sūtraveṣṭitān  Vis 
vedikopari saṃsthāpya caturvedādimantrataḥ 
teṣāṃ madhye muniśreṣṭha dravyāṇi viniveśayet  Vis 
pādyaṃ tu madhyame bhāge pūrvabhāger'ghyameva ca 
yāmye tvācamanīyaṃ syādgandhaṃ vāruṇagocare  Vis 
puṣpatoyaṃ nyaset some kṛśānau taṇḍulodakam 
nairṛte dadhi vinyasya vāyavye kṣīrameva ca  Vis 
aiśānye vinyasedājyaṃ gandhayuktaṃ śubhaṃ mune 
evaṃ tu navakaṃ sthāpya kūrcāṃsteṣu vinikṣipet  Vis 
cakrikāṃ sthāpayetteṣu gandhapuṣpaṃ vinikṣipet 
tatastu rajanīcūrṇaṃ pūrve vā cottare 'tha vā  Vis 
sthāpayitvārcayettasmin gandhapuṣpākṣataiḥ kramāt 
kalaśān navavastraistu veṣṭayet praṇavena tu  Vis 
puṇyāhaṃ vācayet samyagyāthātathyena nārada 
gandhapuṣapādinābhyarcya toraṇe 'ṣṭaghaṭān nyaset  Vis 
pūrvādi cottarānteṣu dvau dvau tu kalaśau nyaset 
gandhatoyena saṃpūrya gandhapuṣpādinārcayet  Vis 
svanāmnā caiva sarveṣāṃ mantraṃ tu munipuṅgava 
ṣaḍakṣaramanusmṛtya sādhakaḥ paramārthavit  Vis 
pādyādyaiḥ kalaśaiḥ sarvaiḥ deveśamabhiṣecayet 
snapanānte tu mantrajño rajanīmabhiṣecayet  Vis 
śuddhasnānaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā alaṃkṛtya janārdanam 
snānodakaṃ to gṛhya vaiṣṇavān prokṣayedbudhaḥ  Vis 
taṃ gṛhītvā tu bhaktānāṃ sarveṣāṃ mūrdhni nikṣipet 
gaṅgāsnānaphalaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvapāpapraṇāśanam  Vis 
sarvasaṃpatsamṛddhiḥ syāditi śāstrasya niścayaḥ 
pūrvavadyānamadhye tu devamāropya mantravit  Vis 
purāṇoktataṭāke vā nadītīre 'thavā mune 
devadevaṃ samānīya mūlamantreṇa sādhakaḥ  Vis 
snāpayetteyamadhye tu pūrvavanmunipuṅgava 
mahājanān samāhūya dadyāttīrthamanuttamam  Vis 
svastivācanasaṃyuktaṃ śaṅkhadundubhisaṃyutam 
devālayaṃ kramādgatvā dvāramāśritya nārada  Vis 
arghyapādyādinābhyarcya rakṣāṃ kurvīta mantravit 
annena vātha puṣpairvā aṣṭadigbalimācaret  Vis 
sudarśanena mantreṇa pūrvādiṣu yathākramam 
devāgāraṃ samāśritya svastivācanapūrvakam  Vis 
pūrvavaddevamabhyarcya mahānnaṃ ca nivedayet 
ācāryaṃ pūjayet paścāt yathāśaktyatra nārada  Vis 
apūpādīni cānyāni upahārāṇi dāpayet 
tāmbūlaṃ dāpayet paścāt vidhivat parameṣṭhinā  Vis 
śeṣakarmāṇi sarvāṇi rājavat pratikārayet 
yaḥ kārayettu matimān ihalāke śriyaṃ labhet  Vis 
sa yāti viṣṇusālokyaṃ viṣṇusārūpyameva ca 
atha vā muniśārdūla tīrthasnānavidhiṃ śṛṇu  Vis 
nadīpulinatīre tu maṇḍapaṃ kārayet kramāt 
atha vā suprapāṃ kṛtvā caturdvārasamanvitām  Vis 
vāsādhivāsane proktaṃ prapālakṣaṇamuttamam 
evaṃ lakṣaṇasaṃyuktāṃ prapāṃ kṛtvā munīśvara  Vis 
aindrādīśānaparyantaṃ gomayenānulepayet 
pūrvoktaśālīnāstīrya vitānādyairalaṃkṛtam  Vis 
puṣpamālādisaṃyuktaṃ tanmadhye kalaśān nyaset 
pūrvavannavakaṃ sthāpya pūrvavat snānamācaret  Vis 
tīrthasnānaṃ tato brahman mahājanasamanvitam 
nadyāṃ hrade taṭāke vā deveśaṃ snānamācaret  Vis 
tīre devaṃ samānīya śuddhasnānaṃ samācaret 
arghyādinārcayeddevamalaṃkṛtya prayatnataḥ  Vis 
śeṣakarmāṇi sarvāṇi asmin pūrvavadācaret 
dviprakāraṃ mayā proktaṃ tīrthasnānaṃ munīśvara  Vis 
sādhakecchānurūpeṇa yathāyogaṃ samācaret 
tīrthasnānavidhiḥ proktaḥ pūrvapūrvā garīyasī  Vis 
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktamamāvāsyotsavaṃ param 
anyathā niṣphalaṃ yāti rogavṛddhirdhanakṣayaḥ  Vis 
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena kārayedvidhipūrvakam 
iti śrīpañcarātre viṣvaksenasaṃhitāyāṃ amāvāsyotsavavidhirnāmāṣṭāviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ 
ekonatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
viṣvaksenaḥ
rāghavasyaiva vakṣyāmi tathā janmadinakriyām 
ṛkṣe punarvasau kāryaṃ caitre nāvamike tithau  Vis 
māghamāse 'thavā brahyan rāghavotsavamuttamam 
kṛtvāṅkurārpaṇaṃ pūrvaṃ tataścotsavamācaret  Vis 
snapanaṃ vidhivat kṛtvā sāyāhne rāghavasya tu 
ācāryaṃ pūjayet paścāt vastrahemāṅgulīyakaiḥ  Vis 
godānaṃ bhūmidānaṃ ca suvarṇaṃ rajataṃ tathā 
paśvājyatiladānaṃ ca gogrāsaṃ ca yathāvidhi  Vis 
kautukaṃ bandhayet paścāt supuṇyāhapuraḥsaram 
homaṃ caiva vidhānena kārayet sādhakottmaḥ  Vis 
samidho mūlamantreṇa praṇavenājyameva ca 
pratyekamaṣṭāviṃśaśca caruhomamathācaret  Vis 
ṣoḍaśarcaṃ ca puṃsūktamato devāḥ ṣaḍarcakam 
pañcopaniṣadaṃ caiva viṣṇornukamiti tryṛcā  Vis 
dvādaśākṣaramantreṇa vauṣaḍantena homayet 
etānpūrṇāhutiṃ hutvā homaśeṣaṃ samāpayet  Vis 
tato homāvasāne tu puṇyāhaṃ kārayet kramāt 
tatastu dāpayettatra homapuṇyāhadakṣiṇām  Vis 
ātmanyāropayedagnimātmānaṃ cārpayeddharau 
rāghavaṃ pūjayet paścāt rāmamantreṇa mantravit  Vis 
havirnivedayet paścāt pañcadhā parameṣṭhinā 
odanaṃ kṛsaraṃ gaulyaṃ pāyasaṃ dadhisaktukam  Vis 
pānīyaṃ ca sugandhāḍhyaṃ mukhavāsaṃ ca dāpayet 
vividhāni ca bhakṣyāṇi vividhāni phalāni ca  Vis 
brāhmaṇān bhojayettatra vaiṣṇavān vedapāragān 
geyanṛttavinodādyai rātriśeṣaṃ samāpeyat  Vis 
prabhātāyāṃ tu śarvaryāmalaṃkāraṃ tu dāpayet 
alaṃkṛtya janān sarvān viṣṇupriyatamān samān  Vis 
tailaiścandanapaṅkaiśca aṅgarāgaiśca sarvaśaḥ 
haridrācūrṇapuṣpaiśca vastrairnānāvidhaistathā  Vis 
jalayuktāśca śataśo jalamiśrairitastataḥ 
anyonyaṃ cikṣukṣi
puḥ sarve nṛttagītasamanvitāḥ  Vis 
citradhvajavitānaiśca cāmarastālavṛntakaiḥ 
śaṅkhadundubhinirghoṣaiḥ kṣvelitāsphoṭitairapi  Vis 
nṛttageyaiśca vādyaiśca bhaktairbhāgavataistathā 
jayaśaṣdaravaiścaiva yuktaṃ kuryānmahotsavam  Vis 
tailagandhajalairyuktaṃ rajanīcūrṇasaṃyutam 
grāmaṃ paribhramīkṛtya gaccheyuḥ punarālayam  Vis 
snāpayeddevadevaṃ taṃ yathāvibhavavistaram 
vastrābharaṇagandhādyairalaṃkṛtya prayatnataḥ  Vis 
mahāhavirnivedyātha bhaktānāṃ caiva pūjanam 
evaṃ yaḥ kārayed bhaktya cotsavaṃ rājajanmani  Vis 
sa yāti viṣṇusālokyaṃ kramāt pāriṣadeśvaraḥ 
iti śrīpāñcārātre viṣvaksenasaṃhitāyāṃ śrīrāmajanmotsava vidhirnāma ekonatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
triṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
viṣvaksenaḥ
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi kṛṣṇajanmadinotsavam 
sarvalokahitārthāya saṃbhūtaṃ yādave kule  Vis 
devakyāṃ vasudevasya devānāṃ hitakāmyayā 
śrāvaṇe kṛṣṇapakṣe ca rohiṇyāmaṣṭame tithau  Vis 
aṅkurārpaṇapūrvaṃ tu saptapañcadine 'thavā 
madhyarātre tu pūrve tu kṛṣṇabimbamanuttamam  Vis 
navanītanaṭaṃ vāpi sarpanṛttamathāpi vā 
caturbhujaṃ vāpi tathā pūjayettaddine mune  Vis 
prāsādapūrvabhāge tu maṇḍapaṃ caturaśrakam 
vitānadhvajasaṃyuktaṃ darbhamālāsamāvṛtam  Vis 
puṣpamālyairalaṃkṛtya muktādāmai
ralaṃkṛtam 
indrādīśānaparyantaṃ mārjanaṃ praṇavena tu  Vis 
prokṣayedgandhatoyena dvādaśākṣaravidyayā 
gomayena samālipya pūrvādikramayogataḥ  Vis 
pradīpaṃ ca caturdikṣu dīpayet sādhakaḥ kramāt 
pālikābhiralaṃkṛtya maṇḍapasya samantataḥ  Vis 
maṇḍapasya ca madhye tu catuṣpādāsanaṃ nyaset 
tatrordhve chādanaṃ kuryāt sitapuṣpaṃ vinikṣipet  Vis 
arcayedgandhapuṣpaistu dharmādikramayogataḥ 
bimbaṃ tu sthāpayettatra brāhmaṇaiḥ svastivācya ca  Vis 
kautukaṃ bandhayitvā tu brāhmaṇanāmanujñayā 
aṅguṣṭhānāmikābhyāṃ tu dvādaśākṣaravidyayā  Vis 
mukhavāsaṃ tato dadyāt tālavṛntaiśca vījayet 
chatracāmarasaṃyuktaṃ nṛttagītasamanvitam  Vis 
vīṇāveṇusamāyuktaṃ kautukaṃ bandhayeddhareḥ 
śaṅkhadundubhisaṃyuktaṃ svastivācanapūrvakam  Vis 
pādukādvayasaṃyuktaṃ śayane saṃniveśayet 
pūrvavacchayanaṃ kalpya tanmadhye devamānayet  Vis 
dakṣiṇe balabhadraṃ ca paścāttatrādhivāsayet 
aṣṭākṣareṇa digbandhaṃ kārayet sādhakottamaḥ  Vis 
tathaiva vinyaseddevaṃ viṣṇumantreṇa sādhakaḥ 
pādyārghyācamanīyaṃ ca gandhapuṣpaṃ tathaiva ca  Vis 
puṇyāhaṃ vācayettatra vaiṣṇavairvedapāragaiḥ 
ācāryaḥ śuklavāsāstu śuklayajñopavītavān  Vis 
ūrdhvapuṇḍradharaścaiva sapavitrakarastathā 
ājānupādau prakṣālya dvirdvirācamanīyakam  Vis 
devasya dakṣiṇe pārśve uttarābhimukhāsane 
prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ kṛtvā sṛṣṭinyāsaṃ tathaiva ca  Vis 
tathaiva devaṃ vinyasya mantramaṣṭākṣaraṃ mune 
sauvarṇādighaṭaṃ gṛhya śuddhatoyena mantravit  Vis 
tatpātraṃ kṣālayet paścāt viṣṇugāyatriyā mune 
toyapūrṇaṃ sugandhaṃ ca sūtravastrasamanvitam  Vis 
dhānyarāśau vinikṣipya tasya madhye mahāmune 
mūlaberāttato devaṃ dhyāyannārāyāṇaṃ prabhum  Vis 
śyāmalaṃ bālavapuṣaṃ kṛṣṇaberamunasmaran 
tattoyaṃ pratimāmūrdhni secayenmūlavidyayā  Vis 
kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā namaskṛtya punaḥ punaḥ 
śayane śāyayitvā tu taṃ devaṃ mūlavidyayā  Vis 
tathaiva balabhadraṃ ca śāyayettasya mantrataḥ 
vastrairācchādayeddevaṃ sitapuṣpaiḥ samarcayet  Vis 
tato nārāyaṇaṃ sūktamuccaret sādhakottamaḥ 
śaṅkhadundubhisaṃyuktaṃ vedādhyayanasaṃyutam  Vis 
vīṇāveṇusamāyuktaṃ jhallarīmaddalairyutam 
vārasairandhrisaṃyuktamācāryo mantramuccaran  Vis 
śaṅkhādighoṣasaṃyuktaṃ tato devaṃ samuddharet 
gandhapuṣpaṃ vinikṣipya namaskṛtya punaḥ punaḥ  Vis 
śrīramājyena saṃyuktaṃ bhalabhadrāya dāpayet 
vaiṣṇavebhyaḥ sadasyānāṃ sarveṣāṃ ca pradāpayet  Vis 
kṣīraṃ dadhighṛtaṃ caiva pradadyādbalakṛṣṇayo 
kadalīpanasaṃ caiva jambvādiphalameva ca  Vis 
tadante devadevasya dāpayenmūlavidyayā 
tailaṃ ca rajanīcūrṇaṃ tāvubhau mūrdhni secayet  Vis 
śeṣaṃ ca vaiṣṇavebhyastu dadyāt sarvamathāpi vā 
śaṅkhadundubhinirghoṣaiḥ tūryaveṇusamanvitaiḥ  Vis 
nṛttagītasamāyuktaṃ brāhmaṇaiḥ svastivācanam 
rāmakṛṣṇo tu saṃsthāpya cāsane puṣpasaṃyute  Vis 
arghyapādyādinābhyarcya homakarma samācaret 
nityāgnau vātha pūrvasmin kārayedvā mahāmune  Vis 
vaiṣṇavāgnau tu juhuyāt samidājyacarūṇi ca 
mūlamantreṇa mantrajñaḥ pañcaviṃśatisaṃkhyayā  Vis 
pratyekaṃ tu muniśreṣṭha paścācchāntiṃ samācaret 
madhunā payasā dadhnā hūyatena
ghṛtena ca  Vis 
tathaiva juhuyānmantraiḥ pūrṇāhutimathācaret 
homānte devadeveśaṃ snāpayedvidhicoditam  Vis 
kṛṣṇagandhena kāṣṭhane uśīraiścandanena ca

siddhārthasarṣapaiścaiva sarvadhānyāni sādhakaḥ

tatastu rajanīcūrṇaṃ snāpayeddevamūrdhani 
puṣpaṃ datvā namaskṛtya maṅgalālāpanaṃ kuru  Vis 
śuddhasnānaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā gandhatoyena sādhakaḥ 
vastrābharaṇamālyaiśca kṛtvā gandhānulepanam  Vis 
arcayedvidhivaddevaṃ gandhapuṣpādibhistathā 
alaṃkṛtya tato devaṃ nīrājanasamanvitam  Vis 
godānaṃ bhūmidānaṃ ca hiraṇyaṃ vastrabhūṣaṇam 
sarvadānaṃ tato dadyāt brāhmaṇebhyo yathākramam  Vis 
tadante vaiṣṇavān pūjya bhojanācchādanādibhiḥ 
tāmbūlaṃ vātha sarveṣāṃ yathāvittānusārataḥ  Vis 
hiraṇyaṃ vātha vastraṃ vā gāvo vā dhānyameva vā

dānasyānantaraṃ devamarghyapādyādinārcayet 
pāyasaṃ kṛsaraṃ gaulyaṃ śuddhānnaṃ ca pṛthak pṛthak  Vis 
kadalīpanasairyuktaṃ deveśāya nivedayet 
pānīyācamanīyaṃ ca dadyāddevāya bhaktitaḥ  Vis 
bhojyāsanaṃ vyapohyāśu devaṃ bhogāsane nayet 
devasyācamanaṃ dadyānmukhavāsaṃ pradāpayet  Vis 
pūrvamālāṃ visṛjyātha cānmālāṃ tu dāpayet 
devadevamalaṃkṛtya mukhavāsaṃ punardadet  Vis 
nṛttagītasamāyuktaṃ vīṇāveṇusamanvitam 
devāgāraṃ paribhramya garbhagehe nayeddharim  Vis 
prabhātāyāṃ tu śarvaryāmutsavaṃ kārayettataḥ 
grāme vā nagare vāpi mārgaśuddhiṃ ca kārayet  Vis 
śibikāṃ vā rathaṃ vāpi kuñjaraṃ vā hayaṃ tu vā

evaṃ devamalaṃkṛtya sthāpayedyānamadhyame

paṭahaistālasaṃyuktaṃ kṛtvā grāmaṃ paribhramet 
tailaiścandranasaṃyuktaṃ rajanīcūrṇameva ca  Vis 
dāpayedvaiṣṇavānāṃ tu sadasyānāṃ viśeṣataḥ 
punaḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā devālayamanuttamam  Vis 
vidhivat snapanaṃ kṛtvā devadevaṃ sanātanam 
mahāhavirnivedyātha garbhāgāre nayeddharim  Vis 
iti saṃkṣepataḥ proktaḥ kṛṣṇajanmadinotsavaḥ 
sarvapāpakṣayakaraḥ sarvayajñaphalapradaḥ  Vis

mune yaugapadyena sāṃnidhyamasmin krameṇeti vā saṃśayaḥ prādurāsīt  Vis

athānyo mahābhogayogapradāyī prajānāṃ tathā vṛddhido muktidaśca 
paraṃ mūlamantreṇa saṃsmṛtya pañcā ṅgulaṃ hṛdi spṛśya bimbasya mudrām  Vis 
pradṛśyāṅgulisaṃjñitāṃ pādamūle praṇamyākṣataṃ vāpi puṣpaṃ prakīrya 
mune vidyayāṣṭārṇayaivātha cārghyaṃ punaḥ pādyācamanaṃ gandhapuṣpam  Vis 
tato dhūpadīpaṃ pradāyātha bhūtānnaṃ nivedyāntarāvaraṇaṃ kalpya samyak 
tathāvaraṇānāṃ yathāpūrvamarghyā dyanenaiva mantreṇa puṣpaṃ pradāya  Vis 
nivedyātha tāmbūlikāmacyutāya pradīpyo baliṃ homamante vidhāya

nāradaḥ

athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi hetirājasya lakṣaṇam 
śṛṇu nārada guhyena
uttamādi krameṇa tu  Vis 
sahasrāraṃ mahācakraṃ śatāraṃ vārdhameva vā 
ṣoḍaśāraṃ tu vā cakraṃ dvādaśāramathāpi vā  Vis 
kārayenmuniśārdūla sauvarṇādikrameṇa tu

kārayeddhetirājānamuttamādhamamadhyataḥ

athavātra muniśreṣṭha mānamārgaṃ vidhīyate

cakreṇa dviguṇīkṛtya daṇḍākārāyataṃ bhevat

viṃśatyaṅgulamānaṃ tat pādāyataṃ kramāt sadā

madhyamādhamacakre 'smin nālaṃ kartṛvaśāt kuru

bhaktanāṃ darśanārthaṃ yat cakraṃ tu sumanoramam 
tathaiva kārayedvidvān hetirājasya lakṣaṇam  Vis

  genaiva śuddhyati 
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktaṃ hetirājasya lakṣaṇam

athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi dravyaśuddhividhiṃ param 
ratnāni hemavastāṇi bhūṣaṇādīṃśca tāmrajān  Vis 
annaṃ toyaṃ dadhikṣīre ghṛtaṃ madhugulādayaḥ 
madhuparkaśca puṣpāṇi mukhavāsopahārakam  Vis 
evamādīni cānyāni deveśoya nivedayet 
niveditāni vastūni śuddhāśuddhāni vai śṛṇu  Vis 
annādīnupahārāṃstān varjayenmunisattama

tathaiva tāmrakalaśān vastreṇa pariveṣṭayet  Vis 
mantramāhātmyamātreṇa śuddhyante nātra saṃśayaḥ 
annaṃ toyaṃ dadhikṣīraṃ ghṛtaṃ madhu gulaṃ tathā  Vis

kaniṣṭhamiviṣṭa

tāladvayaṃ tadardhaṃ vā prāsādāt parivārakam 
visṛjya kalpayeddhīmān dvitrihasatamathāpi vā  Vis 
caturhastaṃ pañcahastaṃ vyapohyante mahāmune 
kalpayet parivārāṇāṃ hastamātraṃ samantataḥ  Vis 
śilābhiriṣṭakābhirvā ācāryāṅgulinā mune 
caturaṅgulamutsedhaṃ madhye padmaṃ sakarṇikam  Vis 
kārayet paritaḥ pīṭhaṃ mekhalādvayasaṃyutam 
tālamātreṇa vā kuryāt balipīṭhaṃ samantataḥ  Vis 
tathaiva parivārāṇāṃ prākārānmānamatra tu 
evaṃ kalpya tato pīṭhaṃ parivārasya tu sarvaśaḥ  Vis 
maṇḍapādvā mahāpīṭhaṃ prākārādvā mahāmune 
hastaṃ ṣoḍaśamutsṛjya ācāryāṅgulināgrataḥ  Vis 
aṣṭahastaṃ tadardhaṃ vā visṛjyānte mahāmune 
kārayedvā mahāpīṭhaṃ pūrvāpūrvā garīyasī  Vis

viviktane paraṃ guhyaṃ śṛṇu nārada tattvataḥ  Vis 
tricatuḥpañcahastaṃ vā vistārāyāmatādṛśam taḥ samam 
pādukādyabjaparyantamuttamādikrameṇa tu  Vis 
kārayecchāstradṛṣṭena śilpinā kuśalena tu 
uttame 'pyuttamaṃ kuryāt madhyame madhyamaṃ kuru  Vis 
adhame 'pyadhamaṃ kuryāt vibhavasyānu rūpataḥ 
ṣaṭsaptahastāyataṃ vāpi
tatsamaṃ vistṛtaṃ bhavet  Vis

caiva pañcakairjagatī tathā  Vis 
triyaṃśaṃ kumudaṃ caiva ekāṃśena tu paṭṭikā

triyaṃśervalabhī chandaḥ triyaṃśaṃ karṇikocchrayam yaḥ

śilpakāryāvasāne tu prokṣayettantravittamaḥ

ayane cottare kuryāt pūrvapakṣe śubhe 'hani

takṣakriyāṃ samāpyātha prokṣayettantravittamaḥ

devāgrapīṭhayormadhye maṇḍapaṃ kārayet sudhīḥ 
maṇḍapasya vidhānena toraṇāni tu pūrvavat  Vis 
kṛtvā tu pūrvavat samyak vediṃ kuryāttu madhyataḥ

susnigdhaṃ gdhāṃ
kārayettatra darpaṇodarasaṃnibha bhām 
gomayenopalipyātha prokṣayedgandhavāriṇā  Vis 
tadvedipīṭhayormadhye vṛttaṃ vā caturaśrakam 
kārayettatra kuṇḍaṃ tu madhyame homamācaret  Vis 
śālidroṇadvaye vedyāṃ sakūrcaṃ sāpidhānakam 
sahiraṇyaṃ savastraṃ ca saritsalilapūritam  Vis 
sasūtraṃ kālarahitaṃ droṇapūrṇaṃ suśobhanam

aindrādīśānaparyantaṃ kalaśān sthāpayet pṛthak 
kumudaṃ kumudākṣaṃ ca puṇḍarīkaṃ ca vāmanam  Vis 
śaṅkukarṇaṃ sarpanetraṃ sumukhaṃ supratiṣṭhitam 
gandhādibhiḥ samabhyarcya homaṃ kuryādanandritaḥ  Vis 
samidājyacarūn dadhnā madhunā payasāpi ca

sumuhūrte tu saṃprāpte brāhmaṇānāmunajñayā 
svastisūktikta
yuto gatvā vimānaṃ tu pradakṣiṇam  Vis 
svasvasthāne tu saṃprokṣya tattatsthānān smaran budhaḥ 
kumbhodakādaśeṣaṃ tu mahāpīṭhe 'bhiṣecayet  Vis 
viṣṇupāriṣadān sarvān saṃsmaret sādhakottamaḥ

vedādhyayanasaṃyuktaṃ balikarma samāpayet

mahāhavirnivedyātha puṇyāhaṃ punarācaret

ācāryaṃ pūjayet paścāt hemaratnāṅgulīyakaiḥ 
idaṃ dhanyaṃ yaśasyaṃ ca sarvaśāntikaraṃ bhavet  Vis

viṣvaksenaḥ                
puṇyāhaṃ vācayettatra brāhmaṇaiḥ saha mantravit 
pañcabhārapramāṇaṃ vā tadardhaṃ vārdhameva vā  Vis 
tannyūnaṃ na hi kartavyaṃ śālisaṃcayamuttamam 
tatrordhve vikiredvidvān tadardhaṃ taṇḍulaṃ tathā  Vis 
taṇḍulopari vinyasya cāṣṭapatrābjamuttamam 
tatra madhye likhedbījaṃ dale cāṣṭākṣaraṃ nyaset  Vis 
madhyame navakumbhaṃ tu sthāpayet sādhakottamaḥ 
sūtravastrasamāyuktaṃ ratnamālyeralaṃkṛtam  Vis 
gandhodakena saṃpūrṇaṃ vastragyugmena veṣṭitam 
pūrvādi cāṣṭakumbhasya vastramekaikameva vā  Vis 
diṅmūrtyādīni cāṣṭānāmekavastramathāpi vā

trisaptapañcadarbhairvā kṛtvā kūrcaṃ vinikṣipet

sahasraśīrṣā puruṣaḥ sahasrākṣāḥ sahasrapāt 
sahasrakuntalopetaṃ sahusramakuṭānvitam  Vis 
sahasrādityasaṃkāśaṃ sahasrendunibhānanam 
sahasravāhanairyuktaṃ sarvadiṅnāsikānvitam  Vis 
śaṅkhacakragadāpāṇiṃ sarvapraharaṇānvitam 
prāsādarūpamityāhuḥ pūrvarātre 'dhivāsayet  Vis 
taddhyānenaiva devarṣe samyak snānamavāpnuyāt 
mokṣārthī mokṣamāpnoti tasmāddhyānaṃ viśiṣyate  Vis 
maṇḍapādiṣu sarveṣu dhyānamevaṃ prakīrtitam 
tasmin madhye nayedvidvān smaran tat parameṣṭhinā  Vis 
pūrvādi cottarānte tu tanmūrtiṃ tu vicintayet 
āgneyādiṣu koṇeṣu vainateyādikān nyaset  Vis 
mṛtagasyādhipatiṃ siṃhaṃ vainateyāṃśakaṃ nyaset 
tasmin pūrṇaghaṭe madhye pauruṣaṃ sūktamabhyaset  Vis 
digdevādiṣu kumbheṣu tattanmūrtiṃ japet kramāt 
ṛgādīnāṃ tu vedānāṃ sāramuddhṛtya nārada  Vis 
pūrvādisomaparyantamuccaret susvareṇa tu 
tataḥ pūrṇaghaṭādīni cārcayettena mantrataḥ  Vis 
havirnivedayet paścāt mantreṇa parameṣṭhinā 
mukhavāsaṃ tato dadyāt rakṣāṃ kṛtvāṣṭadikkrāmat  Vis 
ghaṇṭādhvanisamāyuktaṃ gandhapuṣpādibhiḥ saha 
haviṣā balidānaṃ tu kārayedaṣṭadikṣu ca  Vis 
kumudādīni sarvāṇi gṛhṇanti balimuttamam 
śaṅkṣadundubhinirghoṣaṃ kṛtvāsmin munisattama  Vis 
tataḥ puṣpāñjaliṃ kṛtvā sādhakaḥ paramārthavit 
namaskṛtyākhilān sarvān maṅgalānuccaretkramāt  Vis 
prabhātāyāṃ tu śarvaryāmācāryaḥ snānamācaret 
sūktena puruṣeṇaiva mantraṃ vā parameṣṭhinā  Vis 
kumbhasthitena deveśaṃ pūjayet puruṣottamam 
gandhādi dīpaparyantaṃ tattanmantreṇa sādhakaḥ  Vis 
pūrvādīśānaparyantamarcayedaṣṭadigghaṭān 
mahāmumbhādi saṃgṛhya prāsādaṃ tu paribhramet  Vis

svastivācanasaṃyuktaṃ garbhāgāraṃ praveśayet  Vis 
devasyāgre tu saṃsthāpya taṇḍulopari nārada 
mahākumbhasthadeveśaṃ vidhinādhipatiṃ param  Vis 
tatpūrvapārśve saṃsthāpya taṇḍuleṣu ghaṭān kramāt 
arghyapādyādinābhyarcya mukhavāsāvasānakam  Vis 
evamabhyarcya matimān kṣamyatāmiti coccaran

kṣantumarhasi deveśa paripūrṇaṃ tadastu me 
evaṃ kṛtvā tu mantrajño maṅgalāni samīrayet  Vis 
ācāryaḥ puṣpamādāya namaskṛtya hariṃ prabhum

tathaivāṣṭaghaṭācchaktiṃ taddehe viniveśayet

mūlaberasya mūrdhneva secayettāṃstribindunā 
devapāde tu hastābhyāṃ puṣpaṃ datvā punaḥ punaḥ  Vis 
tataḥ puruṣasūktaṃ tu brāhmaṇaiḥ saha saṃjapet 
tasmin kāle mahāprājña ācāryaṃ pūjayeddhanaiḥ  Vis 
navavastrāṅgulīyaistu kaṭakādivibhūṣaṇaiḥ

atropayuktaṃ yaddravyaṃ devatālaṃkṛtaṃ tiḥ vinā

niveditaṃ tu tatsarvaṃ sāttvatebhyo nivedayet

kriyāvasāne matimān citrakarma ca kārayet  Vis 
havanaṃ maṇḍapādyeṣu evameva samācaret

vāsādhivāsanaṃ caiva prāsādaprokṣaṇe mune

anyathā kurute mohāt grāmanāśo dhanakṣayaḥ

asmin munivaraśreṣṭha trapukaṃ cāyasaṃ vinā  Vis

cāturvarṇyasamopetaḥ
sadācāraparāyaṇaḥ 
sadvaṃśyaḥ sarvaśāstrajño lokajñaḥ sarvadharmavit  Vis

viṣvaksenaḥ

vṛttaṃ vākṛti vijñeyaḥ
caturaśraṃ tu vādhiḥ

sahasraśīrṣādīni di
sūktaṃ tu puruṣeṇa tu  Vis 
mulaberānnayet kumbhe devaṃ prāsādarūpiṇam

droṇaśāliṃ tu vistīrya tadardhaṃ taṇḍulaṃ tathā  Vis

caṇḍālādyaiśca saṃspṛṣṭaṃṣṭe
prāyaścittamidaṃ smṛtam  Vis

āyurārogyaputrādīn labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ 
utsavānte pralepānte durjanasparśane tathā  Vis 
durnimittātto

ardhacitrapratiṣṭhāsmin śeṣaṃ sādhāraṇaṃ bhavet

caṇḍālādyaiśca saṃspṛṣṭaṃṣṭe
prāyaścittaṃ samācaret

dhūpadīpaṃ pau

kṛṣṇakuṣṭhaśarīre

puruṣaśca ṣe ca

saṃpaśyan śūlarājānaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā  Vis 
ārogśyaṃ balamaiśvaryaṃ kīrtiṃ vidyādhanāgamam 
labhate nāsti sandeho darpaṇasya ca darśanāt  Vis 
lābhahāniryaśo hānirāyurhānistathaiva ca 
sarvahānirbhavatyeva nagnasyaiva ca darśanāt  Vis 
cittārthaṃ labhate tatra śubhaṃ vāpyaśubhaṃ tu vā 
śatrukṣayaṃ ca bhavati pradīpaṃ yastu paśyati  Vis 
arthahānirmanastāpaḥ gṛhe duścaritaṃ bhavet 
vidhavādarśanaṃ yasya bhavatyatra na saṃśayaḥ  Vis 
arthalābho manastuṣṭiḥ gṛhe saṃpadbhaviṣyati 
cintitārthaṃ labhettatra sumaṅgalyāḥ pradarśane  Vis 
śmaśānaṃ dṛśyate yatra grāmanāśaṃ dhanakṣayam 
bandhudevaviyogaṃ ca sarvate bhayameva vā  Vis 
abhayaṃ sarvatattveṣu kūrmarāpajapradarśanāt 
rājyaṃ śriyaṃ ca saṃprāpya kṣemārogyayuto bhavet  Vis 
śatruvṛddhirdhanacchedaḥ vyādhirdurbhikṣavardhanam 
cintitaṃ naśyate
 tatra mahākālīpradarśanāt  Vis 
vijayaṃ cārthalābhaṃ ca kīrtiśrīvardhanaṃ tathā 
putrapautravivṛddhiśca durge dṛṣṭe na saṃśayaḥ  Vis 
vyādhiṃ pravāsaṃ maraṇaṃ vipatsyati na saṃśayaḥ 
pañcāsyapannagaṃ paśyet pāpibhiścābhibhūyate  Vis 
vyādhināśo
mahadduḥkhaṃ kuṭumbasya vināśanam 
ālokite mahāpāpe gardabhe syānna saṃśayaḥ  Vis 
jaradgavaṃ prapaśyetā narāḥ śokārṇavaṃ punaḥ 
vrajanti vyādhinā pīḍā kalahaṃ ca gṛhe bhavet  Vis 
cakravartinamāyāntaṃ avalokya janādhipam 
śriyaṃ prāpnoti putrāṃśca puṣṭiṃ ca labhate naraḥ  Vis 
caturmukhaṃ samālokya brahmāṇaṃ kamalāsanam 
sarvādhipatyamāpne vaṃśavṛddhiśca jāyate  Vis 
viṣṇumālokya deveśaṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharam 
sarvādhipatyamāsthāya sthitiṃ ca labhate naraḥ  Vis 
rudramālokya bhūteśaṃ śūlapāṇimumāpatim 
śatrusainyaṃ mahajjitvā modate saha bandhubhiḥ  Vis 
ete ślokā mayoddiṣṭāḥ śakunānāṃ viśeṣataḥ 
etāṃstu pustake likhya vivekaṃ sumanoramam  Vis 
ekapatre tathaikaikaṃ ślokaṃ saṃlikhya vāgyataḥ 
sūtreṇa sūtrayitvā tu puṣpādibhirathārcayet  Vis 
anujñāpya tato devaṃ vighneśaṃ gaṇanāyakam 
ānīya tu tataḥ śiṣyān baddhanetrān yathākramam  Vis 
teṣāṃ haste tu puṣpāṇi nidhāya ca samāhitaḥ 
ādāya pustakaṃ paścāt praṇavena samāhitaḥ  Vis 
śiṣyahaste nidhāyātha namaskṛtvā prasādya ca 
prārthayecca sa tenātha vighnarājāgnisaṃbhavam  Vis 
namaste 'stu jagannātha lambodara gajānana 
saṃśaye 'smin mahābāho saṃtyaṃ saṃdarśayasva naḥ  Vis 
satyaṃ hi bhavatāmāhuḥ manuyastattvadarśinaḥ 
iti vijñāpya deveśaṃ śiṣyaṃ brūyāttataḥ param  Vis 
visraṃsayitvā sūtraṃ tu patraṃ gṛhṇīṣva pustake 
ityuktastu tataḥ śiṣyaḥ srasayitvā tu sūtrakam  Vis 
gṛhṇīyāt patramekaṃ tu hastaprāptaṃ yadṛcchayā 
ācāryastu tato tetrabandhanaṃ pravimucya ca  Vis 
dehi patramiti bruyāt śiṣyaṃ prati samāhitaḥ 
śiṣyastu patraṃ dadyācca guruhaste mahāmune  Vis 
gurustu vācayet patramasaṃmūḍhena cetasā 
taduktaṃ vidhivajjñātvā śubhaṃ vā yadi vāśubham  Vis 
tataḥ śiṣyaṃ pratibrūyādyathoktaṃ sarvameva tu 
pratiśiṣyaṃ tathā kṛtvā jñātvā karma śubhāśubham  Vis 
dīkṣayecchiṣyamācāryastatparaṃ lakṣaṇānvitam 
etat pustakamādāya sūtrayitvā vicakṣaṇaḥ  Vis 
anyeṣāmapi bhaktānāmanena vidhinā punaḥ 
pūjayitvā gaṇeśaṃ tu pustakaṃ ca yathākramam  Vis 
śubhāśubhavidhiṃ prājñaḥ prabrūyāddeśikottamaḥ 
na nāstikānāṃ saṃpaśyet nābhaktānāṃ kadācana  Vis 
na nindakānāṃ sarveṣāṃ anācārajuṣāmapi 
durvṛttānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ bāhyadīkṣājuṣāmapi  Vis 
asaṃbhāṣyeṇa paśyecca na vijñāte kadācana 
śiṣyāṇāṃ vanitānāṃ tu bhaktānāmapi sarvadā  Vis 
saṃśayāviṣṭacetānāṃ kṛpaṇānāṃ gurau sadā 
ajihmakānāṃ bhaktānāṃ deyametadyathātatham  Vis 
anuktaguṇayuktānāṃ yadi paśyettu dadyāttu deśikaḥ 
devatāśca prakupyante
 na tathyaṃ ca bhaviṣyati  Vis 
iti vijñāya sarvaṃ tu prapaśyecchakunāni tu 
śakunānte tato vighnanāyakaṃ pūjayet kramāt  Vis 
pustakaṃ pūjayet paścāt gandhapuṣpādibhiḥ punaḥ 
ācāryaṃ pūjayet paścāt sarvasvaṃ vādharmeva vā  Vis 
yathāvittānusāreṇa
 pūjayedgurupūjanam 
udvāsayettato devamākāśe gaṇanāyakam  Vis 
iti śrīpāñcarātre viṣvaksenasaṃhitāyāṃ dīkṣāśakunavistāro nāma saptatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ 
aṣṭatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
viṣvaksenaḥ
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi jalasaṃprokṣaṇaṃ param 
rahasyaṃ paramaṃ guhyaṃ sarvapāpapraṇāśanam  Vis 
tava snehāt pravakṣyāmi tridaśerapi durlabham 
sadya eva tu kartavyaṃ prāyaścittaṃ tu nārada  Vis 
na tithirna ca nakṣatraṃ kālavelā na vidyate 
duḥsthitaṃ susthitaṃ vāpi devabimbaṃ na cālayet  Vis 
śilābimbaṃ tathā lauhaṃ bimbaṃ vā caikaberakam 
daivādvā mānuṣādvāpi mohādvā munisattama  Vis 
cālayedyadi tadbimbaṃ prāyaścittaṃ viśeṣataḥ 
kārayenmuniśārdūla sarvasaṃpatsukhāvaham  Vis 
prāsādakaraṇe kāle navakarmakṛte sati 
citrakarmakṛte vāpi citrakārādi saṃspṛśet  Vis 
spṛśyate vā nikṛṣṭaistu devaścaṇḍālapātakaiḥ 
pīṭhe śvabhrasthite kāle calite pūrvavat kṛte  Vis 
candanādīni puṣpāṇi tathā sarvauṣadhīni ca 
kuśapallavadūrvāśca pūrayitvā tadūrdhvataḥ  Vis 
yojayet pañcagavyena prāṅmukhaḥ sakuśodakam 
arcayitvārghyagandhādyaiḥ sāṅmūlaṃ samuccaran  Vis 
ācchādya navavastreṇa dadyādbhūtabaliṃ tataḥ 
devatāyatanagrāmanagareṣvapi pallike  Vis 
sthāpanāspadamāsādya śodhanaṃ pañcagavyakaiḥ 
tatra madhye khanet śvabhraṃ mūlamantramudīrayan  Vis 
aṅguṣṭhodaramāvartya tridhā sūtreṇa veṣṭayet 
tenaiva bhrāmayenmadhye sthāpya tatrāvaṭaṃ khanet  Vis 
hastamātramadhastācca ṣaḍaṅgulasamanvitam 
saṃprokṣya pañcagavyena tatra ratnādikaṃ nyaset  Vis 
śeṣaṃ dhyātvā tadūrdhve tu abhyarcyārghyādibhiḥ kramāt 
vāsasācchādya digbandhamācaredastramuccaran  Vis 
saṃspṛśca gavyakumbhābhyāṃ dhyātvā mūlaṃ japedguruḥ 
prabhātāyāṃ tu śarvaryāṃ kṛtvā snānādikīṃ kriyām  Vis 
kumbhasthaṃ nṛhariṃ pūjya japāntaṃ pūrvavartmanā 
puṇyāhavācanaṃ kṛtvā muhūrte śobhane guruḥ  Vis 
padmapatrāvavṛ
tu kumbhaṃ śvabhre tāreṇa vinyaset 
paritaḥ sarvadhānyena pūrayitvā caśalaṃ  yathā  Vis 
pañcagavyaṃ samuddhṛtya ghaṭasthaṃ kalaśaṃ laban 
tenaiva pūrayet kumbhaṃ śvabhrasthaṃ mūlamuccaran  Vis 
samabhyarcyārghyapuṣpādyaiḥ pūrayenmṛdbhirāhṛtaiḥ 
śaṃsūktaṃ bhadrasūktaṃ ca svastisūktaṃ ca pākkṛte  Vis 
etat sādhāraṇaṃ proktaṃ bahuberaikaberayoḥ 
sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpannamaṅgayuktaṃ dvijottamam  Vis 
padavākyapramāṇajñaṃ devayajña vratasthitam 
evaṃ lakṣaṇasaṃyuktamācāryaṃ tantrapāragam  Vis 
jñātvā tenaiva kartavyaṃ jalasaṃprokṣaṇaṃ śubham 
prāsādāgre munireṣṭha kuryānmaṇḍapamuttamam  Vis 
dakṣiṇe 'pyathavā kuryāt uttare vā mahāmune 
aiśāne vātra matimān yathālābhaṃ sudikṣu ca  Vis 
caturaśraṃ sukhaṃ samyak vistārāyāmatādṛśamtaḥ samam 
karaṣoḍaśakaṃ vāpi hastaṃ pañcadaśaṃ tu vā  Vis 
stambhaṣoḍaśasaṃyuktaṃ caturdvārasamanvitam 
iṣṭakādārupāṣāṇaiḥ kṛtāṃ samyaksuvedikām  Vis 
hastamātrasamāyuktaṃ dhvajāśāmukhatoraṇam 
darbhamālāparivṛtaṃ puṣpamālyairalaṃkṛtam  Vis 
phalapallavamālādyairdhūpadīpasamanvitam 
śālisaṃcayasaṃpūrṇaṃ prāgudakpravaṇaṃ śubham  Vis 
vitānenordhvamācchādya nānāvastrairalaṃkṛtam 
chatracāmarasaṃyuktaṃ muktādāmai
 ralaṃkṛtam  Vis 
dhvajairnānārvidheścitrairdīpamālāvirājitam 
varṣavātairna cākrāntaṃ pālikābhiralaṃkṛtam  Vis 
etasya maṇḍapasyāgra'pyattare vā yathākramam 
īśāne vā muniśreṣṭha kuryāt snapanamaṇḍapam  Vis 
hastadvayapramāṇena visatārāyāmatādṛśam taḥ samam 
maṇḍapasyaiśapūrve tu snapanārthaṃ suvedikām  Vis 
hastocchrayāṃ tadardhāṃ vā hyuttare śvabhrasaṃyutām 
dhārāyugvedikāṃ kuryāt paścime kalaśān nyaset  Vis 
snapanaṃ kārayedevaṃ ekāśītikrameṇa tu 
ekaberavidhānaṃ cet mūlārcāyāṃ prayojayet  Vis 
karmārcāyāṃ tu kartavyaṃ bahuberavidhau sati 
snapanaṃ vidhivat kṛtvā tataḥ karma samārabhet  Vis 
pītavastraistu śuklairvā veṣṭayeddevapīṭhakam 
tato 'smin maṇḍape dvāri kalaśāṃstoraṇadhvajān  Vis 
gandhapuṣpaiḥ samabhyarcya svanāmnaiva pṛthakpṛthak 
tato maṇḍapavedyāṃ ca nikṣipecchālisaṃcayam  Vis 
śālimadhye likhet padmamaṣṭapatraṃ sakarṇikam 
sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ vāpi tāmraṃ vā mṛṇmayaṃ tu vā  Vis 
droṇadvayena saṃpūrṇaṃ nimnoṣaṃ nirdeṣaṃ
kalaśaṃ śubham 
vastrapūtajalaiḥ pūrṇaṃ sakūrcaṃ sāpidhānam  Vis 
sasūtraṃ vastrayugmena veṣṭitaṃ ratnasaṃyutam 
aṣṭaśaktisamāyuktaṃ sauvarṇāyudhapañcayuk  Vis 
tatkumbhaṃ praṇavenaiva śālipadme tu vinyaset 
tataḥ padmadaleṣvaṣṭakalaśān parito nyaset  Vis 
pūrvavattoyasaṃpūrṇān sahiraṇyān savastrakān 
sāpidhānān sakūrcāṃśca mukhe cāśvatthapallavān  Vis 
arcayedgandhapuṣpaiśca dīpairanyaiḥ pavitrakaiḥ 
pūjayenmūlamantreṇa tattanmūrtimanusmaran  Vis 
viṣṇuṃ caiva mahāviṣṇuṃ sadāviṣṇuṃ ca madhyame 
vāsudevāniruddhāntaṃ
nyaset pūrvādidikṣu ca  Vis 
nyasecchriyādiśāntyantamāgneyādividikṣu ca 
evaṃ nyasya vidhānena gandhapuṣpādibhiryajet  Vis 
etānapi samabhyarcya homakarma samārabhet 
pūrvādi cottarāntaṃ tu kuṇḍāni parikalpayet  Vis 
vāsudevaṃ yajet pūrvaṃ kuṇḍe tu caturaśrake 
ardhacandrāgnikuṇḍe tu yāmye saṃkarṣaṇaṃ yajet  Vis 
vāruṇyāṃ vartule kuṇḍe pradyumnaṃ tu yajedbudhaḥ 
uttare 'bje trikoṇe vā aniruddhaṃ yajet prabhum  Vis 
pālāśaṃ khādiraṃ vāpi bailvamaudumbaraṃ tathā 
aṣṭottaraśataṃ hutvā pṛthakpūrvāditaḥ kramāt  Vis 
samidājyacarūn lājaiḥ juhuyurmūrtipāḥ pṛthak 
evaṃ homaṃ praśaṃsanti ekahomena cāpyalam  Vis 
kārayeccaturaśre tu juhuyāttadvidhānataḥ 
vaiṣṇavīkaraṇārthāya kuṇḍaṃ pūrvavadācaret  Vis 
tatkuṇḍe muniśārdūla ācāryo homamācaret 
samidājyena caruṇā juhuyāttu punaḥ punaḥ  Vis 
samidho mūlamantreṇa praṇavenājyameva ca 
caruṃ puruṣasūktena pratyekaṃ ṣoḍaśāhutīḥ  Vis 
evaṃ hutvā vidhānena punarājyena homayet 
pauruṣeṇa ca sūktena juhuyādviṣṇubhaktitaḥ  Vis 
tato nārāyaṇaṃ sūkta sṛṣṭyādipratipādakam 
samyagjñātvā muniśreṣṭha kālyāṃ tu juhuyāt kramāt  Vis 
pañcopaniṣadairmantraiḥ juhuyāttu punaḥ punaḥ 
pūrvavacchāntihomaṃ tu kārayecca vidhānataḥ  Vis 
evaṃ hutvā muniśreṣṭha kautukaṃ bandhayeddharim 
pūrvoktena vidhānena pūjayeddhavirantakam  Vis 
dvādaśākṣaramantreṇa mūrtimantreṇa caiva hi 
kṣaumasūtreṇa vā tatra kārpāsaṃ vā mahāmune  Vis 
prokṣayenmūlamantreṇa tatsūtraṃ tu punaḥ punaḥ 
rātrau mahotsavaṃ kuryāt śaṅkhatūryādinisvanaiḥ  Vis 
kautukaṃ samalaṃkṛtya taṇḍulopari nārada 
paścādgrāmaṃ paribhramya mahādīpasamūhayuk  Vis 
bandhayet kautukaṃ paścāt pūrvoktena vidhānataḥ 
rātrau homaḥ prakartavyaḥ jalasaṃprokṣaṇaṃ divā  Vis 
na kuryāt prokṣaṇaṃ rātrau na divā homamācaret 
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena rātrau homaṃ prakalpayet  Vis 
prabhāte sumuhūrte tu jalasaṃprokṣaṇaṃ kramāt 
prokṣayettu vidhānena bimbādyāvaraṇāntikam  Vis 
āvāhayettato devaṃ nārāyaṇamanāmayam 
śaṅkhacakradharaṃ devaṃ pītavāsasamacyutam  Vis 
sarvābharaṇasaṃyuktaṃ vanamālāvirājitam 
rājāvartamaṇiprakhyaṃ hārakeyūrabhūṣitam  Vis 
śrīvatsavakṣasaṃ cāru makarākṛtikuṇḍalam 
kambugrīvaṃ mahābāhuṃ kiñcitprahasitānanam  Vis 
evaṃ dhyātvā mahāviṣṇuṃ garuḍopari saṃsthitam 
saha dvādaśabhiścaiva mūrtibhirdaśabhistathā  Vis 
lokapālaistathādityai rudrairvasubhireva ca 
ṛṣibhiścāraṇaiḥ siddhaiḥ kiṃnarairapsaro gaṇaiḥ  Vis 
evaṃ dhyātvā mahāviṣṇuṃ nārāyaṇamanāmayam 
tattanmantreṇa saṃsthāpya prokṣayedgandhavāriṇā  Vis 
śeṣodakena matimān prokṣayet parivārakam 
praṇavādisvamantraistu parivārānaśeṣataḥ  Vis 
pūrvādikalaśān gṛhya mahāpīṭhe 'bhiṣecayet 
tataḥ puruṣasūktena pūjayet puruṣottamam  Vis 
havirnivedayet paścāt pūrvoktena vidhānataḥ 
caṇḍādibhyo baliṃ dadyāddikṣu caiva vidikṣu ca  Vis 
balibimbasamāyuktaṃ balibhramaṇamācaret 
evaṃ baliṃ kramāt kuryāt śaṅkhatūryādisaṃyutam  Vis 
pradakṣiṇaṃ tataḥ kuryāt praṇipatya kṣamāpayet 
ācāryadakṣiṇāṃ datvā brāhmaṇān bhojayettataḥ  Vis 
hotṝṃścaiva susaṃpūjya ācāryaṃ pūjayet punaḥ 
hārakeyūrasaṃyuktaṃ kaṭisūtrāṅgulīyakaiḥ  Vis 
vividhāni ca vastrāṇi ācāryāya nivedayet 
dakṣiṇāṃ cottamāṃ dadyāt gāṃ ca datvā payasvinīm  Vis 
ardhaṃ vāpi dhanaṃ deyaṃ mūrtipānāṃ hitaiṣiṇām 
pādonaṃ sādhakānāṃ ca dīkṣitānāṃ tadardhakam  Vis 
annadānaṃ ca sarveṣāṃ dadyāddevasamīpataḥ 
pavitrāropaṇepyevaṃ dakṣiṇāṃ dāpayenmune  Vis 
iti samyak samākhyātaḥ jalasaṃprokṣaṇakramaḥ 
etadvicārya kartavyaṃ
pañcarātraviśāradaiḥ  Vis

ekonacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
viṣvaksenaḥ
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi prāyaścittavidhiṃ param 
pūjanādiṣu sarvāsu kriyāsu munisattama  Vis 
prātaḥ sandhyārcanāhīne madhyāhne dviguṇaṃ caret 
prātarmadhyāhnayorhīne sāyāhne triguṇaṃ caret  Vis 
ekāhamarcanāhīne upavāsavrataṃ caret 
kalaśairnavabhiḥ snāpya pūrvoktena vidhānataḥ  Vis 
puṇyāhaṃ vācayettatra bhojyā vai brāhmaṇāstrayaḥ 
arcayitvā yathānyāyaṃ pūrvoktena vidhānataḥ  Vis 
dvitīye dviguṇaṃ caiva tṛtīye triguṇaṃ caret 
evameva tu kartavyaṃ dvādaśāhāntameva ca  Vis 
pakṣahīnaṃ bhavettasmin snāpayedadhamottamam 
brāhmaṇān bhojayettatra viprān dvādaśaṃ pāyasaiḥ  Vis 
māsahīnaṃ bhavettatra vāstuhomena saṃyutam 
adhamottamamārgeṇa snapanaṃ kārayeddhareḥ  Vis 
puṇyāhaṃ vācayettatra pūjayet pūrvavat kramāt 
brāhmaṇān bhojayettatra śiṣṭān pañcadaśādhikān  Vis 
etat krameṇa kṛtvā tu trimāsāntaṃ viśeṣataḥ 
trimāsādīni ṣaṇmāsādarvāk pūjāvilopane  Vis 
saṃmārjyāntarbahirgehaṃ prakṣālya vidhivattadā 
dhūpayitvāgarudhūpena puṇyāhaṃ tatra kārayet  Vis 
uttamottamamārgaṃ vā hyekāśītikrameṇa vā 
snāpayeddevadeveśaṃ yathāvittānusārataḥ  Vis 
brāhmaṇān bhojapettatra pūrvavaddhomamācaret 
mahāhavirnivedyātha pūjayet puruṣottamam  Vis 
tataḥ paraṃ trivarṣāt prāk snapaṃna cottamottamam 
snāpayenmuniśārdūla pūrvoktena vidhānataḥ  Vis 
brāhmaṇān bhojayettatra yathāvittānusārataḥ 
tadūrdhvaṃ dvādaśādarvāk prāyaścittaṃ vidhīyate  Vis 
praṇavena nirīkṣyātha garbhagehaṃ tu sādhakaḥ 
pañcagavyaṃ kramāt kṛtvā garbhāgāraṃ vidhodhayet  Vis 
uttamottamamārgaṃ vāpyathavā madhyamaṃ tu vā 
snāpayeddevadeveśaṃ yathāvibhavavistaram  Vis 
brāhmaṇān bhojayettatra yathāvittānusārataḥ 
śāntihomaṃ krāmat kṛtvā pūrvavat pūjayetaddharim  Vis 
ata ūrdhvaṃ muniśreṣṭha prāyaścitaṃ vidhīyate 
jalasaṃprokṣaṇaṃ kuryāt puṇyāhoktipuraḥsaram  Vis 
brāhmaṇān bhojayettatra tena śāntirbhaviṣyati 
pūjāṅgadravyahīnaṃ cet arghyādihavirantakam  Vis 
hīnairdravyaistu deveśamarcayeddviguṇaṃ punaḥ 
aṣṭākṣareṇa mantreṇa devāgre tu śataṃ japet  Vis 
taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ prāyaścittamidaṃ bhavet 
prāyaścittaṃ kramāt kuryāt taddravyeṇa dine dine  Vis 
etat saṃkṣepataḥ proktaṃ pūjālope tu nārada 
ālaye patite tatra bālasthānaṃ tu kārayet  Vis 
deveśaṃ vidhivat sthāpya pūjayettu dine dine 
ālayaṃ pūrvavat kṛtvā prokṣaṇaṃ kārayettataḥ  Vis 
bhinnālaye tu tatsthāne śailaṃ vā dāru yojayet 
iṣṭakāsudhayāyuktaṃ navakarmāṇi kārayet  Vis 
citrābhāsālaye tatra citrakarma samācaret 
snapanaṃ tatra kurvīta mūrtihomaṃ ca kārayet  Vis 
brāhmaṇān viṣṇubhaktāścaṃ bhojanaṃ kārayettataḥ 
mahāhavirnivedyātha pūjayet puruṣottamam  Vis 
dahane tu pravakṣyāmi prāyaścittavidhikramam 
prāsādaṃ maṇḍapaṃ vātha prākāraṃ gopuraṃ tathā  Vis 
prāsādābhyantaraṃ vāpi pacanālayameva vā 
vinodamaṇḍapaṃ caiva yāgamaṇḍapameva vā  Vis 
puṣpasthāne jalasthāne cānyasminnitareṣu ca 
pramādādagnidagdhaṃ cet samyagutpādya pūrvavat  Vis 
snapanaṃ tu trirātrāt prāk kārayedadhamottamam 
brāhmaṇān bhojayettatra puṇyāhaṃ caiva kārayet  Vis 
nārāyaṇopaniṣadaṃ paṭhettantrottarakramāt 
aṣṭākṣareṇa juhuyādājyena śatamāhutīḥ  Vis 
yadi dagdhaṃ vimānaṃ cet kevalaṃlā
pratimā punaḥ 
dagdhasya caikadeśaṃ cet samyagutpādya pūrvavat  Vis 
snapanaṃ cottamaṃ kuryāt adhamottamameva vā 
snāpayeddevadeveśaṃ pūjayet pūrvavat kramāt  Vis 
vimānaṃ bahudagdhaṃ cet bālasthānaṃ prakalpayet 
navagehaṃ kramāt kṛtvā śeṣakarmāṇi kārayet  Vis 
nāradaḥ
ukto me bhavatā doṣaḥ sthānasya tu viśeṣataḥ 
atyadbhutānāṃ sarveṣāṃ doṣānme brūhyaśeṣataḥ  Vis 
ālaye devadevasya ye doṣāḥ prabhavanti vai 
haviṣāṃ caiva ye doṣāḥ tathopakaraṇeṣu ca  Vis 
viṣvaksenaḥ
sādhu pṛṣṭaṃ tvayā deva vaktavyaṃ ca mayādhunā 
ālaye devadevasya ye doṣāstān bravīmi te  Vis 
valmīkadarśane caiva tathā sarpasya darśane 
anyeṣāṃ caiva jantūnāṃ saviṣāṇāṃ munīśvara  Vis 
madhupralambane caiva buddhipūrvāgnipātane 
vaidyudaśanipāte ca ulkāpāte tathaiva ca  Vis 
pramādāt pratimā vāpi dvidhā caiva bhevadyadi 
ulūkavāsane caiva vṛkṣāṇāṃ ca samudbhave  Vis 
vimānasya ca bhede ca sarveṣāṃ ca vināśakṛt 
keśakīṭādipāte ca jalajānāṃ nipātane  Vis 
anyeṣāṃ caiva jantūnāṃ vinipāte haviḥṣu ca 
garbhāgāre tathā viṣṇoḥ upahāre tathaiva ca  Vis 
maṇḍape devadevasya prathamāvaraṇe 'thavā 
dvitīye vā tṛtīye vā balipīṭheṣu sarvaśaḥ  Vis 
agnisthāne jalasthāne puṣpasthāne tathaiva ca 
āsthānamaṇḍape caiva tathālaṃkāramaṇḍape  Vis 
līlāsthāneṣu cānyeṣu gavāṃ sthāne tathaiva ca 
śithilīnāṃ samudbhāve doṣān vakṣye munīśvara  Vis 
valmīkadarśane vyādhiḥ mṛtyuḥ sarpasya darśane 
anāvṛṣṭirmadhoścaiva durbhikṣamitareṣvapi  Vis 
śithilīśilīndhra
darśane caiva pratimāyāṃ hareryadi 
rājā mṛtyumavāpnoti rājyabhraṃśamathāpi vā  Vis 
vyādhiṃ vā mahādāpnoti śatrubhirvā parābhavam 
putradāraviyogaṃ vā labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ  Vis 
grāmāṇāṃ nagarāṇāṃ ca deśasya ca balasya ca 
vināśamāpnuyāt samyak sadyo vā syādupalpavaḥ  Vis 
pīṭhe garbhagṛhe caiva upahāre tathaiva ca 
amātyamantriṇāṃ doṣāḥ prakṛtīnāṃ tathaiva ca  Vis 
sthānāntareṣu sarvatra śithilīnāṃ tu darśane 
rāṣṭre doṣā bhaviṣyanti dubhikṣavyādhisaṃbhavāḥ  Vis 
śunaiśvabhir
vā vānarairvāpi gṛdhraiśca kṛmikīṭakaiḥ 
piṅgalairvāyasaiścaiva pakṣibhiḥ kukkuṭādibhiḥ  Vis 
tathānyaistādṛśairbhūtaiḥ pratimā spṛśyate yadi 
sthānanāśamavāpnoti grāmasyānarthameva ca  Vis 
prāyaścittaṃ pravakṣyāmi valmīkādeśca darśane 
tadapi pratimāyāṃ cedyātrāṃ kṛtvā yathāvidhi  Vis 
taddeśaṃ śodhayitvā tu yāvatsamyagbhaveddṛḍham 
pūrvavat kalpayitvā tu punaḥsaṃsthāpayet kramāt  Vis 
jalasaṃprokṣaṇaṃ vāpi kuryānmantrīṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ 
dūṣitaṃ cetaradbimbaṃ jantubhiḥ sparśane sati  Vis 
mārjayitvā kuśairdarbhaiḥ puṇyāhaṃ tatra kārayet 
snapanaṃ kārayet paścāt karmārcāyāṃ yathāvidhi  Vis 
juhuyāt pañcamantraistu pratyekaṃ śatamāhutīḥ 
tataśca śithilījāte pīṭhe garbhagṛhepi vā  Vis 
śodhayitvā tu taṃ deśaṃ dṛḍhīkṛtya prayatnataḥ 
snapanaṃ vidhivat kṛtvā caikāśītikrameṇa tu  Vis 
śāntihomaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā puṇyāhenaiva śuddhyati 
vimāne madhunotpanne prākāre 'bhyantare 'pi vā  Vis 
prakṣālya pañcagavyena bahirantaḥ samantataḥ 
snapanaṃ cāpi kṛtvā tu puṇyāhenaiva śuddhyati  Vis 
anuktānāṃ tu sarveṣāṃ prāyaścitaṃ vidhīyate 
uttamaṃ madhyamaṃ vāpi adhamottamameva vā  Vis 
snāpayeddevadeveśaṃ pūjayedvidhipūrvakam 
śāntihomaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā puṇyāhenaiva śuddhyati  Vis 
nṛttagītaṃ ca vādyaṃ ca kārayeddevasannidhau 
tadante pūjayitvā tu japenmūrtiṃ yathākramam  Vis 
brāhmaṇāna bhojayitvā tu vaiṣṇavāṃśca viśeṣataḥ 
alaṃkāravidhiṃ kṛtvā naivedyaṃ ca mahāhaviḥ  Vis 
nityadīpavināśe tu prāyaścittaṃ vidhīyate 
kapilājyaṃ śarāve tu sthāpayitvāstramantrataḥ  Vis 
dīpayitvā muniśreṣṭha dīpamudrāṃ pradarśayet 
nityāgnau samidājyena caruṇā hūyate pṛthak  Vis 
śataṃ vāpi tadardhaṃ vā tasyārdhaṃ vāhutīḥ kramāt 
kārayenmūrtimantreṇa pratyekaṃ juhuyāt kramāt  Vis 
havirādyeṣa sarveṣu keśakīṭādipātane 
evameva tu kartavyaṃ prāyaścittaṃ tu nārada  Vis 
śuddhasnānaṃ purā kṛtvā tadbimbaṃ parameṣṭhinā 
adhamottamamārgeṇa snapanaṃ kārayet kramāt  Vis 
pañcopaniṣadairmantraiḥ pratyekaṃ śatamāhutīḥ 
puṇyāhaṃ vācayitvā tu tena śāntirbhaviṣyati  Vis 
deveśaṃ pūjayet paścāt pūrvoktena vidhānataḥ 
ācāryaṃ pūjayet paścāt yathā tuṣṭo bhaviṣyati  Vis 
ihopayuktadravyāṇi ācāryāya nivedayet 
prāyaścittaṃ pravakṣyāmi maraṇe devatālaye  Vis 
caṇḍālapatitādīnāṃ maraṇe vartite sati 
garbhāgāre 'thavā cārdhamaṇḍape vā munīśvara  Vis 
prāsādasthitapīṭhāgre tathābhyantaramaṇḍape 
khātvā caiva dhanurmātraṃ taṃ deśamaśilā tu cet  Vis 
saṃpūrya saikatairmṛdbhiḥ kṣālayitvā tu vāriṇā 
ālayaṃ pañcagavyena bahirantaśca śodhayet  Vis 
samidājyena caruṇā pratyekaṃ tu sahasrakam 
aṣṭadikṣu yathānyāyaṃ juhuyānmūlamantrataḥ  Vis 
brāhmaṇān bhojayet paścāt prāsādasya samantataḥ 
puṇyāhaṃ vācayettatra kārayedadhamottamam  Vis 
snāpeyadvidhivat samyagyathāvittānusārataḥ 
etadardhaṃ tu śūdrasya maraṇe kārayedbudhaḥ  Vis 
tadardhaṃ tu dvijātīnāṃ maraṇe devatālaye 
maṇḍape gopure teṣāṃ maraṇe vartite sati  Vis 
bhūśuddhiṃ pūrvavat kṛtvā puṇyāhaṃ caiva kārayet 
homamekaṃ tu kartavyamālayasyottare budhaḥ  Vis 
śilāmayaṃ cettadgehaṃ garbhāgārādi nārada 
kapilāgomayaṃ grāhyaṃ mūlamantreṇa mantravit  Vis 
garbhāgārādi sarvatra vāyumantreṇa lepayet 
saṃprokṣya pañcagavyena śeṣa pūrvavadācaret  Vis 
bhūgupte cāgnidagdhe ca jalāviṣṭe nirāspade 
mantreśaṃśe
ciralupte ca punaḥ sthāpanamācaret  Vis 
tasmādūrdhvaṃ tu vidhivat bimbasthāpanamārabhet 
aṅgahīnasya berasya aṅgahīnaṃ 
bhavedyadi  Vis 
suvarṇena tadaṅgaṃ tu kṛtvā sandhāpayeddaḍham 
evaṃ kṛtvā vidhānena punaḥ sthāpanamārabhet  Vis 
jalavāsavidhānena pūrvavaccheṣamācaret 
athavātra muniśreṣṭha jalasaṃprokṣaṇa tu vā  Vis 
kārayeddevadevasya tena śāntirbhaviṣyati 
santyājyaṃ dārujaṃ bimbaṃ sandheyaṃ mṛṇmayaṃ bhavet  Vis 
chinne bhinne tathā vaktre mūlārcāyāṃ pramādataḥ 
kalpayitvā tu deveśe bālasthānakrameṇa tu  Vis 
yuktyā yuktiviśeṣeṇa śilpibhiḥ kārayeddṛḍham 
kṛtvā varṇairalaṃkāraṃ pratiṣṭhāṃ punarārabhet  Vis 
sauvarṇapratimāyāṃ tu chinne bhinne ca vaktrake 
drāvayitvā sakṛt siktaṃ kṛtvā saṃsthāpayet punaḥ  Vis 
tatastu bahudhā bhinnaṃ tāmraṃ cāpsu vinikṣipet 
ekadhā ca dvidhā bhinnaṃ tāmreṇaiva tu yojayet  Vis 
tatsarvaṃ pūrvavat kṛtvā bimbaṃ kuryānnavaṃ śubham 
tāmrabimbaṃ tu saṃsthāpya nityaṃ pūjā pravartate  Vis 
bimbaṃ sulakṣaṇopetaṃ rājataṃ saṃbhavedyadi 
jalādhivāsanādīni tasmin kāryāṇi sarvaśaḥ  Vis 
tāmrabimbagatāṃ śaktiṃ rājate sthāpya yatnataḥ 
tāmrabimbaṃ parityajya rājataṃ sthāpayet kramāt  Vis 
tathaiva rājataṃ tyaktvā sauvarṇaṃ sthāpayet kramāt 
kadācidapi na tyājyaṃ sauvarṇaṃ bhūtimicchatā  Vis 
svadharmayuktajātibhyo durvṛtte 'pi tathā dvija 
mukhya eva sadā vipra tathaivottamaberakam  Vis 
sauvarṇameva sarveṣāṃ mukhyabimbaṃ praśasyate 
saṃsthāpya svasya sthāne tu pūjayettu dine dine  Vis 
brahmasthāne sthitaṃ bimbaṃ karmārcāṃ na tu cālayet 
calanaṃ tu bhavettasmin rājyasya calanaṃ bhavet  Vis 
tatsthānaṃ nidhanaṃ yāti grāmasya nidhanaṃ bhavet 
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena uktakāle tu cālayet  Vis 
ayane viṣuve caiva saṃkrāntyāṃ grahaṇe tathā 
prātaḥsandhyārcanane
snānavelāyāṃ munisattama  Vis 
snānabimbavihīne tu calanaṃ tu samācaret 
dvitīyāvaraṇādbāhye karmārcāṃ na tu cālayet  Vis 
pramādādvāpi mohādvā calanaṃ cenmunīśvara 
jalasaṃprokṣaṇaṃ kṛtvā supuṇyāhapuraḥsaram  Vis 
adhamottamamārgeṇa snāpayedberamuttamam 
ekaberavidhāne tu prāyaścittaṃ vidhīyate  Vis 
snapanaṃ sthāvarārcāyāṃ kartavyaṃ vidhivat sadā 
prāsādaṃ tu navaṃ kṛtvā pañcagavyena śodhayet  Vis 
adhamottamamārgeṇa snāpayet puruṣottamam 
evameva tu kartavyaṃ ṣaṅviṃśadvatsarāntakam  Vis 
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi jalasaṃprokṣaṇaṃ kramāt  
tasmāttenaiva śuddhiḥ syāt sarvaśāntirbhaviṣyati  Vis 
aṅgahīnaṃ bhavedbimbaṃ punarutpādya pūrvavat 
saṃsthāpya vidhivat pūrvaṃ punaḥ sthāpanamācaret  Vis 
nāradaḥ
senāpate mahāprājña snapanasya prasīda me 
aśāstrīye mahādoṣān sarvān me brūhyaśeṣataḥ  Vis 
yairdeṣaiḥ snapanodbhūtai rājarāṣṭraṃ vinaśyati 
paśavaśca prajāścaiva sasyādinidhanāni ca  Vis 
viṣvaksenaḥ
snapanasya pravakṣyāmi mahādoṣān munīśvara 
śalabhairgandhaduṣṭaistu duṣṭāḥ syuḥ sarvamānavāḥ  Vis 
sādhite kalaśe bhinne taddravyaiḥ pūrayet punaḥ 
ūnaiśca kalaśairūnavibhavāḥ sarvamānavāḥ  Vis 
kṛmikīṭapataṅgādidravyeṣu patane yadi 
tatsarvaṃ varjayennityaṃ viṣṇuyāgeṣu sarvaśaḥ  Vis 
varjitaistu sadā dravyaiḥ deveśasyārcanaṃ yadi 
ṣaṣṭirvarṣasahasrāṇi narakaṃ pratipadyate  Vis 
keśayuktaṃ tu yaddravyaṃ nipāte nipated
viṣṇumūrdhani 
mūrdhābhiṣiktaṃ rājānaṃ nāśayennātra saṃśayaḥ  Vis 
anyeṣvapi ca duṣṭeṣu patiteṣu mahāmune 
etadeva phalaṃ prāha svayaṃ nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ  Vis 
paryuṣitairna cāmbhābhiḥ kalaśeṣu prapūrayet 
yadi lobhena gṛhṇīyāt kākayoniśataṃ vrajet  Vis 
purāṇasarpiṣā devaṃ snāpayedyadi lobhataḥ 
gṛdhrayoniśataṃ gacchet tadante sūkaro bhavet  Vis 
mahiṣājyena deveśaṃ snāpayedyadi mohataḥ 
gṛdhrayoniśataṃ gacchet tadante kukkuṭo bhavet  Vis 
snāpayitvānyathājyena kṛkalāsaśataṃ vrajet 
dadhiyuktaṃ tu yat kṣīraṃ snāpayedyadi lobhataḥ  Vis 
daridro mānuṣo loke janmaścājaajajanma
śataṃ vrajet 
rasadravyaṃ ca vanyaistu niyujyānmākṣikaṃ naraḥ  Vis 
yadi tatpūjito vipra vṛṣajanmaśataṃ vrajet 
kṛmikīṭapataṅgānāṃ dravyeṣu patite patanaṃ yadi  Vis 
tatsarvaṃ varjayennityaṃ viṣṇuyāgeṣu sarvaśaḥ 
dṛśyate sādhitaṃ caiva taddravyaṃ tu parityajet  Vis 
tān sarvānna spṛśedyastu kalaśe sādhite punaḥ 
tathā vai dṛśyate cāpi tato 'nyāni ca vinyaset  Vis 
śvānakukkuṭacaṇḍālaiḥ sādhite
dṛśyate punaḥ 
parityajya tato 'nyāṃśca sādhayet kalaśān punaḥ  Vis 
udakyāntyajairvāpi sādhite
dṛśyate punaḥ 
parityajya tato vidvān punaścānyaṃ tu vinyaset  Vis 
duṣṭairhi vīkṣitaṃ caiva pādaspṛṣṭaṃ ca yadbhavet 
rājānaṃ rājamātraṃ ca yajamānamathāpi vā  Vis 
nāśayet saparīvāraṃ sapaśudravyasaṃcayam 
sāmātyaṃ sapuraṃ rāṣṭraṃ duṣṭadravyābhiṣecane  Vis 
vyādhayaśca bhavantyugrā anāvṛṣṭistathaiva ca 
bhūtavetālarakṣāṃsi piśācoragadānavāḥ  Vis 
bādhante hyaniśaṃ hyete rājānaṃ rāṣṭrameva ca 
āḍhakaṃ vā tadardhaṃ vā tannyūnaṃ parivarjayet  Vis 
snehadravyāṇi sarvāṇi sādhako mantravittamaḥ 
vastrasūtravihīne tu toraṇādibhireva vā  Vis 
nṛttagītādibhirvāpi gandhapuṣpādibhistathā 
alaṃkāraraiḥ
vihīnaṃ vā devadevasya śāṅrgiṇaḥ  Vis 
yasmin rāṣṭre muniśreṣṭha snapanaṃ syāt kadācana 
tadrāṣṭraṃ corabhūyiṣṭhaṃ śatrubhiścaiva hanyate  Vis 
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena yathāśāstraṃ yathākramam 
snapanaṃ kārayedviṣṇoḥ bhūtimicchan parāṃ gatim  Vis 
doṣāṇāṃ ca praśamanaṃ vyādhīnāṃ caiva sarvaśaḥ 
grahāṇāṃ śāntaye caiva śatrūṇāṃ ca jayāya ca  Vis 
āyurārogyavṛddhyarthaṃ putrapautravivṛddhaye 
kāmānāṃ caiva sarveṣāṃ vṛddhaye sarvavarṇinām  Vis 
vidhihīnaṃ kriyāhīnaṃ dravyahīnaṃ tathaiva ca 
mānahīnaṃ tu yaddravyaṃ pūjāhīnaṃ ca yadguroḥ  Vis 
kālātītaṃ prajāhīnaṃ kartṛdeśeṣu sarvaśaḥ 
ābhicāraṃro
bhavet sadyo grāmasya nagarasya ca  Vis 
evaṃ yathoktasnapanaṃ kārayedyastu mānavaḥ 
mucyate pātakaiḥ sarveḥ padmapatramivāmbhasā  Vis 
godhnaḥ pitṛdhno mātṛdhno bhrūṇahā gurutalyagaḥ 
surāpaḥ svarṇahārī ca paradārābhimarśakaḥ  Vis 
ete cānye ca mucyante pāpebhyaḥ snapanena vai 
snapane hyadhikaṃ puṇyaṃ vidyate munisattama  Vis 
aśvamedhasahasraṃ tu yatkuryāt kāyaśodhanam 
snapanena tu tadviṣṇoḥ labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ  Vis 
dhvajasthāne pravakṣyāmi prāyaścitaṃ tu nārada 
apramāṇapaṭaṃ citraṃ vaiṇavaṃ daṇḍameva vā  Vis 
anuktādhikahīnaṃ ca prayatnena vivarjayet 
varjitena kṛtaṃ cettanniṣphalaṃ syānna saṃśayaḥ  Vis 
dhvajādhivāsane kāle kumbhe cāvāhya vāhane 
tatkumbhapatane caiva calane bhedane tathā  Vis 
pratimāparikumbhe ca tadgrāmaśca vinaśyati 
snapanaṃ tatra kartavyaṃ deveśasyādhamettamam  Vis 
śāntihomaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā grāmadoṣanikṛntanam 
punarutpādayet kumbhaṃ saṃsthāpya vidhipūrvakam  Vis 
dhvaje lakṣaṇahīne tu garuḍe vā viśeṣataḥ 
kartṛbhartṛvināśaḥ syāt tatrastho narakaṃ vrajet  Vis 
kṣipraṃ tyaktvā dhvajaṃ tatra ācāryeṇa samāhitaḥ 
dhvajamutthāpayet sadyaḥ sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutam  Vis 
pūrvoktavidhinā samyak śeṣaṃ karma samārabhet 
grāmapradakṣiṇe kāle patite vātakopite  Vis 
durbhikṣaṃ vartate tatra kartāro vyādhipīḍitāḥ 
taddoṣaparihārāya snapanaṃ cādhamottamam  Vis 
puṇyāhaṃ vācayettatra brāhmaṇānāṃ ca bhojanam 
kārayenmuniśārdūla śeṣa pūrvavadācaret  Vis 
ācāryaṃ pūjayet paścāt yathāśāstroktamārgataḥkam 
patanādbhedane caiva dhvajaṃ tyaktvā tu tatkṣaṇāt  Vis 
snapanaṃ cottamaṃ kṛtvā devadevasya cakriṇaḥ 
vāstuhomaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā puṇyāhaṃ vācayettataḥ  Vis 
utpādya coddharet samyak dhvajaṃ lakṣaṇasaṃyutam 
grāmapradakṣiṇe kāle balihīnaṃ bhavedyadi  Vis 
sa grāmo nidhanaṃ yāti tatrastho narakaṃ vrajet 
taddoṣaparihārāya prāyaścittaṃ vidhīyate  Vis 
snāpayeddevadeveśaṃ pañcāśat kalaśaiḥ krāmat 
pūjayitvā tato devaṃ punargrāmaṃ paribhramet  Vis 
balidānasamāyuktaṃ paścādutthāpayet khagamddhvajam

saṃkaraḥ parihartavyo rājarāṣṭrasukhāya ca  Vis 
yaddaivatyaṃ kṛtaṃ kṣetraṃ vidhinā karṣaṇādinā 
tadanyadaivataṃ vipra manasāpi na kalpayet  Vis 
yadi vā sthāpyate mohāddaṇḍyo vadhyaḥsa pāpabhāk 
sa kartā saṃkarasyāpi rājño rāṣṭrasya tasya hi  Vis 
pañcarātraṃ tu śaivaṃ vai vaikhānasavidhānakam 
teṣāṃ vāstvādisāṃkaryāt kiñcideva viśeṣakam  Vis 
sāttvataṃ sarvavṛddhyarthaṃ śaivaṃ sarvavināśakṛt 
vaikhānasamanarthārthaṃ tasmāttatparivarjayet  Vis 
asthānasthāpitāḥ kecit svasthāna parivarjitāḥ 
devatādvayakopena sarvaṃ naśyatyasaṃśayaḥ  Vis 
saṃkaro dvividhaḥ proktaḥ sarvaprāṇivināśanaḥ 
jātisaṃkaraṇaṃ caiva tantrasaṃkaraṇaṃ tathā  Vis 
jātisaṃkaraṇenaiva jagaccaṇḍālatāṃ vrajet 
tantrasaṃkaraṇenaiva rājārāṣṭraṃ vinaśyati  Vis 
rāṣṭraṃ śarīraṃ rājastu rājā jīvaḥ sa ucyate 
rāṣṭrakṣaye kṣayo rājñaḥ tasmādrakṣyaṃ dvayaṃ budhaiḥ  Vis 
caṇḍālatvaṃ gate loke vedāḥ sarve tirohitāḥ 
tirohiteṣu vedeṣu yajñādikratavastathā  Vis 
ekavarṇaṃ jagatsarvaṃ vastu niśceṣṭakaṃ bhavet  
jātisaṃkaradoṣeṇa dvijānāṃ maraṇaṃ bhavet  Vis 
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena sāṃkaryaṃ parivarjayet 
devadevātparaṃ nānyattadāyattā hi siddhayaḥ  Vis 
iti cintyaiva bhūtānāṃ vayaṃ devamupāsmahe 
sarvadevamayo viṣṇurbhagavān bhūtabhāvanaḥ  Vis 
sarvaprāṇihitārthāya nānyaivaiko 'pi dṛśyate 
brahmā rudraśca śakraśca vasavo varuṇastathā  Vis 
yakṣagandharvasiddhaśca bhūtavetālarākṣasāḥ 
śaktayaśca tathā cānyāḥ sarvāḥ viṣṇuvibhūtayaḥ  Vis 
tāśca sarvāḥ prasīdanti purā cārthārthināṃ nṛṇām 
pūjyamāne tu satataṃ tattatpūjāvidhānataḥ  Vis 
sarvaprāṇihitārthāya munibhiḥ karuṇātmabhiḥ 
kṛtāni tattadyogyāni śāstrāṇi munipuṅgava  Vis 
vaidikaṃ tāntrikaṃ caiva tathā vaidikatāntrikam 
trividhaṃ karma saṃproktaṃ pañcarātrārṇavāmṛtam   Vis 
vaidikaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ tu rājñāṃ vaidikatāntrikam 
tāntrikaṃ vaiśyaśūdrāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ tāntrikaṃ tu vā  Vis 
bhārgaveṇoktadharmeṇa pratilomādi kārayet 
aśrīkaramasaumyaṃ tadabrāhmaṇaparigraham  Vis 
avaidikatvāttattantraṃ vaikhānasamathādhamam 
saṃkaraḥ parihartavyo brāhmaṇaiśca jagaddhitaiḥ  Vis 
vāstau bimbasya pūjāyāṃ pūjakasya ca saṃkaraḥ 
sarvathā parihartavyo prāyaścittaiḥ pṛthagvidhaudhaiḥ  Vis 
nāradaḥ
prāyaścittaṃ samācakṣva bimbasaṃkaraṇādiṣu 
yatkṛtvā sarvadoṣāśca naśyantyaśubhahetavaḥ  Vis 
viṣvaksenaḥ
na tithirna ca nakṣatraṃ kālavelā na vidyate 
saṃkaraṃ tayajyate kṣipraṃ sarvaprāṇihitāya vai  Vis 
sadya eva tu kartavyā saṃkarasya tu niṣkṛtiḥ 
niṣkṛtyāharahaḥ
paścāt rājarāṣṭrasuvṛddhikṛt  Vis 
grāmasya nagarasyāpi sarvasaṃpatsukhāvaham 
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena kṣipraṃ śāntiṃ samācaret  Vis 
yattantreṇa samārabdhaṃ tattantreṇaiva kārayet 
anyathā cenmahādoṣo rājarāṣṭravināśakṛt  Vis 
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena na kuryāttantrasaṃkaram 
ekāhamarcanāhīne svakalpoktavidhānataḥ  Vis 
ekāśītikramāt kṛtvā snapanaṃ sādhakottamaḥ 
śāntihomaṃ kramāt kṛtvā snapanaṃ sādhakottamaḥ  Vis 
śāntihomaṃ kramāt kṛtvā vāstuhomaṃ tathaiva ca 
brāhmaṇān bhojayet paścādaṣṭottaraśataṃ kramāt  Vis 
tasyārdhaṃ vā tadardhaṃ vā yathāvittānusārataḥ 
caturmūrtividhiṃ smṛtvā pañcamūrtividhi tyajet  Vis 
parivārāṇi sarvāṇi pūrvavat sthāpayet kramāt 
tattvanyāsaṃ kramāt kṛtvā sṛṣṭinyāsaṃ tathaiva ca  Vis 
mūlamantreṇa matimān mūlamūrtimanusmaran 
pūjayet satataṃ paścāt pūrvoktena vidhānataḥ  Vis 
mahāhavirnivedyātha kārayedgurupūjanam 
pūjālope 'pi cettatra punastenaiva pūjayet  Vis 
tatra sāttvatamārgeṇa pūjyamāne dine dine 
tantrāntareṇa deveśaṃ kadācinna tu pūjayet  Vis 
pūjayedyadi saṃmohānniṣphalaṃ syānnaṃ saṃśayaḥ 
tatpūjāharahaḥ paścāttadgrāmasya vināśakṛt  Vis 
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena pūjayettaddvijottama 
pūrvaṃ karmārcanādīnāṃ śuddhasnānaṃ tu kārayet  Vis 
jalasaṃprokṣaṇādīni mūlārcāyāṃ niyojayet 
snapanādīni karmāṇi karmārcāyāṃ niyojayet  Vis 
utsavaṃ kārayettasmin balihomapuraḥsaram 
ekāhaṃ vā tryahaṃ vātha saptāhaṃ vā munīśvara  Vis 
kārayedutsavaṃ tatra yathāśaktyānurūpataḥ  
etat krameṇa kartavyaṃ dvādaśābdāntameva ca  Vis 
ekābde rakṣasāṃ sthānaṃ vāsaḥ
tasmācchāntiṃ tu kāreyat 
dvyabde ca yakṣavāsastu tryabde bhūtasaṃkulam  Vis 
caturabde piśācānāṃ pañcābde dānavālayam 
pañcavarṣamatīte tu nivāso brahmarakṣasām  Vis 
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena kṣipraṃ śāntiṃ tu kārayet 
dvādaśābdāt purā kuryāt jalasaṃprokṣaṇena tu  Vis 
evameva tu kartavyaṃ viṃśadvarṣāntameva tu 
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi prāyaścittaṃ tu nārada  Vis 
jalasaṃprokṣaṇaṃ kuryājjalavāsapuraḥsaram 
brāhmaṇān bhojayet paścānmahāhavipuraḥsaram  Vis 
ṣaṭtriṃśadvatsarādarvāk tāvattenaiva kārayet 
ṣaṭtriṃśadvatsarādūrdhvaṃ prāyaścittaṃ vidhīyate  Vis 
pañcagavyaṃ kramāt kṛtvā garbhāgāraṃ viśodhayet 
puṇyāhaṃ vācayitvā tu brāhmaṇānāmanujñayā  Vis 
jalādhivāsanādīni pūrvoktenaiva kārayet 
godānaṃ bhūmidānaṃ ca hiraṇyaṃ vastrameva ca  Vis 
sarvadānaṃ tataḥ kuryāt brāhmaṇebhyo yathākramam 
evaṃ tadvardhayitvā tu pañcāśadvatsarāntakam  Vis 
pañcāśadvatsarādūrdhvāṃ prāyaścittaṃ vidhīyate 
jalādhivāsanādīni punaḥ sthāpanamārabhet  Vis 
brāhmaṇān bhojayettatra śeṣaṃ pūrvavadācaret 
etat krameṇa kartavyaṃ śatavarṣāntameva ca  Vis 
saṃvatsaraśatādūrdhvaṃ śūnyasthānaṃ bhaveddhruvam 
tadgrāmaṃ nidhanaṃ yāti tatrasthā narakaṃ vrajet  Vis 
tadgrāmaṃ nidhanaṃ yāti tasmācchāntiṃ tu kārayet 
śāntiṃ kṛtvā vidhānena pañcarātreṇa pūjayet  Vis 
pūjālope 'pi cettasmin punastenaiva pūjayet 
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena kṣipraṃ śāntiṃ samācaret  Vis 
iti śrīpāñcarātre viṣvaksenasaṃhitāyāṃ prāyaścittavidhirnāma ekonacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
